<section id="brief-description">     <h1 class="town-name" data-town-type="hamlet" data-town-name="Bugshaw">         The          <span data-town-type="hamlet">             Hamlet         </span> of          <span data-town-name="Bugshaw">             Bugshaw         </span>     </h1>     <p role="main">         <span data-town-type="hamlet" data-town-name="Bugshaw">             Bugshaw         </span> is          a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="c626d3e4-f05e-4cbf-95e7-27ea9770d264" id="c626d3e4-f05e-4cbf-95e7-27ea9770d264" role="tooltip" title="With a population of 547.">hamlet</span>          located in the arid mountains,          where the vegetation is lush.          Bugshaw grew around a well-traveled crossroads, and is comprised <span class="tippy-races-percentage"></span>. They are       a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="8cbd0d7c-bad4-4926-925d-f28199be388e" id="8cbd0d7c-bad4-4926-925d-f28199be388e" role="tooltip" title="Men occupy most positions of authority.">patriarchal</span>    <span class="tip dotted" data-id="f4ec15c5-42f9-4d55-8fcf-7a635746d49b" id="f4ec15c5-42f9-4d55-8fcf-7a635746d49b" role="tooltip" title="Trade and industry are controlled by private owners for profit, rather than the state.">capitalist</span> <span class="tip dotted" data-id="aec0a96b-d65c-490e-90d0-8fa1a56a989c" id="aec0a96b-d65c-490e-90d0-8fa1a56a989c" role="tooltip" title="Governed by the scholars.">sophocratic</span> <span class="tip dotted" data-id="b058cda8-795b-40d4-8eb5-89397efd1cb2" id="b058cda8-795b-40d4-8eb5-89397efd1cb2" role="tooltip" title="The crown holds supreme judicial power, but day to day affairs are held by parliament.">constitutional monarchy</span> that <span class="tippy-religion-percentage"></span>.</p></section> <p>The nearest <span class="tip" title="This changes each time you click."><a class="link-internal" href="#null">landmark</a></span> is <span id="random">Morla’s Daughter: In the middle of a swamp is a lone mountain with a small town at the top. There is something weird about the tortle settlement that leads visitors to think they are hiding something…even the mountain is shaped like a turtle shell.</span> A population of 547, the denizens live a modest existence.  A new moon is currently taking place.</p> <article><h3>Government in Bugshaw</h3>The people of Bugshaw work in exchange for payment from their employers, which they use to buy the necessities. Mr <a data-id="748556c0-9087-4dd7-9194-ee75c3570e85" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 748556c0-9087-4dd7-9194-ee75c3570e85" title="A quite squat male dwarf with a rather bony chin called Whurbin Fire-Forge who is a noble." href="#748556c0-9087-4dd7-9194-ee75c3570e85">Whurbin Fire-Forge</a> is the head of state, but affairs are handled by <a data-id="leader" data-object-type="faction" class="link-internal leader" title="A very small scholars guild called The Brotherhood of Knowledge Holders" href="#leader">The Brotherhood of Knowledge Holders</a>, the head of whom is Ms <a data-id="22369fb4-68a3-494b-85ea-7d3ed282214e" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 22369fb4-68a3-494b-85ea-7d3ed282214e" title="A fair skinned built like a brick shithouse dwarf called Eridred Durthane who is a professor." href="#22369fb4-68a3-494b-85ea-7d3ed282214e">Eridred Durthane</a>.</article> <article><h4>Economics</h4>Trade is reasonable in Bugshaw, and people live a modest existence because of it; some taxes are applied to certain goods and services that are rendered in the city, but the more creative entrepreneurs can find loopholes to make a better profit. Welfare is above average, considering the modest quality of life. Citizens can expect a decent education, provided they can pay for it. Healthcare is overtaxed and underfunded, though.</article> <article><h4>Law and Order</h4>The policing presence in Bugshaw is more of a militia; some of the members of <a data-id="a30067a9-e4b7-44a7-bf1e-aa74c832fe11" data-object-type="faction" class="link-internal a30067a9-e4b7-44a7-bf1e-aa74c832fe11" title="A quite small guards watch called The Truncheon of Bugshaw" href="#a30067a9-e4b7-44a7-bf1e-aa74c832fe11">The Truncheon of Bugshaw</a> are part time, and there is little need for the use of force outside of intruders. Law in Bugshaw is very much punitive based, and those that breach the laws can expect hard labor, incarceration, or sometimes public execution. Crime is an ugly stain on humanity, to be punished. Magic has not been codified into the laws.</article><br><details id="TownListRaces" open=""><summary>Racial Demographics</summary> <div class="classTable" id="races">     Bugshaw is comprised <span <h1>Overview of the buildings in Bugshaw</h1><section id="brief-description">     <h1 class="town-name" data-town-type="hamlet" data-town-name="Bugshaw">         The          <span data-town-type="hamlet">             Hamlet         </span> of          <span data-town-name="Bugshaw">             Bugshaw         </span>     </h1>     <p role="main">         <span data-town-type="hamlet" data-town-name="Bugshaw">             Bugshaw         </span> is          a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="d1f9a521-bfc7-4150-adfb-5f857f7be66a" id="d1f9a521-bfc7-4150-adfb-5f857f7be66a" role="tooltip" title="With a population of 547.">hamlet</span>          located in the arid mountains,          where the vegetation is lush.          Bugshaw grew around a well-traveled crossroads, and is comprised <span class="tippy-races-percentage"></span>. They are       a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="05b11816-08af-4108-a169-67e43ccb9691" id="05b11816-08af-4108-a169-67e43ccb9691" role="tooltip" title="Men occupy most positions of authority.">patriarchal</span>    <span class="tip dotted" data-id="c5f8da03-a32b-4043-a047-096c21d0e7e7" id="c5f8da03-a32b-4043-a047-096c21d0e7e7" role="tooltip" title="Trade and industry are controlled by private owners for profit, rather than the state.">capitalist</span> <span class="tip dotted" data-id="668fd0d2-88b5-4402-b178-ba837b02cc73" id="668fd0d2-88b5-4402-b178-ba837b02cc73" role="tooltip" title="Governed by the scholars.">sophocratic</span> <span class="tip dotted" data-id="b1eb65dc-32a8-4fab-b934-69743a9daa66" id="b1eb65dc-32a8-4fab-b934-69743a9daa66" role="tooltip" title="The crown holds supreme judicial power, but day to day affairs are held by parliament.">constitutional monarchy</span> that <span class="tippy-religion-percentage"></span>.</p></section> <span id="detailed-description" class="tip hide-on-print" title="Find the overview of the town and its sociopolitical structure here!"><a data-passage="TownOutput" class="link-internal" href="#null">Detailed description of Bugshaw</a></span> <br>  <span id="buildings" role="list">                              <p role="listitem">                <br>         At the top of a small hill is the road <a data-id="ed6d7af5-caa3-499d-a759-3d4b334f931f" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal ed6d7af5-caa3-499d-a759-3d4b334f931f" title="Thrahak Road is a rather wide gravel and hewn rock road. It is made of colourful rocks and pebbles. There is a large rock to the side of the road. The name comes from the Thrahak family who wield an amount of political power." href="#ed6d7af5-caa3-499d-a759-3d4b334f931f">Thrahak Road</a>. The name comes from Finelien Goldfinder, who was a well respected local who was killed in war." href="#fe95c8d8-14ea-4c39-a7df-ef48072c80bd">Finelien's Square</a> is                     <a data-id="8d8166e3-d5fa-448e-b30a-107dca99ee86" data-object-type="building" class="link-internal 8d8166e3-d5fa-448e-b30a-107dca99ee86" title="A market that's claustrophobic. It is riddled with the refuse of merchant horses and other livestock, and is known for the entertainers and musicians set up around the bazaar." href="#8d8166e3-d5fa-448e-b30a-107dca99ee86">The Markets</a>     </p>                                           <p role="listitem">                <br>         At the bottom of a hill is <a data-id="2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716" title="Main Street is a path-sized gravel and hewn rock street. Nearby is                      <a data-id="b3f8adaa-4019-491e-8219-dcdc1e86c745" data-object-type="building" class="link-internal b3f8adaa-4019-491e-8219-dcdc1e86c745" title="A somewhat cramped apothecary that's extremely messy, and is known for its wonderful tonics." href="#b3f8adaa-4019-491e-8219-dcdc1e86c745">Marked Liquid</a>     </p>                                           <p role="listitem">                <br>         Along <a data-id="c8e768e0-44a0-4ad3-a239-76129978fb0f" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal c8e768e0-44a0-4ad3-a239-76129978fb0f" title="Wells Row is a narrow gravel and hewn rock road. Their specialty is doing exceptionally good work for fairly decent prices.." href="#9f3bb9c4-8481-4d5f-9198-a6c443071b02">Sew New</a>     </p>                                           <p role="listitem">                <br>         Further towards the centre of Bugshaw is <a data-id="ab084fd0-08e9-4d0e-a2e4-320e42f6e9a3" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal ab084fd0-08e9-4d0e-a2e4-320e42f6e9a3" title="Autumn Street is a wide gravel and hewn rock street. \page

<h2>The Town Square</h2>
<span id="313de281-ff30-4147-931b-1853af52a0f5"></span><p>You're in the town square.  It's relatively large, and somewhat dirty. It features an old, withered cypress tree. Legend says that it will flower on the darkest day of the land, to give the people hope.  As you walk through the square, you see <a data-id="90fc56a8-d234-4b2f-8b79-485c7a44e743" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 90fc56a8-d234-4b2f-8b79-485c7a44e743" title="A light tan skinned built like a brick shithouse dwarf called Kilvar Torunn who is a peasant." href="#90fc56a8-d234-4b2f-8b79-485c7a44e743">a middle aged man with a very narrow waist</a> who is wearing some jewellery that infers they may be royalty of some sort.</p> <p>There's a <a data-id="c3cb6fb4-8eca-4b11-8926-9e28e81d858d" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal c3cb6fb4-8eca-4b11-8926-9e28e81d858d" title="A tan skinned rather small dwarf called Marastyr Burrowfound who is a merchant." href="#c3cb6fb4-8eca-4b11-8926-9e28e81d858d">merchant</a> who is arguing with a man over some attempted haggling. There's also a noticeboard, which has various posters, requests, and announcements tacked to it.</p>   <section id="poster"><span class="macro-live macro-live-block"></span></section>

\page

<h2>The Markets</h2>
<span id="8d8166e3-d5fa-448e-b30a-107dca99ee86"></span><p>You wander through the streets of Bugshaw, and come across the market, which is located in a series of small buildings connected by covered awnings. It seems that the vendors are organised by nothing; the place is a big disorganized mess. The market is known for the entertainers and musicians set up around the bazaar, and is riddled with the refuse of merchant horses and other livestock. Today the market is fairly packed, and people are bustling about and jostling each other to get to certain merchants.</p> <section><h3>Merchants</h3>  <p>A  <a data-id="28d514fc-8a4c-46f6-a3f0-927bf25d0150" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 28d514fc-8a4c-46f6-a3f0-927bf25d0150" title="A prime adult aged woman with a sharp chin called Pynelope Pitt who is a merchant." href="#28d514fc-8a4c-46f6-a3f0-927bf25d0150">prime adult aged human with a sharp chin</a> is beckoning "Dire ferret skins! Dire ferret skins! Even a dwarf would buy at this price!" from a semi-permanent wooden stall.</p>  <p>A  <a data-id="d22452e3-ff6e-4b75-9e15-83c776ddd8d7" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal d22452e3-ff6e-4b75-9e15-83c776ddd8d7" title="An adult dwarf with a long, horselike face called Diesa Rumnaheim who is a merchant." href="#d22452e3-ff6e-4b75-9e15-83c776ddd8d7">quite solidly built female dwarf</a> is selling perfumes and scented oils from a myriad of pockets in the vendor's clothes.</p>  <p>Off to the side, a  <a data-id="98a206db-8a47-4bb8-a34d-dde7b66c8eb3" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 98a206db-8a47-4bb8-a34d-dde7b66c8eb3" title="A fair skinned rather squat dwarf called Oskar Foamtankard who is a merchant." href="#98a206db-8a47-4bb8-a34d-dde7b66c8eb3">fair skinned rather squat dwarf</a> is hawking goods, saying "Light the way with my candle helmet! Be the envy of your friends!" from a sizable horse-drawn wagon.</p>  <p>Off to the side, a  <a data-id="b5f63f8e-9591-4158-913d-66b33e3cc005" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal b5f63f8e-9591-4158-913d-66b33e3cc005" title="A dwarf with a scraggly beard called Olunt Loderr who is a merchant." href="#b5f63f8e-9591-4158-913d-66b33e3cc005">somewhat tiny male dwarf</a> is shouting out "Cure that painful boil with my all-in-one healing tincture!<blockquote>It's just rancid vinegar</blockquote> Essential for the intrepid adventurer!" from a racks of goods set up in a circle.</p> </section>

<h2>Marked Liquid</h2>
<span class="flex-line"></span> <span id="b3f8adaa-4019-491e-8219-dcdc1e86c745"></span><p>You enter Marked Liquid, a shabby hewn rock apothecary with a white tiled roof. Looking around, Marked Liquid must have had an explosion the day before; there is no other possible reason that a shop that deals with magical, often volatile chemicals would be so cluttered, crowded, and blatantly a danger to itself and the half-mile radius surrounding it. There are pots and pans of mixtures that have already spilt over crowding the desk, with potions that are currently brewing strewn around the floor. There's little hope to walk through the shop without putting your boot in something that you probably would prefer not to put it in. Just as you try and hesitate, you hear the distinct sound of 'no, please don't go!' come from the floorboards, which at first seemed to be sticky, but on closer inspection, was more... 'grabby'. There is a chemist behind the shop counter currently pouring ingredients into a tube.</p> <section><h3>Chemist</h3><p>a very tall man with very rounded ears welcomes you warmly while you look around. He introduces himself as <a data-id="db6e2980-9267-4a78-9445-ec70589b1a87" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal db6e2980-9267-4a78-9445-ec70589b1a87" title="A very tall man with very rounded ears called Antonyr Underwood who is an alchemist." href="#db6e2980-9267-4a78-9445-ec70589b1a87">Antonyr Underwood</a>, the proud owner of the shop, and asks what he can do for you.</p>  <h6>Antonyr Underwood</h6>Antonyr looks concerned, and idly shifts a box of wispstalks as he talks. The very tall man talks about the weather as he carefully measures out ingredients for a new potion as you peruse the shop. Antonyr tells you that he is working on a component for a summoning ritual, and points to the <span class="macro-linkappend">quite large glass pot</span><span class="macro-linkappend-insert macro-linkappend-in">. Looking inside the pot, you see a chunky blue liquid with constantly moving and shifting liquid bubbling away</span>.</section> <span class="macro-live macro-live-block"></span> <span class="click-and-remove-link"><b>Generate a random potion!</b></span> <span class="macro-live macro-live-block"></span> <h6>Marked Liquid's Potions and Wares</h6><div class="descriptive">    Antonyr Underwood smiles, and says "What are you after? <h2>Ashburn Grave</h2>
<br><span id="585c6515-6dc5-4e1c-b9c0-9ef0a8e41a09"></span><p>Ashburn Grave is chiseled into an enormous glacier and was built as a later addition.  It is known for being haunted by vengeful ghosts, and consists of organized around a large central cell block or pit.  It is rumoured that hidden inside the dungeon is the preserved head of an ancient villain.</p> <h4>Cells</h4><p>The cells inside the dungeon are aging, but sturdy; the walls have some cracks, and prisoners are kept in cells that accommodate up to two prisoners, each shackled to the wall.</p> <p>Prisoners of Ashburn Grave are treated like dogs; they receive poor quality meals and enough healing to keep them alive. The jailer, <a data-id="15c70e01-539c-4186-92c0-4f0ef5ecf436" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 15c70e01-539c-4186-92c0-4f0ef5ecf436" title="An extremely obese female dwarf with a wide ribcage called Gillydd Gorunn who is a jailer." href="#15c70e01-539c-4186-92c0-4f0ef5ecf436">Gillydd Gorunn</a>, is a haunted woman who applied to job to ulitmately free their lover, only for them to die before she had the chance.</p> <span class="click-and-remove-link"><b>Meet a prisoner</b></span> <span class="macro-live macro-live-block"><div id="prisoners"></div></span> <div id="BuildingRelationshipsTable">   <div class="classTable">   <table>     <tr>       <th>Name</th>       <th>Race</th>       <th>Occupation</th>       <th>Relationship</th>     </tr>            <tr>         <td><a data-id="15c70e01-539c-4186-92c0-4f0ef5ecf436" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 15c70e01-539c-4186-92c0-4f0ef5ecf436" title="An extremely obese female dwarf with a wide ribcage called Gillydd Gorunn who is a jailer." href="#15c70e01-539c-4186-92c0-4f0ef5ecf436">Gillydd Gorunn</a></td>         <td>Dwarf</td>         <td><span class="tip dotted" data-id="d3a57683-8c7e-4edf-85e0-027e507d5193" id="d3a57683-8c7e-4edf-85e0-027e507d5193" role="tooltip" title="Supervises a jail and the prisoners in it.">Jailer</span></td>         <td>                      <span class="tip dotted" data-id="147383df-9b39-452c-827b-641a8b788a42" id="147383df-9b39-452c-827b-641a8b788a42" role="tooltip" title="Ashburn Grave is a workplace to Gillydd">Jailer</span>                    </td>       </tr>        </table> </div>  </div><br>

<h2>The Famed Fabricator</h2>
<span class="flex-line"></span> <span id="5f855fcf-984b-4cb2-a420-b961b684c987"></span> <p>You make your way down <span class="tip dotted" data-id="ac3b370c-b2a5-4e30-be6e-7fd0fe08c8fb" id="ac3b370c-b2a5-4e30-be6e-7fd0fe08c8fb" role="tooltip" title="Pope Street is a rather wide gravel and hewn rock street. It is a loose gravel that was taken from a river bed. There's a wagon with a cracked wheel by the side of the road. ">Pope Street</span>, and enter The Famed Fabricator and see that inside, the shabby hewn rock farrier shop with a straw roof is cavernous. The smithy is fastidious, with a swept floor and tools stored neatly on the walls. There's a desk in the corner with a piece of parchment showing the current project's measurements, and the materials are neatly stored in bins. Clearly, whatever apprentice has been charged with upkeep of the smithy has taken their job very seriously. You can see that activity in The Famed Fabricator is very busy. There is a blacksmith currently picking his nose.</p> <p>On the bench lies a morning star. It's obviously amateurish. Alvyn moves around the shop, unsure of himself, betraying his lack of skills. <section><h3>Blacksmith</h3><p>The blacksmith nods at you when you come inside. He introduces himself as <a data-id="c8dbb261-15fc-46bc-9799-2a1e7a13b81f" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal c8dbb261-15fc-46bc-9799-2a1e7a13b81f" title="A somewhat squat male gnome with colorfully painted nails called Alvyn Gimlen who is a farrier." href="#c8dbb261-15fc-46bc-9799-2a1e7a13b81f">Alvyn Gimlen</a>, the proprietor of the smithy, and asks what he can do for you.</p> <br><h6>Alvyn Gimlen</h6>Alvyn looks content, and while you chat, he moves around the shop, preparing a new project for work. Alvyn finds working in the smithy fun, and says that the patrons of The Famed Fabricator are somewhat stingy.<br><br><br><span class="macro-live macro-live-block"></span></section> <span class="macro-live macro-live-block"></span> <span class="macro-linkappend"><h4>Buy something</h4></span><div class="descriptive"> "I'm not sure what you might find of interest- just a bunch of horseshoes and nails. Be my guest, though." The somewhat squat male gnome with colorfully painted nails says, apparently well aware that the smithy isn't exactly doing too well.</div> <h2>The Hibiscus Bush Herb Shop</h2>
<span id="a6319684-6fc2-489b-988c-3efac85097ca"></span><br>You come inside The Hibiscus Bush Herb Shop, a shabby hewn rock building with a decently built straw roof. <h2>The Bugshaw Boot Shop</h2>
<span id="e3a37436-de29-4f29-8ce7-59ea1c1832e2"></span><br>You come inside a shabby hewn rock shoemaker shop with a decently built straw roof called The Bugshaw Boot Shop. You notice several finely made paintings of shoes hanging on different walls.<br><br>This shoemaker shop is known for mostly making shoes for women. There is a <a data-id="9f200a5a-aed8-4156-abe7-b1bb4e0297d4" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 9f200a5a-aed8-4156-abe7-b1bb4e0297d4" title="A somewhat short male half-orc called Druuk Prathka who is a shoemaker." href="#9f200a5a-aed8-4156-abe7-b1bb4e0297d4">somewhat short male half-orc</a> currently starting to knod off in a corner of the room. He welcomes you, and asks what you are after.<br><br>       <table>   <tr>    <th>Goods</th>    <th>Cost</th>   </tr>                                   <tr>      <td>                  <span class="tip dotted" data-id="6413dc76-21fa-4c26-9f18-f30be3620f6f" id="6413dc76-21fa-4c26-9f18-f30be3620f6f" role="tooltip" title="A pair of barely ankle height boots made of some kind of leather">Short boots</span>             </td>      <td> 1 Silver</td>     </tr>                                   <tr>      <td>                  <span class="tip dotted" data-id="4b2933c8-8e2b-40ee-bf9f-7c6b480934ff" id="4b2933c8-8e2b-40ee-bf9f-7c6b480934ff" role="tooltip" title="A tall pair of thick leather boots">High boots</span>             </td>      <td> 1 Silver 5 Copper</td>     </tr>                                   <tr>      <td>                  <span class="tip dotted" data-id="eeb9094f-2a17-40d6-8912-710e7ce4f631" id="eeb9094f-2a17-40d6-8912-710e7ce4f631" role="tooltip" title="A fine looking pair of shoes with a thick heel on the back">Heeled shoes</span>             </td>      <td> 1 Silver</td>     </tr>                                   <tr>      <td>                  <span class="tip dotted" data-id="addd8bc6-4ceb-41ac-81a1-4d694df8ded2" id="addd8bc6-4ceb-41ac-81a1-4d694df8ded2" role="tooltip" title="A fancy looking pair of shoes made to wear to formal events">Dress shoes</span>             </td>      <td> 2 Silver 5 Copper</td>     </tr>                                   <tr>      <td>                  <span class="tip dotted" data-id="2a96765c-d76b-4620-a11e-5fda982d3e35" id="2a96765c-d76b-4620-a11e-5fda982d3e35" role="tooltip" title="Repair services for shoes or boots of any kind within reason">Shoe repair</span>             </td>      <td> 1 Silver</td>     </tr>     </table>  <br>

<h2>Rusty's Cutlass</h2>
<span id="c27da45c-e3b7-4c1d-9b9c-a2a941d1d9b5"></span><p>You make your way down <span class="tip dotted" data-id="b0960f45-d68a-4102-8ca1-ab810f1e1541" id="b0960f45-d68a-4102-8ca1-ab810f1e1541" role="tooltip" title="Gunnloa Street is a narrow gravel and hewn rock street. It is made of poorly packed gravel, which shifts around under foot. Grated storm drains at regular intervals grant access to the sewer system. It has been named after Gunnloa Durthane, who was a much beloved prostitute, one of whose clients bought the road as a thankyou.">Gunnloa Street</span>, and enter Rusty's Cutlass a shabby hewn rock building with a decently built straw roof. Inside, the huge hewn rock building is fastidious. You notice several pieces of pottery with very vulgar acts painted on them. When people talk about Rusty's Cutlass, they say you can pay for the services offered with criminal favors. Apparently, it specialises in discrete service for high end clientele. Rumours abound in whorehouses, and Rusty's Cutlass is no different; apparently, all the beds are infested with bedbugs.</p> <section><h3>Brothel Mistress</h3> <p>The Mistress is pouring over a book titled The Complete Works of Archilochus, she appears to be a large madam with a no-nonsense attitude. As soon as you enter the dwarf smiles, greets you, and walks over to where you are. She introduces herself as <a data-id="4569e416-b02c-4ae2-8187-b5acc0186187" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 4569e416-b02c-4ae2-8187-b5acc0186187" title="An old woman with thick braids of hair banded with gold called Artin Battlehammer who is a pimp." href="#4569e416-b02c-4ae2-8187-b5acc0186187">Artin Battlehammer</a>, the Mistress of Rusty's Cutlass, and asks what she can do for you.</p></section>  <span class="macro-live macro-live-block"></span> <details id="CreateNewNpc" open=""><summary>Customers</summary> <div id="BuildingRelationshipsTable">   <div class="classTable">   <table>     <tr>       <th>Name</th>       <th>Race</th>       <th>Occupation</th>       <th>Relationship</th>     </tr>            <tr>         <td><a data-id="4569e416-b02c-4ae2-8187-b5acc0186187" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 4569e416-b02c-4ae2-8187-b5acc0186187" title="A somewhat tiny female dwarf called Artin Battlehammer who is a pimp." href="#4569e416-b02c-4ae2-8187-b5acc0186187">Artin Battlehammer</a></td>         <td>Dwarf</td>         <td><span class="tip dotted" data-id="4899ee49-612c-4a31-a871-e2ee018a3fb7" id="4899ee49-612c-4a31-a871-e2ee018a3fb7" role="tooltip" title="Controls prostitutes and arranges clients for them, taking part of their earnings in return.">Pimp</span></td>         <td>                      <span class="tip dotted" data-id="e2008d4f-87ea-46bf-8ce7-9ac8763f0eb6" id="e2008d4f-87ea-46bf-8ce7-9ac8763f0eb6" role="tooltip" title="Owns Rusty's Cutlass.">Pimp</span>                    </td>       </tr>        </table> </div>  </div></details>

There is a <a data-id="1f2c392b-cf56-48fd-a228-16a8e75ce96b" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 1f2c392b-cf56-48fd-a228-16a8e75ce96b" title="A rather small woman with nails sharpened to a point called Falkrann Fahack who is a barber." href="#1f2c392b-cf56-48fd-a228-16a8e75ce96b">rather small woman with nails sharpened to a point</a> currently playing cards. <h2>The Church of Consecrated Souls</h2>
<span id="9421eee5-6a99-4648-9a39-2b8bfa69e9c1"></span><p>You come across a shabby hewn rock church with a thatched roof. This church is protected by sellswords.</p> <p>You enter the large, rather messy church and notice a kneeler beneath a small statue or icon. The main room is octagonal in shape and is decorated with mostly wealthy looking holy art. The interior walls of the church are actually the hollowed husk of an enormous tree and the the ceiling is connected to the floor by columns. The church was designed by a renowned theologian of the clergy and it is arranged in a concentric fashion; the inner areas are inaccessible to most visitors.</p> <p>Within this holy place they pray to one god, but not the one the temple was originally dedicated to. The temple itself was originally dedicated to friendship and community and is known for dancing monks.</p> <h3>Priest</h3> <p>A temple priest is currently placing some nice smelling incense in a dirty looking incense holder. The priest greets you, and introduces himself as <a data-id="2df24fb6-82c5-411c-869a-9a872a88a8f0" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 2df24fb6-82c5-411c-869a-9a872a88a8f0" title="A somewhat squat male dwarf called Erias Eversharp who is a deacon." href="#2df24fb6-82c5-411c-869a-9a872a88a8f0">Erias Eversharp</a>. He informs you the temple has confessionals open if you wish to confess.</p> <h6>Blessing</h6> <p class="descriptive">The priest raises his hand above you and mumbles some words in a language you do not understand. You are told by the priest that you are now blessed with a depth of feeling that was locked deep within you.</p> <span class="macro-linkappend"><h4>Buy something</h4></span> <h2>The Brotherhood of Knowledge Holders</h2>
<span id="leader"></span> <span class="flex-line">    </span> <p class="no-indent"><span class="first-character">T</span>he Brotherhood of Knowledge Holders is a scholars guild. It's new, and the very small faction has an excellent reputation, and is motivated by fame. They are rumoured to own a powerful artifact.</p>  <section><h3>Governance</h3> <p>It's ruled by     <a data-id="22369fb4-68a3-494b-85ea-7d3ed282214e" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 22369fb4-68a3-494b-85ea-7d3ed282214e" title="A fair skinned built like a brick shithouse dwarf called Eridred Durthane who is a professor." href="#22369fb4-68a3-494b-85ea-7d3ed282214e">Eridred Durthane</a>, who was the most charismatic of the group. She is reasonably competent, and her position is stable due to internal power struggles. Bribes are sometimes accepted. </p></section> <p><h3>Members</h3>Members of The Brotherhood of Knowledge Holders are identifiable by the ring that members are given. Membership requires referral by an existing member, and costs a single gold piece. The initiation into The Brotherhood of Knowledge Holders involves a simple form to be filled.</p>  <div id="NPC"></div> <div id="BuildingRelationshipsTable">    <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary> <table> <tr>   <th>Name</th>   <th>Race</th>   <th>Occupation</th>   <th>Relationship</th> </tr>    <tr><td><a data-id="22369fb4-68a3-494b-85ea-7d3ed282214e" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 22369fb4-68a3-494b-85ea-7d3ed282214e" title="A fair skinned built like a brick shithouse dwarf called Eridred Durthane who is a professor." href="#22369fb4-68a3-494b-85ea-7d3ed282214e">Eridred Durthane</a></td>   <td>Dwarf</td>   <td><span class="tip dotted" data-id="dbf5e8e9-bda1-4fbe-a703-3106923d4dd3" id="dbf5e8e9-bda1-4fbe-a703-3106923d4dd3" role="tooltip" title="A teacher of the highest rank in a college or university.">Professor</span></td>   <td><span class="tip dotted" data-id="2d179e54-4596-4c36-a26c-eab10e3734ba" id="2d179e54-4596-4c36-a26c-eab10e3734ba" role="tooltip" title="[object Object] is the leader of The Brotherhood of Knowledge Holders, and is reasonably competent.">Head of Faction</span></td></tr>  </table></details> </div> </div> <section><h3>Resources</h3><p>They have limitless resources.      A handful of debtors     are jealously guarded, as are               one or two valuable magical weapons,              a significant number of gems,              a handful of magical trinkets,          and sheafs of magic scrolls. </p></section> <h3>Politics</h3>The Brotherhood of Knowledge Holders have a handful of trusted allies; <br>     A guild of craftsmen and more than a couple rangers can be called on for aid.    The Brotherhood of Knowledge Holders have more enemies than one would expect;      A guild of bandits     wish ill of The Brotherhood of Knowledge Holders. Their other enemies also include               a guild of priests,          and a guild of bandits.

\page

<h2>The Bugshaw Poems</h2>
<span id="4e9d6125-84a4-4466-9afc-1656f996e113"></span> <span class="flex-line">    </span> <p class="no-indent"><span class="first-character">T</span>he Bugshaw Poems is a bards college. It's relatively new, and the miniscule faction has an excellent reputation, and is motivated by fame. They are against the current political regime.</p>  <section><h3>Governance</h3> <p>It's ruled by     <a data-id="6c910ab4-f5db-468c-a838-f08c52e11dd3" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 6c910ab4-f5db-468c-a838-f08c52e11dd3" title="A quite solidly built male dwarf called Kildrak Holderhek who is a bard." href="#6c910ab4-f5db-468c-a838-f08c52e11dd3">Kildrak Holderhek</a>, who was the strongest of the group. He is somewhat incompetent, and his position is very unstable due to conflicts with rivaling factions. Bribes will be met with laughter. </p></section> <p><h3>Members</h3>Members of The Bugshaw Poems are identifiable by the ring that members are given. Membership requires a display of skill, and costs ten gold pieces. The initiation into The Bugshaw Poems involves a secret ritual.</p>  <div id="NPC"></div> <div id="BuildingRelationshipsTable">    <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary> <table> <tr>   <th>Name</th>   <th>Race</th>   <th>Occupation</th>   <th>Relationship</th> </tr>    <tr><td><a data-id="6c910ab4-f5db-468c-a838-f08c52e11dd3" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 6c910ab4-f5db-468c-a838-f08c52e11dd3" title="A quite solidly built male dwarf called Kildrak Holderhek who is a bard." href="#6c910ab4-f5db-468c-a838-f08c52e11dd3">Kildrak Holderhek</a></td>   <td>Dwarf</td>   <td><span class="tip dotted" data-id="106008b5-8306-499e-a6f8-8f13d6fcba4a" id="106008b5-8306-499e-a6f8-8f13d6fcba4a" role="tooltip" title="Uses their artistic talents to induce magical effects.">Bard</span></td>   <td><span class="tip dotted" data-id="e5ba6413-6dfb-4399-913d-976499cb4caf" id="e5ba6413-6dfb-4399-913d-976499cb4caf" role="tooltip" title="[object Object] is the leader of The Bugshaw Poems, and is somewhat incompetent.">Head of Faction</span></td></tr>  </table></details> </div> </div> <section><h3>Resources</h3><p>They have quite poor resources.      A handful of magical trinkets and a drawer of blackmail material are their only significant resources.   </p></section> <h3>Politics</h3>The Bugshaw Poems have few allies; <br>     A large number of priests are the only others they can rely on.    The Bugshaw Poems have some enemies;      A guild of bandits and a guild of bandits are the only that wish The Bugshaw Poems ill.

\page

<h2>The Collective of Memorized Evokers</h2>
<span id="7702d28c-f33e-4da7-9b2d-073eea621f26"></span> <span class="flex-line">    </span> <p class="no-indent"><span class="first-character">T</span>he Collective of Memorized Evokers is a wizards college. It's ancient, and the quite small faction has an excellent reputation, and is motivated by vengeance. They are rumoured to own a powerful artifact.</p>  <section><h3>Governance</h3> <p>It's ruled by     <a data-id="235fc7f0-e90d-46c6-9be6-648fd5f6bef5" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 235fc7f0-e90d-46c6-9be6-648fd5f6bef5" title="A dark tan skinned quite squat dwarf called Orsik Silverstone who is a wizard." href="#235fc7f0-e90d-46c6-9be6-648fd5f6bef5">Orsik Silverstone</a>, who was able to rise to power through nepotism. He is of mild incompetence, and his position is stable due to internal power struggles. Bribes are sometimes accepted. </p></section> <p><h3>Members</h3>Members of The Collective of Memorized Evokers are identifiable by the sash that members are given. Membership requires some social status, and costs three hundred gold pieces, provided there's an empty slot. The initiation into The Collective of Memorized Evokers involves an oath to be taken.</p>  <div id="NPC"></div> <div id="BuildingRelationshipsTable">    <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary> <table> <tr>   <th>Name</th>   <th>Race</th>   <th>Occupation</th>   <th>Relationship</th> </tr>    <tr><td><a data-id="235fc7f0-e90d-46c6-9be6-648fd5f6bef5" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 235fc7f0-e90d-46c6-9be6-648fd5f6bef5" title="A dark tan skinned quite squat dwarf called Orsik Silverstone who is a wizard." href="#235fc7f0-e90d-46c6-9be6-648fd5f6bef5">Orsik Silverstone</a></td>   <td>Dwarf</td>   <td><span class="tip dotted" data-id="2c79c92e-13dd-4de8-8aa5-42ef1a04c87c" id="2c79c92e-13dd-4de8-8aa5-42ef1a04c87c" role="tooltip" title="Derives their magical abilities through study.">Wizard</span></td>   <td><span class="tip dotted" data-id="b7b9ff7f-6265-4964-9afa-9552c13476db" id="b7b9ff7f-6265-4964-9afa-9552c13476db" role="tooltip" title="[object Object] is the leader of The Collective of Memorized Evokers, and is of mild incompetence.">Head of Faction</span></td></tr>  </table></details> </div> </div> <section><h3>Resources</h3><p>They have significant resources.      A drawer of magic scrolls     are in their proverbial warchest, as are               a handful of favours,              a handful of gems,          and a handful of debtors. </p></section> <h3>Politics</h3>The Collective of Memorized Evokers have few allies; <br>     A veritable army of bandits are the only others they can rely on.    The Collective of Memorized Evokers have some fearsome enemies;      A guild of assassins     are rivals. Other enemies include               a guild of seers,              a guild of assassins,          and a guild of priests.

<h2>The Truncheon of Bugshaw</h2>
<span id="a30067a9-e4b7-44a7-bf1e-aa74c832fe11"></span> <span class="flex-line">    </span> <p class="no-indent"><span class="first-character">T</span>he Truncheon of Bugshaw is a guards watch. It's recently established, and the quite small faction has an excellent reputation, and is motivated by money. They are rumoured to be under investigation.</p> <section><h3>Policing</h3><p>Bugshaw is policed by The Truncheon of Bugshaw, rather than a separate guard. The guard is underfunded, and their equipment is always in slight disrepair. Their officers are held accountable for their actions when public pressure fors for it, though The Truncheon of Bugshaw does not have the funding to perform training exercises.<br>One can recognise a member of The Truncheon of Bugshaw by the dark grey and white livery adorned with an image of an octopus.</p></section><br><section><h4>Law in Bugshaw</h4>Law in Bugshaw is very much punitive based, and those that breach the laws can expect hard labor, incarceration, or sometimes public execution. Crime is an ugly stain on humanity, to be punished.</section> <section><h3>Governance</h3> <p>It's ruled by     <a data-id="d30e76cd-2bc7-475b-a9bb-95ba914a70a6" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal d30e76cd-2bc7-475b-a9bb-95ba914a70a6" title="An unbelievably large dwarven man called Taklinn Ironfist who is a fighter." href="#d30e76cd-2bc7-475b-a9bb-95ba914a70a6">Taklinn Ironfist</a>, who was able to rise to power by completing an ordeal. He is quite competent, and his position is relatively stable due to internal power struggles. Bribes are sometimes accepted. </p></section> <p><h3>Members</h3>Members of The Truncheon of Bugshaw are identifiable by their love of a good fight. Membership requires some social status, and costs twenty gold pieces. The initiation into The Truncheon of Bugshaw involves a simple form to be filled.</p>  <div id="NPC"></div> <div id="BuildingRelationshipsTable">    <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary> <table> <tr>   <th>Name</th>   <th>Race</th>   <th>Occupation</th>   <th>Relationship</th> </tr>    <tr><td><a data-id="d30e76cd-2bc7-475b-a9bb-95ba914a70a6" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal d30e76cd-2bc7-475b-a9bb-95ba914a70a6" title="An unbelievably large dwarven man called Taklinn Ironfist who is a fighter." href="#d30e76cd-2bc7-475b-a9bb-95ba914a70a6">Taklinn Ironfist</a></td>   <td>Dwarf</td>   <td><span class="tip dotted" data-id="14132126-a93d-44a8-8a23-fa7d08b7396a" id="14132126-a93d-44a8-8a23-fa7d08b7396a" role="tooltip" title="A common warrior.">Fighter</span></td>   <td><span class="tip dotted" data-id="396164bd-8cc7-49fc-9f62-df8f2b674835" id="396164bd-8cc7-49fc-9f62-df8f2b674835" role="tooltip" title="[object Object] is the leader of The Truncheon of Bugshaw, and is quite competent.">Head of Faction</span></td></tr>  </table></details> </div> </div> <section><h3>Resources</h3><p>They have extensive resources.      A significant number of gems     are part of those resources. Also at their disposal are               a handful of contacts,              a handful of magic scrolls,          and a handful of magical weapons. </p></section> <h3>Politics</h3>The Truncheon of Bugshaw have some strong allies; <br>     A veritable army of knights and a veritable army of merchants can be called on for aid.    The Truncheon of Bugshaw have some fearsome enemies;      A guild of assassins     are rivals. Other enemies include               a guild of thieves,              a guild of bandits,          and a guild of assassins.

<h2>Travok Frostbeard</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /tɹɑvʌk fɹɔstbɪɹd /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="33dd9ac4-862f-4ba4-a45d-f28a0832ae59">          <span class="first-character">T</span>ravok Frostbeard    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="eb69f77c-18cc-4592-8458-0f2cd02b7308" id="eb69f77c-18cc-4592-8458-0f2cd02b7308" role="tooltip" title="41 years old, to be exact.">an early middle aged</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="999d1eb0-a192-4fa9-8007-fe1a13452039" id="999d1eb0-a192-4fa9-8007-fe1a13452039" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 3″">quite squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="707e1f20-642e-4d07-889d-66ec04c84fd6" id="707e1f20-642e-4d07-889d-66ec04c84fd6" role="tooltip" title="192lbs. (with a BMI of 36)">quite large</span>, and has brown eyes        and a rather wild, unkempt beard,    with brown skin.    The most notable physical trait of Travok is that he has a ring of thorns tattoo. </p> <p>   Travok sweats profusely and easily.            He is temperate and slow to believe in people.     When he is relaxed, he is reserved.  In moments of stress, he becomes stubborn.  Religion-wise, Travok is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="80d50725-d568-4ccb-8450-6bbe6c70bd9d" id="80d50725-d568-4ccb-8450-6bbe6c70bd9d" role="tooltip" title="Travok is a faithful follower of undefined, and enjoys confronting others to challenge beliefs that differ from his own.">an outspoken believer</span>.  <p>          Perhaps due to sexism,       Travok has recently been slightly unsuccessful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="b14bfb8c-f4ac-4d89-8e38-02f62a555f17" id="b14bfb8c-f4ac-4d89-8e38-02f62a555f17" role="tooltip" title="Unlawfully occupies an uninhabited building or unused land.">squatter</span>, with a background of being a peasant.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="1d2d16fd-e259-4d9d-a567-f452446a52de" id="1d2d16fd-e259-4d9d-a567-f452446a52de" role="tooltip" title="Travok lives a squalid existence, eating terrible food with no alcohol, and few creature comforts">paupery</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Travok currently has 7 sp in his pockets,    and 70 Gold 1 Silver 9 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="36400128-f336-4c8e-9072-030ddab0d4a1" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 36400128-f336-4c8e-9072-030ddab0d4a1" title="Duke Road is a wide paved rock road. <h2>Whurbin Fire-Forge</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /wɝbɪn undefinedundefined /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="748556c0-9087-4dd7-9194-ee75c3570e85">          <span class="first-character">W</span>hurbin Fire-Forge    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="5ef44335-e827-4457-8f19-34709869af56" id="5ef44335-e827-4457-8f19-34709869af56" role="tooltip" title="118 years old, to be exact.">a middle aged</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="47bac89c-c529-4a07-9cc5-0fb06fb7ccf8" id="47bac89c-c529-4a07-9cc5-0fb06fb7ccf8" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 3″">quite squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="38e93dac-99b4-4855-bfa9-af3a6b98450f" id="38e93dac-99b4-4855-bfa9-af3a6b98450f" role="tooltip" title="186lbs. (with a BMI of 35)">built like a brick shithouse</span>, and has blue eyes        and a long, flowing beard,    with fair skin.    The most notable physical trait of Whurbin is that he has a rather bony chin. </p> <p>   Whurbin has poor hygiene.            He is subjective.     When he is relaxed, he is dour.  In moments of stress, he becomes destructive.  Religion-wise, Whurbin is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="ecb40402-6e16-4a64-b2d3-1946a215bc69" id="ecb40402-6e16-4a64-b2d3-1946a215bc69" role="tooltip" title="Whurbin Fire-Forge is a casual follower of Artemis, and can be quite rude towards those who worship 'inferior' gods.">an open-minded seeker</span> of <a data-id="artemis" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal artemis" title="Artemis is the goddess of the Hunt and young girls. She can change others into animals as punishment for transgressions against her and she demands appropriate respect from mortals." href="#artemis">Artemis</a>.  <p>          Perhaps due to sexism,       Whurbin is a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="c44e3007-5b72-4e98-b053-b80139826424" id="c44e3007-5b72-4e98-b053-b80139826424" role="tooltip" title="A person belonging to a class with high social or political status.">noble</span>, with a background of being a noble.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="ae9534d8-5036-4425-8b5d-c1cb78c4a888" id="ae9534d8-5036-4425-8b5d-c1cb78c4a888" role="tooltip" title="Whurbin lives a comfortable life, filled with good food and wine">nobility</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Whurbin currently has 12 sp and 7 gp in his pockets,    and 200 Gold 6 Silver 1 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="36400128-f336-4c8e-9072-030ddab0d4a1" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 36400128-f336-4c8e-9072-030ddab0d4a1" title="Duke Road is a wide paved rock road. It is made of polished marble, intricately paved to form repeating geometric pattern. There is a large rock to the side of the road. " href="#36400128-f336-4c8e-9072-030ddab0d4a1">Duke Road</a>.               Whurbin knows Common and Dwarvish.                 Whurbin has a wife, <a data-id="b4507891-46b5-4aa5-b149-15e9f3edc20c" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal b4507891-46b5-4aa5-b149-15e9f3edc20c" title="A built like a wrestler dwarven woman called Whurdred Deepdelver who is a courtier." href="#b4507891-46b5-4aa5-b149-15e9f3edc20c">Whurdred Deepdelver</a>.    </p> <section>Whurbin currently earns 2 Gold 5 Silver 7 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>3 Gold 6 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 6 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>2 Gold 5 Silver 7 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="788ab4a0-9ca8-4c6d-b7ab-7a919530fc02" id="788ab4a0-9ca8-4c6d-b7ab-7a919530fc02" role="tooltip" title="Whurbin lives a comfortable life, filled with good food and wine">comfortable</span>)</td><td>2 Gold 9 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 3 Silver 5 Copper</td></tr>          <tr><td>Money owed to <a data-id="33dd9ac4-862f-4ba4-a45d-f28a0832ae59" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 33dd9ac4-862f-4ba4-a45d-f28a0832ae59" title="A quite large male dwarf called Travok Frostbeard who is a squatter." href="#33dd9ac4-862f-4ba4-a45d-f28a0832ae59">Travok Frostbeard</a></td><td>107 Gold 1 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by my extended family as an only child. I had a comfortable upbringing in a rundown shack.  I had a few close friends, and my childhood was a relatively normal one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a noble</summary> <div class="descriptive">"My family has been disgraced, and I intend to restore our once pristine reputation. I earnt my place as a noble, working tirelessly day in, day out. Nothing is more important that the other members of my family. It is my duty to respect the authority of those above me"</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I used to play cards in a pub, and one time supposedly cheated a <a data-id="387de87d-7c3f-422e-8ada-f71e3a4221f3" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 387de87d-7c3f-422e-8ada-f71e3a4221f3" title="An ancient dwarf with feet like a chimp called Barendd Bofdarm who is a peasant." href="#387de87d-7c3f-422e-8ada-f71e3a4221f3">man</a> out of his winnings; it was a misunderstanding, but I cannot convince him otherwise. I would rather have backup the next time that I face him. How could I ever forget the time I met the love of my life, who is no longer with me. At one point to pay off a debt, I spent some time as a noble. There was this one time, I once found a cursed book. The book sucked the reader in to a nightmarish world. I forget exactly when, but at one point, I was caught and convicted of racketeering, and spent 4 years chained to an oar before being released. To pay off a debt, I had to work as a noble.I was on a long journey when I found a Maverick Mirror of Malediction.<blockquote><h4>Maverick Mirror of Malediction</h4>The bearer has a +1 bonus to any skill check involving gambling and games of chance (Insight, Sleight of Hand, Investigation, etc). Contains 1d4 unreplenishable charges of the Bane spell(1st level).</blockquote>After that, I was falsely accused of murder, but eventually was acquitted. It took up years of my life, though, and I still get antsy around guards that I don't know.You might not believe it, but I spent some time working as a noble. <h2>Garur Morigak</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ɡɹɝ mɔɹʌɡʌk /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="09fc91a8-73db-42b4-9590-420aa14a05cd">          <span class="first-character">G</span>arur Morigak    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="c5990b78-8e25-4638-8f02-3998a864fecf" id="c5990b78-8e25-4638-8f02-3998a864fecf" role="tooltip" title="84 years old, to be exact.">a middle aged</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="742ae6f6-9146-4f9b-8b35-71246fceaf11" id="742ae6f6-9146-4f9b-8b35-71246fceaf11" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 4″">quite squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="8bd04be2-0503-4919-8aff-5e8b729d77f2" id="8bd04be2-0503-4919-8aff-5e8b729d77f2" role="tooltip" title="192lbs. (with a BMI of 35)">quite large</span>, and has gray eyes        and a dreadful beard,    with pale skin.    The most notable physical trait of Garur is that he has a wide chin. </p> <p>   Garur often sniffs audibly.         He has a severe underbite.        When he is relaxed, he is fearful.  In moments of stress, he becomes secretive.  Religion-wise, Garur is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="c127484a-a7e8-4ea7-81a4-5cacb069caeb" id="c127484a-a7e8-4ea7-81a4-5cacb069caeb" role="tooltip" title="Garur Morigak is critical of religion, but is nominally a follower of Zeus. Despite his supposed faith, he enjoys ragging on any and all religions, and will openly criticize any faithful people he meets.">a critical student</span> of <a data-id="zeus" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal zeus" title="Zeus is the leader of the Greek gods, and lives atop Mount Olympus, where he rules over the mortal world below." href="#zeus">Zeus</a>.  <p>      Garur is a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="31a61cf6-0325-4c30-bc9c-19787872b854" id="31a61cf6-0325-4c30-bc9c-19787872b854" role="tooltip" title="Bets money on sports, card games, or games of chance in the hope of a profit.">gambler</span>, with a background of being a peasant.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="7ae0df76-cb66-423b-b519-59e8ad398350" id="7ae0df76-cb66-423b-b519-59e8ad398350" role="tooltip" title="Garur lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">peasantry</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Garur currently has a compass in his pockets,    and 110 Gold 2 Silver 9 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="ab084fd0-08e9-4d0e-a2e4-320e42f6e9a3" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal ab084fd0-08e9-4d0e-a2e4-320e42f6e9a3" title="Autumn Street is a wide gravel and hewn rock street. It is a loose gravel that was taken from a river bed. There's a bench on the side of the road, with the wood being smoothed out from many sittings. " href="#ab084fd0-08e9-4d0e-a2e4-320e42f6e9a3">Autumn Street</a>.               Garur knows Common and Dwarvish.           </p> <section>Garur currently earns 1 Gold 2 Silver 2 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 3 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 8.5 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="f33e5a5f-c54d-48e0-9082-be0f19e75eee" id="f33e5a5f-c54d-48e0-9082-be0f19e75eee" role="tooltip" title="Garur lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 3 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 1 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>               <tr><td>Money owed by </td><td>78 Gold 3 Copper</td></tr>      </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born on a wagon, and was raised by my adoptive family as an only child. I had a poor upbringing in a small house. I didn't know my parents growing up. Others saw me as different, or strange, and so I had few companions.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a gambler</summary> <div class="descriptive">"  I'm working as a gambler. The work is alright, if a little dull   <b>Survival</b>. Everything I do is to ensure I will see another sunrise."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I came across a trinket in a field- It's a Waterborne Miner's Pick of Healing.<blockquote><h4>Waterborne Miner's Pick of Healing</h4>The item floats on water or other liquids. Its bearer has advantage on Strength (Athletics) checks to swim. This item contains 4 weak healing nodes. As an action, a character can use one node to heal 1d4 hit points at touch range. The item regains 1d4 charges at sunrise.</blockquote> At one point for a while I did some work as a peasant. One time I met the love of my life, who is no longer with me. You might not believe it, but because of a promise, I did some time as a peasant. I used to play cards in a pub, and one time supposedly cheated a <a data-id="1bb093cb-bfae-4b8d-afe3-76a043151374" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 1bb093cb-bfae-4b8d-afe3-76a043151374" title="A dwarf with a goatee called Einkil Ironfist who is a peasant." href="#1bb093cb-bfae-4b8d-afe3-76a043151374">man</a> out of his winnings; I suppose that I'm at least partially to blame. I couldn't care less if he tries to do anything about it.Oh, and I can't forget the time I met a <a data-id="83323e6e-03c7-45b3-a11b-1113ac367f8d" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 83323e6e-03c7-45b3-a11b-1113ac367f8d" title="A rather squat dwarven man called Erias Glanhig who is a peasant." href="#83323e6e-03c7-45b3-a11b-1113ac367f8d">man</a>, and we played cards. He decided that I was cheating- it was all a setup, but a very good one. I hope to apologise to him if I ever encounter him again. I once found a cursed book. The book forced you to see the dead.One time, I was part of a real curse. My friends and I once came upon a snake who was trapped beneath a rock and we helped it out. The snake spoke to us and said a miracle would befall us soon, but nobody believed them. Within a few weeks, everyone in town had gotten terribly ill.Not to mention there was the time I met up with an adventurer who generously gave me a Inaccurate Waterskin of Shade.<blockquote><h4>Inaccurate Waterskin of Shade</h4>The bearer gains a +1 bonus to Charisma (Deception) checks. The bearer suffers no harm in temperatures as high as 120 degrees Fahrenheit.</blockquote> At one point, I was caught and convicted of murder, and spent 4 years in jail before managing to escape.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr>       <th>Name</th>       <th>Race</th>       <th>Occupation</th> <h2>Resh Rangakk</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ɹɛʃ ɹæŋɡʌk /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="156f232b-b2cc-4238-8e75-1cc65ec4d273">          <span class="first-character">R</span>esh Rangakk    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="aff72812-c390-4528-a585-82c32b47b6d9" id="aff72812-c390-4528-a585-82c32b47b6d9" role="tooltip" title="51 years old, to be exact.">an old</span> male half-orc.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="e5585174-5f34-40d7-a340-62c47be0230f" id="e5585174-5f34-40d7-a340-62c47be0230f" role="tooltip" title="5ft. 9″">medium sized</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="955d852b-e182-47e7-94fd-f2c568a48ed0" id="955d852b-e182-47e7-94fd-f2c568a48ed0" role="tooltip" title="165lbs. (with a BMI of 20)">thin</span>, and has yellow eyes    with pale skin.    The most notable physical trait of Resh is that he has a narrow, sunken chin. </p> <p>   Resh exaggerates details.            He is perky, merciless, and fearless.     When he is relaxed, he is confident.  In moments of stress, he becomes pushy.  Religion-wise, Resh is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="627d398b-a1a0-45ce-8380-4c057e3bb33e" id="627d398b-a1a0-45ce-8380-4c057e3bb33e" role="tooltip" title="Resh Rangakk is a quiet follower of undefined, and is not shy about criticizing followers of other gods.">a quiet true believer</span>.  <p>          Despite sexism against him,         Resh has been having mild success as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="cde676c4-2daf-4a99-abea-de8eacfd85c9" id="cde676c4-2daf-4a99-abea-de8eacfd85c9" role="tooltip" title="Bets money on sports, card games, or games of chance in the hope of a profit.">gambler</span>, with a background of being a hermit.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="7fc9f8b4-9043-4d38-a2db-80971c05f1cd" id="7fc9f8b4-9043-4d38-a2db-80971c05f1cd" role="tooltip" title="Resh lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">peasantry</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Resh currently has a potion of Polymorph Self worth 350gp in his pockets,    and 50 Gold 7 Silver 1 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716" title="Main Street is a path-sized gravel and hewn rock street. Resh has a wife, <a data-id="ab935dc2-ca60-40af-a67a-b3a5ac34daa1" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal ab935dc2-ca60-40af-a67a-b3a5ac34daa1" title="A tan skinned somewhat short half-orc called Greeba Dargakk who is a peasant." href="#ab935dc2-ca60-40af-a67a-b3a5ac34daa1">Greeba Dargakk</a>.    </p> <section>Resh currently earns 1 Gold 2 Silver 2 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 3 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 8.5 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="ad98f057-92e7-4ff9-9e5b-3c7331b60b7e" id="ad98f057-92e7-4ff9-9e5b-3c7331b60b7e" role="tooltip" title="Resh lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 3 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 1 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>               <tr><td>Money owed by <a data-id="22369fb4-68a3-494b-85ea-7d3ed282214e" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 22369fb4-68a3-494b-85ea-7d3ed282214e" title="A fair skinned built like a brick shithouse dwarf called Eridred Durthane who is a professor." href="#22369fb4-68a3-494b-85ea-7d3ed282214e">Eridred Durthane</a></td><td>546 Gold 2 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>      </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by my adoptive family as an only child. Others saw me as different, or strange, and so I had few companions.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a gambler</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I never liked the people that I grew up with, so it was easy for me to leave it all behind and strike out a new life, alone. <h2>Eridred Durthane</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ɹʌdɹʌd dɝθeɪn /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="22369fb4-68a3-494b-85ea-7d3ed282214e">          <span class="first-character">E</span>ridred Durthane    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="68263b4d-4d30-4cd6-9fe2-82acae2cca3d" id="68263b4d-4d30-4cd6-9fe2-82acae2cca3d" role="tooltip" title="37 years old, to be exact.">a mid thirties</span> female dwarf.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="d4dfc702-b19f-472a-9e9e-6fdacdb00a7c" id="d4dfc702-b19f-472a-9e9e-6fdacdb00a7c" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 1″">rather squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="221a5e12-7101-40ad-aa48-1042fc36c010" id="221a5e12-7101-40ad-aa48-1042fc36c010" role="tooltip" title="186lbs. (with a BMI of 38)">built like a brick shithouse</span>, and has green eyes    with fair skin.    The most notable physical trait of Eridred is that she has a weak chin. </p> <p>   Eridred loses train of thought easily.            She is chaste.     When she is relaxed, she is devout.  In moments of stress, she becomes angry.  Religion-wise, Eridred is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="e0c15c67-ad49-4d7f-a690-7806ed5b2207" id="e0c15c67-ad49-4d7f-a690-7806ed5b2207" role="tooltip" title="Eridred Durthane is usually a quiet follower of Dionysus, but can be quite rude to anyone who criticizes her choice of deity.">a casual observer</span> of <a data-id="dionysus" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal dionysus" title="Dionysus is the god of Wine and Theatre, his revelry is open to all. However, he has his dark side - he is the god of madness the anger of Dionysus is a terrifying thing" href="#dionysus">Dionysus</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against her,         Eridred is currently having mild success as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="601386c8-60b5-49e9-aae9-3673110fb8b5" id="601386c8-60b5-49e9-aae9-3673110fb8b5" role="tooltip" title="A teacher of the highest rank in a college or university.">professor</span>, with a background of being an acolyte.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="c1204df3-8f5f-48dd-a805-e2384a4b9335" id="c1204df3-8f5f-48dd-a805-e2384a4b9335" role="tooltip" title="Eridred lives a comfortable life, filled with good food and wine">nobility</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Eridred currently has hardtack in her pockets,    and 100 Gold 7 Silver 3 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="c3492b51-086e-4701-85ad-9c543b873d49" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal c3492b51-086e-4701-85ad-9c543b873d49" title="Pope Street is a rather wide gravel and hewn rock street. It is a loose gravel that was taken from a river bed. There's a wagon with a cracked wheel by the side of the road. " href="#c3492b51-086e-4701-85ad-9c543b873d49">Pope Street</a>.               Eridred knows Common and Dwarvish.           </p> <section>Eridred currently earns 3 Gold per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>3 Gold 5 Silver 7 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 6 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>3 Gold</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="916df82d-e677-43b4-b5f6-22bb5b7d6275" id="916df82d-e677-43b4-b5f6-22bb5b7d6275" role="tooltip" title="Eridred lives a comfortable life, filled with good food and wine">comfortable</span>)</td><td>3 Gold 7 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 7 Copper</td></tr>          <tr><td>Money owed to <a data-id="156f232b-b2cc-4238-8e75-1cc65ec4d273" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 156f232b-b2cc-4238-8e75-1cc65ec4d273" title="A pale skinned thin half-orc called Resh Rangakk who is a gambler." href="#156f232b-b2cc-4238-8e75-1cc65ec4d273">Resh Rangakk</a></td><td>546 Gold 2 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by my single mother, along with my 3 siblings. <h2>Beloril Bofdarm</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /bʌlɝɪl boʊfdɑɹm /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="b7260a92-78ce-42a5-8eb0-856cd9bf4b17">          <span class="first-character">B</span>eloril Bofdarm    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="2dd6846e-3d1f-4d55-a5a3-ef5cbc619d30" id="2dd6846e-3d1f-4d55-a5a3-ef5cbc619d30" role="tooltip" title="39 years old, to be exact.">an adult</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="28fa6051-4b28-4552-9944-056bfddd7107" id="28fa6051-4b28-4552-9944-056bfddd7107" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 3″">quite squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="8c7d5cd3-c613-4a9c-a450-17a66be49137" id="8c7d5cd3-c613-4a9c-a450-17a66be49137" role="tooltip" title="192lbs. (with a BMI of 36)">built like a wrestler</span>, and has blue eyes        and a goatee,    with white skin.    The most notable physical trait of Beloril is that he has pale, veiny legs. </p> <p>   Beloril sweats profusely and easily.            He is slow to believe in people and craven.     When he is relaxed, he is fearful.  In moments of stress, he becomes scornful.  Religion-wise, Beloril is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="b4f56453-f472-4114-8da1-02327ba0feb7" id="b4f56453-f472-4114-8da1-02327ba0feb7" role="tooltip" title="Beloril is a faithful follower of Zeus, and enjoys confronting others to challenge beliefs that differ from his own.">an outspoken believer</span> of <a data-id="zeus" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal zeus" title="Zeus is the leader of the Greek gods, and lives atop Mount Olympus, where he rules over the mortal world below." href="#zeus">Zeus</a>.  <p>          Perhaps due to sexism,       Beloril has recently been somewhat unsuccessful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="9838675e-ee65-4bf2-80f2-876d7777d189" id="9838675e-ee65-4bf2-80f2-876d7777d189" role="tooltip" title="Steals peoples property, especially by stealth and without using force or violence.">thief</span>, with a background of being a hermit.         He belongs to the paupery social class, but lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though.    </p> <p>   Beloril currently has 22 cp in his pockets,    and 90 Gold 6 Silver 8 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="3c56a361-832d-46b4-aad3-913924724c43" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 3c56a361-832d-46b4-aad3-913924724c43" title="Smith Trail is a path-sized gravel and rock trail. It is a loose gravel that was taken from a river bed. There's a laundry line connecting two houses that are slightly closer together than usual. <h2>Veit Caebrek</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /vit keɪɛbɹɛk /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="bef3d270-7525-4e0f-9bcb-9e9b6f053f31">          <span class="first-character">V</span>eit Caebrek    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="961af9d0-6b0c-41af-a6ff-5f79b9369c74" id="961af9d0-6b0c-41af-a6ff-5f79b9369c74" role="tooltip" title="155 years old, to be exact.">an aged</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="4fe9c45a-aa9a-4289-bf18-fbb24c17d2d7" id="4fe9c45a-aa9a-4289-bf18-fbb24c17d2d7" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 3″">quite squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="64a8ffe0-a185-44bd-b2db-0ab73506e5e8" id="64a8ffe0-a185-44bd-b2db-0ab73506e5e8" role="tooltip" title="186lbs. (with a BMI of 35)">built like a wrestler</span>, and has brown eyes        and a dreadful beard,    with tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Veit is that he has child-sized hands. </p> <p>   Veit is skeptical of everything.            He is fainthearted, but is pitying, merciful.     When he is relaxed, he is compassionate.  In moments of stress, he becomes fanatical.  Religion-wise, Veit is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="94ae904a-6091-4102-b409-5b37bf15b940" id="94ae904a-6091-4102-b409-5b37bf15b940" role="tooltip" title="Veit Caebrek is a casual follower of Hades, and he likes to provoke heated 'debates' with people who follow other religions.">a casual observer</span> of <a data-id="hades" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal hades" title="Hades is the god of the Dead and the first son of Kronos. However when He, Zeus and Poseidon were drawing lots for the division of the cosmos, Hades gained dominion of the Underworld, where he rules over the dead." href="#hades">Hades</a>.  <p>      Veit is a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="2aa2f382-0ed4-4d00-aef3-9e62cf91e34c" id="2aa2f382-0ed4-4d00-aef3-9e62cf91e34c" role="tooltip" title="A pickpocket or thief.">cutpurse</span>, with a background of being an acolyte.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="9de24a29-2ad8-4456-9a3c-20be896c760c" id="9de24a29-2ad8-4456-9a3c-20be896c760c" role="tooltip" title="Veit lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">peasantry</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Veit currently has a deed to a ruined tower in his pockets,    and 80 Gold 7 Silver to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="3c56a361-832d-46b4-aad3-913924724c43" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 3c56a361-832d-46b4-aad3-913924724c43" title="Smith Trail is a path-sized gravel and rock trail. It is a loose gravel that was taken from a river bed. There's a laundry line connecting two houses that are slightly closer together than usual. " href="#3c56a361-832d-46b4-aad3-913924724c43">Smith Trail</a>.               Veit knows Common and Dwarvish.           </p> <section>Veit currently earns  9 Silver 3 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 8.5 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td> 9 Silver 3 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="fa97a21c-33c1-4a5f-a7f6-d9f02f287b10" id="fa97a21c-33c1-4a5f-a7f6-d9f02f287b10" role="tooltip" title="Veit lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">poor</span>)</td><td> 3 Silver</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td> 6 Silver 3 Copper</td></tr>               <tr><td>Money owed by <a data-id="db6e2980-9267-4a78-9445-ec70589b1a87" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal db6e2980-9267-4a78-9445-ec70589b1a87" title="A very tall man with very rounded ears called Antonyr Underwood who is an alchemist." href="#db6e2980-9267-4a78-9445-ec70589b1a87">Antonyr Underwood</a></td><td>280 Gold 9 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>      </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by my extended family as an only child. I had a comfortable upbringing in no real permanent address.  I had a few close friends, and my childhood was a relatively normal one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a cutpurse</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I ran away from home at a young age, and found refuge in a temple. I'm working as a cutpurse. The work is alright, though it can be a bit tedious I will someday get revenge on the corrupt temple hierarchy who branded me a heretic. I believe that the ancient traditions of worship and sacrifice must be preserved and upheld."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I did a stint as a cutpurse. You might not believe it, but there was a pretty nasty zombie outbreak which I had to defend my town against. I acquitted myself well in battle, and was awarded a medal for bravery. I'll always remember the time I met the love of my life, who is no longer with me. I went on a journey to find an ever-burning flame on the back of a giant turtle. I really did make it there, but I don't like to brag about it.One time I learned under the tutelage of <a data-id="a869a677-570a-4a79-a6bc-2892b40a80b2" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal a869a677-570a-4a79-a6bc-2892b40a80b2" title="A quite squat female dwarf called Barbena Silverstone who is a painter." href="#a869a677-570a-4a79-a6bc-2892b40a80b2">Barbena Silverstone</a> a fallen painter. During that time I learned a lot about myself. I'll always remember the time I got to attend the royal feast of a local <a data-id="e90950b8-905b-4f21-94c8-32785a14fec9" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal e90950b8-905b-4f21-94c8-32785a14fec9" title="A dwarf with a long, luxurious beard called Thoradin Glanhig who is a peasant." href="#e90950b8-905b-4f21-94c8-32785a14fec9">noble</a> in celebration of a bountiful summer harvest. I forget exactly when, but at one point, I shook the hand of a passing <a data-id="6f842ac4-ba7c-46d6-8720-063877d71dd6" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 6f842ac4-ba7c-46d6-8720-063877d71dd6" title="A dwarf with a dreadful beard called Fargrim Orcfoe who is a peasant." href="#6f842ac4-ba7c-46d6-8720-063877d71dd6">noble</a>. If I recall their handshake was nothing special. You might not believe it, but I was caught and convicted of theft, and spent 3 years doing hard labour before managing to escape. How could I ever forget the time I found my lost family heirloom, it is a Etherbound Chime of Shifting.<blockquote><h4>Etherbound Chime of Shifting</h4>The bearer can see creatures in the Border Ethereal that overlap with their plane as clearly as if they were fully in the bearer's plane. Such creatures appear as apparitions or ghosts. The bearer may change minor aspects of the physical appearance of this item.</blockquote> I apprenticed under <a data-id="36214210-5179-43d3-91d0-5a73b407e1b9" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 36214210-5179-43d3-91d0-5a73b407e1b9" title="An earlyish thirties dwarf with a face covered in freckles called Anbera Fahack who is a tailor." href="#36214210-5179-43d3-91d0-5a73b407e1b9">Anbera Fahack</a> an up and coming tailor. During that time I realized being in that trade just wasn't for me. At one point, I went to find a sheep that had gone missing, and must have gotten lost- I ended up in a strange land, where the colours were not as they should have been. I eventually found my way back, but never found the missing sheep. It turned up, completely skeletised in my bed three days later.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr>       <th>Name</th>
