<h2>Antonyr Underwood</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /æntʌniɹ ʌndɝwʊd /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="db6e2980-9267-4a78-9445-ec70589b1a87">          <span class="first-character">A</span>ntonyr Underwood    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="9638a9a0-5392-4f82-95e2-2f83de767a42" id="9638a9a0-5392-4f82-95e2-2f83de767a42" role="tooltip" title="25 years old, to be exact.">a prime adult aged</span> male human.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="1429b36a-34ff-46b1-89e7-195d41a57691" id="1429b36a-34ff-46b1-89e7-195d41a57691" role="tooltip" title="6ft. 4″">very tall</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="d8db1ce6-e341-4821-a99e-1d8cdcdfd9d8" id="d8db1ce6-e341-4821-a99e-1d8cdcdfd9d8" role="tooltip" title="228lbs. (with a BMI of 27)">rather solidly built</span>, and has pale green eyes    with fair skin.    The most notable physical trait of Antonyr is that he has very rounded ears. </p> <p>   Antonyr chews with an open mouth.            He is imprudent, irresponsible, and trusting.     When he is relaxed, he is loyal.  In moments of stress, he becomes destructive.  Religion-wise, Antonyr is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="da0a982a-e939-4e40-bcfa-66c769cc2dbe" id="da0a982a-e939-4e40-bcfa-66c769cc2dbe" role="tooltip" title="Antonyr Underwood is critical of religion, but is nominally a follower of Hades. Because of his doubts, he enjoys spirited debates about the flaws of various religions – both other peoples' faiths and his own.">a cautious listener</span> of <a data-id="hades" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal hades" title="Hades is the god of the Dead and the first son of Kronos. However when He, Zeus and Poseidon were drawing lots for the division of the cosmos, Hades gained dominion of the Underworld, where he rules over the dead." href="#hades">Hades</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against him,         Antonyr has recently had mild success as an <span class="tip dotted" data-id="58525376-b8c4-4c95-bccb-81bc1507652f" id="58525376-b8c4-4c95-bccb-81bc1507652f" role="tooltip" title="Transforms or creates something within nature through the magical and scientific manipulation of chemicals.">alchemist</span>, with a background of being a guild artisan.         He belongs to the commoner social class, but lives large, with little care to how much money is spent, splashing out on expensive things on a whim.    </p> <p>   Antonyr currently has 6 cp in his pockets,    and  7 Silver 4 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="ebd5996d-85e2-420b-b1a8-1cb1ad0f6b08" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal ebd5996d-85e2-420b-b1a8-1cb1ad0f6b08" title="Common Crescent is a  gravel and hewn rock road. It is made of colourful rocks and pebbles. A row of houses and buildings is splayed out, with enough room for a horse and cart to turn around. " href="#ebd5996d-85e2-420b-b1a8-1cb1ad0f6b08">Common Crescent</a>.                       Antonyr has a wife, <a data-id="5b87ccc8-9b33-4711-b708-91c13e13ffd7" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 5b87ccc8-9b33-4711-b708-91c13e13ffd7" title="A lean female tiefling called Uzza Meluzan who is a veterinarian." href="#5b87ccc8-9b33-4711-b708-91c13e13ffd7">Uzza Meluzan</a>.    </p> <section>Antonyr currently earns 13 Gold 6 Silver 2 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>15 Gold 3 Silver</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>13 Gold 6 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="173ffe56-f7b5-4f9c-8b4d-a9ab579e471c" id="173ffe56-f7b5-4f9c-8b4d-a9ab579e471c" role="tooltip" title="Antonyr lives large, with little care to how much money is spent, splashing out on expensive things on a whim">aristocratic</span>)</td><td>16 Gold 1 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>-2 Gold 5 Silver</td></tr>          <tr><td>Money owed to <a data-id="b7260a92-78ce-42a5-8eb0-856cd9bf4b17" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal b7260a92-78ce-42a5-8eb0-856cd9bf4b17" title="A built like a wrestler male dwarf called Beloril Bofdarm who is a thief." href="#b7260a92-78ce-42a5-8eb0-856cd9bf4b17">Beloril Bofdarm</a></td><td>93 Gold 6 Silver 4 Copper</td></tr>          <tr><td>Money owed to <a data-id="bef3d270-7525-4e0f-9bcb-9e9b6f053f31" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal bef3d270-7525-4e0f-9bcb-9e9b6f053f31" title="A quite squat dwarven man called Veit Caebrek who is a cutpurse." href="#bef3d270-7525-4e0f-9bcb-9e9b6f053f31">Veit Caebrek</a></td><td>280 Gold 9 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born in a tavern, and was raised by my mother and father as an only child. I had a comfortable upbringing in a rundown shack.  I had several friends, and my childhood was generally a happy one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming an alchemist</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I wanted to get away from my home situation and start a new life, so I learned a trade in secret and ran away one night. My talents were given to me so that I could use them to benefit the world."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I met the love of my life, [object Object]. <h2>Kilia Caebrek</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /kɪliʌ keɪɛbɹɛk /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="2754c122-1ad8-41db-b303-1030e5837db2">          <span class="first-character">K</span>ilia Caebrek    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="2ce5e462-4d3b-4d2b-bcc4-52ba3024f775" id="2ce5e462-4d3b-4d2b-bcc4-52ba3024f775" role="tooltip" title="158 years old, to be exact.">an aged</span> female dwarf.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="be669be2-559e-4b4c-88a9-5b26aacbab94" id="be669be2-559e-4b4c-88a9-5b26aacbab94" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 1″">rather squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="8dafc96d-088c-4dc0-bb00-573504320976" id="8dafc96d-088c-4dc0-bb00-573504320976" role="tooltip" title="162lbs. (with a BMI of 33)">rather round</span>, and has green eyes    with pale skin.    The most notable physical trait of Kilia is that she has long, thick earlobes. </p> <p>   Kilia cannot stop staring at you.            She is torpid and vigilant.     When she is relaxed, she is strict.  In moments of stress, she becomes gluttonous.  Religion-wise, Kilia is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="6d25efd0-683f-43e9-b261-185432092e30" id="6d25efd0-683f-43e9-b261-185432092e30" role="tooltip" title="Kilia Caebrek is critical of religion, but is nominally a follower of Artemis. Despite her supposed faith, she enjoys ragging on any and all religions, and will openly criticize any faithful people she meets.">a critical student</span> of <a data-id="artemis" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal artemis" title="Artemis is the goddess of the Hunt and young girls. She can change others into animals as punishment for transgressions against her and she demands appropriate respect from mortals." href="#artemis">Artemis</a>.  <p>      Kilia is a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="9f11ddd0-65f8-46e1-9d69-54099ebcf99c" id="9f11ddd0-65f8-46e1-9d69-54099ebcf99c" role="tooltip" title="Makes all sorts of baked goods.">baker</span>, with a background of being a peasant.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="ca4dd6b9-d40c-47ec-b024-c59799aa989a" id="ca4dd6b9-d40c-47ec-b024-c59799aa989a" role="tooltip" title="Kilia lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">peasantry</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Kilia currently has a list of people in a nearby city in her pockets,    and 390 Gold 1 Silver 8 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="d228384c-7090-4096-9e5d-cc40b0ca71dc" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal d228384c-7090-4096-9e5d-cc40b0ca71dc" title="Baker Road is a path-sized gravel and hewn rock road. It is made of poorly packed gravel, which shifts around under foot. The road has the occasional pothole. " href="#d228384c-7090-4096-9e5d-cc40b0ca71dc">Baker Road</a>.               Kilia knows Common and Dwarvish.           </p> <section>Kilia currently earns  7 Silver 5 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td> 8 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 8.5 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td> 7 Silver 5 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="93e35c7d-24e4-4448-a07c-fb85a92010ea" id="93e35c7d-24e4-4448-a07c-fb85a92010ea" role="tooltip" title="Kilia lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">poor</span>)</td><td> 2 Silver 8 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td> 4 Silver 7 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by my single mother, along with my 3 siblings. I had a modest upbringing in no real permanent address.  I had a few close friends, and my childhood was a relatively normal one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a baker</summary> <div class="descriptive">"  Watching yeast rise is meditative.   <b>Community</b>. With your friends, family, and neighbours, there's no winter too cold- together we'll be able pull through just about anything."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time for a time, I worked for a famous knight while on a long journey. I forget exactly when, but at one point, I was framed by a <a data-id="08f6a341-3149-43a8-bf89-eef3b3061fa6" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 08f6a341-3149-43a8-bf89-eef3b3061fa6" title="A young adult gnome with thin ruddy cheeks called Dabbledob Nopenstallen who is a peasant." href="#08f6a341-3149-43a8-bf89-eef3b3061fa6">scoundrel</a> for a crime I didn't commit- I admit that I am at least partially at fault. I doubt I'll ever meet him again. Oh, and I can't forget the time I worked as a baker. One time because of a promise, I did some time as a peasant. Not to mention there was the time I was tricked into attending the royal wedding of a local <a data-id="f59661e2-7fe5-45a9-85df-b716951d202e" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal f59661e2-7fe5-45a9-85df-b716951d202e" title="A dwarf with a long, well-kempt beard called Oskar Lutgehr who is a peasant." href="#f59661e2-7fe5-45a9-85df-b716951d202e">noble</a>.I apprenticed under <a data-id="61e41c5d-ae92-4499-8666-03e086c5b4b1" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 61e41c5d-ae92-4499-8666-03e086c5b4b1" title="A dwarf with a well-loved beard, with ornamental beads woven into it called Fargrim Loderr who is a weaponsmith." href="#61e41c5d-ae92-4499-8666-03e086c5b4b1">Fargrim Loderr</a> an adept weaponsmith. During that time my master beat their teachings into me.I'll always remember the time there was no other work so for a while I was a peasant. You might not believe it, but for a while I did some work as a baker.  At one point, My parents gave me a Shepherd's Ale Stine of Faith.<blockquote><h4>Shepherd's Ale Stine of Faith</h4>The bearer gains a +1 bonus to (Wisdom) Animal Handling checks. When the bearer of this item rolls hit dice, they can choose to re-roll them and take the second result.</blockquote></div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details <h2>Penelope West</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /pɛnɛloʊp wɛst /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="021b6917-229d-47dc-8295-b8f4cc6e3e3a">          <span class="first-character">P</span>enelope West    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="46922513-d68a-4dda-8c71-feb4fce75981" id="46922513-d68a-4dda-8c71-feb4fce75981" role="tooltip" title="24 years old, to be exact.">a youthful adult</span> female human.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="fbd8ae93-ec70-4c3f-b74c-4c1d4d77a7a7" id="fbd8ae93-ec70-4c3f-b74c-4c1d4d77a7a7" role="tooltip" title="5ft. 1″">barely five foot</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="5cb40a98-cefe-46f4-a96b-f93df8274d0c" id="5cb40a98-cefe-46f4-a96b-f93df8274d0c" role="tooltip" title="149lbs. (with a BMI of 28)">fat, but muscular</span>, and has hazel eyes    with light skin.    The most notable physical trait of Penelope is that she has a thin, sloped nose. </p> <p>   Penelope is skeptical of everything.        When she is relaxed, she is carefree.  In moments of stress, she becomes destructive.  Religion-wise, Penelope is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="23d00233-bb0e-4a03-b31b-54bfe21b4bcc" id="23d00233-bb0e-4a03-b31b-54bfe21b4bcc" role="tooltip" title="Penelope West is a casual follower of Hermes, and can be quite rude towards those who worship 'inferior' gods.">a cautious listener</span> of <a data-id="hermes" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal hermes" title="Hermes is the hessenger of the gods and the personal messenger of Zeus. He brings the souls of the deceased to the edge of the underworld, where they are ferried deeper by the Cthonic gods" href="#hermes">Hermes</a>.  <p>      Penelope is a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="37c13594-b843-4ae1-a04e-839ff6cab779" id="37c13594-b843-4ae1-a04e-839ff6cab779" role="tooltip" title="Owns or runs a shop.">shopkeep</span>, with a background of being an acolyte.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="fececadd-61fa-4f06-b17c-8e7ffe4a4537" id="fececadd-61fa-4f06-b17c-8e7ffe4a4537" role="tooltip" title="Penelope lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Penelope currently has a wooden comb in her pockets,    and  5 Silver 8 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="ed6d7af5-caa3-499d-a759-3d4b334f931f" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal ed6d7af5-caa3-499d-a759-3d4b334f931f" title="Thrahak Road is a rather wide gravel and hewn rock road. <h2>Eberk Daraln</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ɛbɝk dɑɹæln /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="06fc19ee-0c2c-4d84-8a45-4f94fa9e4663">          <span class="first-character">E</span>berk Daraln    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="f1ea9f8e-0787-4823-8a47-4d24a114cf23" id="f1ea9f8e-0787-4823-8a47-4d24a114cf23" role="tooltip" title="296 years old, to be exact.">an ancient</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="1f0f6395-4eec-416e-aa5c-72cf57f59011" id="1f0f6395-4eec-416e-aa5c-72cf57f59011" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 5″">somewhat squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="de31fb0d-d128-4c91-ba48-c13f37d92c46" id="de31fb0d-d128-4c91-ba48-c13f37d92c46" role="tooltip" title="214lbs. (with a BMI of 38)">unbelievably large</span>, and has gray eyes        and a rather wild, unkempt beard,    with pale skin.    The most notable physical trait of Eberk is that he has a recessed chin. </p> <p>   Eberk embellishes the truth.            He is indulgent.     When he is relaxed, he is weak-willed.  In moments of stress, he becomes withdrawn.  Religion-wise, Eberk is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="84f5ab1f-47d3-487f-8981-db866645db1f" id="84f5ab1f-47d3-487f-8981-db866645db1f" role="tooltip" title="Eberk Daraln is a casual follower of Poseidon, and can be quite rude towards those who worship 'inferior' gods.">a casual observer</span> of <a data-id="poseidon" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal poseidon" title="Poseidon is the god of the Sea - all things underwater are under his purview" href="#poseidon">Poseidon</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against him,         Eberk has been successful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="0e0a6e61-3070-4199-88f7-ec9d7856fa4a" id="0e0a6e61-3070-4199-88f7-ec9d7856fa4a" role="tooltip" title="Held in confinement as a punishment for crimes they have been convicted of.">prisoner</span>, with a background of being an urchin.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="37fcd18e-d454-4465-bcb4-2f177969ba43" id="37fcd18e-d454-4465-bcb4-2f177969ba43" role="tooltip" title="Eberk lives a wretched life of constant filth and misery. There is no respite to this poverty">paupery</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Eberk currently has an explosive rune, dealing 2d4 fire damage in his pockets,    and 300 Gold 7 Silver 1 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="02ff1684-74e8-47c3-b854-120a0fd8bde2" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 02ff1684-74e8-47c3-b854-120a0fd8bde2" title="Strongheart Crescent is a wide, multi-lane gravel and rock square. It is made of colourful rocks and pebbles. There's a wagon with a cracked wheel by the side of the road. It was named after Therlin Strongheart, who was a dwarf who brought riches to the people of Bugshaw." href="#02ff1684-74e8-47c3-b854-120a0fd8bde2">Strongheart Crescent</a>.               Eberk knows Common and Dwarvish.               He predominantly prefers the same gender, but finds other genders attractive            , and has a wife, <a data-id="7584c6fa-73a8-48fe-a7ef-2ca63d92e4da" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 7584c6fa-73a8-48fe-a7ef-2ca63d92e4da" title="A quite solidly built dwarven woman called Valida Goblinbane who is a tanner." href="#7584c6fa-73a8-48fe-a7ef-2ca63d92e4da">Valida Goblinbane</a>.           </p> <section>Eberk currently earns  2 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td> 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td> 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="34f38cd2-203e-402c-b126-ccbe1c7c5058" id="34f38cd2-203e-402c-b126-ccbe1c7c5058" role="tooltip" title="Eberk lives a wretched life of constant filth and misery. There is no respite to this poverty">wretched</span>)</td><td></td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td> 2 Copper</td></tr>               <tr><td>Money owed by <a data-id="15c70e01-539c-4186-92c0-4f0ef5ecf436" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 15c70e01-539c-4186-92c0-4f0ef5ecf436" title="An extremely obese female dwarf with a wide ribcage called Gillydd Gorunn who is a jailer." href="#15c70e01-539c-4186-92c0-4f0ef5ecf436">Gillydd Gorunn</a></td><td>14 Gold 4 Silver 7 Copper</td></tr>      </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born in a temple, and was raised by my mother and father as an only child. I had a squalid upbringing in a rundown shack.  I had a few close friends, and my childhood was a relatively normal one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a prisoner</summary> <div class="descriptive">"My parents died, leaving nobody to look after me, so I took care of myself. I'm doing really well as a prisoner! Maybe it's luck, maybe a natural talent, I don't know. I owe my survival to another urchin who taught me to live on the streets. The low are lifted up, and we all benefit from that."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I was caught and convicted of racketeering, and spent 1 years chained to an oar before being released. After that, to pay off a debt, I spent some time as a urchin.One time for a while I did some work as a urchin. I'll always remember the time I was caught and convicted of murder, and spent 2 years doing hard labour before being released. I did a stint as a urchin.At one point for a time, I worked for a famous armorer while on a long journey. <h2>Gillydd Gorunn</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ɡɪlid ɡɔɹʌn /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="15c70e01-539c-4186-92c0-4f0ef5ecf436">          <span class="first-character">G</span>illydd Gorunn    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="67c8cf1e-dd09-4a33-b988-152d2ea54609" id="67c8cf1e-dd09-4a33-b988-152d2ea54609" role="tooltip" title="102 years old, to be exact.">a middle aged</span> female dwarf.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="13a4c4d2-e804-4f25-ab44-d83fc12368f3" id="13a4c4d2-e804-4f25-ab44-d83fc12368f3" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 2″">rather squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="eb00a9fa-8f05-4935-be8d-accada48e141" id="eb00a9fa-8f05-4935-be8d-accada48e141" role="tooltip" title="176lbs. (with a BMI of 35)">extremely obese</span>, and has dark brown eyes    with white skin.    The most notable physical trait of Gillydd is that she has a wide ribcage. </p> <p>   Gillydd is always shaking.            She is subjective, cruel, and brash.     When she is relaxed, she is quiet.  In moments of stress, she becomes destructive.  Religion-wise, Gillydd is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="809a3a09-b2e3-400d-ba9f-a416321f9f1e" id="809a3a09-b2e3-400d-ba9f-a416321f9f1e" role="tooltip" title="Gillydd Gorunn is a casual follower of Poseidon, and she likes to provoke heated 'debates' with people who follow other religions.">a cautious listener</span> of <a data-id="poseidon" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal poseidon" title="Poseidon is the god of the Sea - all things underwater are under his purview" href="#poseidon">Poseidon</a>.  <p>          Perhaps due to sexism,       Gillydd is a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="9ceb617b-356d-45fe-9866-2cede0c64f6b" id="9ceb617b-356d-45fe-9866-2cede0c64f6b" role="tooltip" title="Supervises a jail and the prisoners in it.">jailer</span>, with a background of being a charlatan.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="75c98612-2491-4d25-831f-7206ca8a6992" id="75c98612-2491-4d25-831f-7206ca8a6992" role="tooltip" title="Gillydd lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">peasantry</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Gillydd currently has map of the local area in her pockets,    and 60 Gold 8 Silver 1 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716" title="Main Street is a path-sized gravel and hewn rock street. It is a loose gravel that was taken from a river bed. There are rows of potted plants and herbs, the produce of which people are free to pick at their leisure. " href="#2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716">Main Street</a>.               Gillydd knows Common and Dwarvish.               She predominantly prefers the same gender, but finds other genders attractive           </p> <section>Gillydd currently earns 1 Gold 2 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 1 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 8.5 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="0698bf3f-28c1-4698-9e8b-1d5ad2385f78" id="0698bf3f-28c1-4698-9e8b-1d5ad2385f78" role="tooltip" title="Gillydd lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 2 Silver 8 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 2 Silver 6 Copper</td></tr>          <tr><td>Money owed to <a data-id="06fc19ee-0c2c-4d84-8a45-4f94fa9e4663" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 06fc19ee-0c2c-4d84-8a45-4f94fa9e4663" title="An unbelievably large dwarven man called Eberk Daraln who is a prisoner." href="#06fc19ee-0c2c-4d84-8a45-4f94fa9e4663">Eberk Daraln</a></td><td>14 Gold 4 Silver 7 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born in a street, and was raised by my single father with my brother. I had a modest upbringing in a rundown shack.  Others saw me as different, or strange, and so I had few companions.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a jailer</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I took up cheating as a hobby, then was sort of adopted by a local scam artist. It just sort of became a way of life for me. I know that jailing is not a pretty profession, but somebody has to do it- might as well be me, right? A powerful person, Lord Zachar, killed someone I love. Some day soon, I'll have my revenge. I distribute the money I acquire to the people who really need it."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I worked as a charlatan. Once I met the love of my life, who is no longer with me. I once saw a true curse. A man stumbled into town claiming to be sent from a god and told us we were being blessed, but nobody believed them. That night, monsters descended upon our town.At one point undefinedI met the love of my life, who is no longer with me. At one point I had a mishap with a mind control spell- someone I thought of as family tried to steal my fortune, but their spell failed. At one point I apprenticed under <a data-id="14309827-fdc6-423d-9936-6ef2e71044db" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 14309827-fdc6-423d-9936-6ef2e71044db" title="An old man with long, monkey like toes called Adrik Balderk who is a leatherworker." href="#14309827-fdc6-423d-9936-6ef2e71044db">Adrik Balderk</a> a famous leatherworker. During that time my master was gentle with their teachings.  At one point, after taking command of a dangerous situation I was awarded a <span class="dotted">     <span class="tip dotted" data-id="9a0809f8-8464-4585-b38d-562b81179a64" id="9a0809f8-8464-4585-b38d-562b81179a64" role="tooltip" title="This medal's emblem is made of gold and has a braided hemp ribbon. The emblem is a pair of wings and the ribbon is coloured black.">medal</span> </span> for patriotism.I keep it above my fireplace to show my guests.</div></details>  <div class="classTable"> <h2>Alvyn Gimlen</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ælvɪn dʒɪmlʌn /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="c8dbb261-15fc-46bc-9799-2a1e7a13b81f">          <span class="first-character">A</span>lvyn Gimlen    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="03565341-56a8-4cee-8117-1db4d576eac4" id="03565341-56a8-4cee-8117-1db4d576eac4" role="tooltip" title="30 years old, to be exact.">a prime adult aged</span> male gnome.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="67f3d4af-0a09-450b-8c2e-6966def977d9" id="67f3d4af-0a09-450b-8c2e-6966def977d9" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 5″">somewhat squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="ab906ab2-3669-4241-9912-4da3e4d6b311" id="ab906ab2-3669-4241-9912-4da3e4d6b311" role="tooltip" title="52lbs. (with a BMI of 13)">bony yet muscular</span>, and has pale blue eyes        and a smattering of hairs on his face,    with light tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Alvyn is that he has colorfully painted nails. </p> <p>   Alvyn blinks constantly.            He is often lustful and brash.     When he is relaxed, he is artistic.  In moments of stress, he becomes compulsive.  Religion-wise, Alvyn is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="43c154f4-52fc-4cd1-afbb-258da5169d34" id="43c154f4-52fc-4cd1-afbb-258da5169d34" role="tooltip" title="Alvyn Gimlen is usually a quiet follower of Artemis, but can be quite rude to anyone who criticizes his choice of deity.">a casual observer</span> of <a data-id="artemis" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal artemis" title="Artemis is the goddess of the Hunt and young girls. She can change others into animals as punishment for transgressions against her and she demands appropriate respect from mortals." href="#artemis">Artemis</a>.  <p>      Alvyn has recently been somewhat unsuccessful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="319225e0-5961-4d83-b5e1-0b67f2091a22" id="319225e0-5961-4d83-b5e1-0b67f2091a22" role="tooltip" title="Trims and shoes horse's hooves.">farrier</span>, with a background of being a criminal.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="b47642af-9a8a-41d7-9da3-6b1ec79116af" id="b47642af-9a8a-41d7-9da3-6b1ec79116af" role="tooltip" title="Alvyn lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">peasantry</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Alvyn currently has hardtack in his pockets,    and  3 Silver 4 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="c8e768e0-44a0-4ad3-a239-76129978fb0f" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal c8e768e0-44a0-4ad3-a239-76129978fb0f" title="Wells Row is a narrow gravel and hewn rock road. It is made of noisy and shifting gravel. Better watch your footing. A crude drawing of an animal carved into a brick wall, affectionately labeled “R.G. Was here.” The name comes from Aelina Wells, a human who cared for orphans." href="#c8e768e0-44a0-4ad3-a239-76129978fb0f">Wells Row</a>.               Alvyn knows Common and Gnomish.           </p> <section>Alvyn currently earns  6 Silver 5 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td> 7 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 8.5 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td> 6 Silver 5 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="db351b45-f86c-4cdd-81d7-b4c4f569f9ea" id="db351b45-f86c-4cdd-81d7-b4c4f569f9ea" role="tooltip" title="Alvyn lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">poor</span>)</td><td> 2 Silver 7 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td> 3 Silver 8 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by my single father, along with my 2 siblings. I had a squalid upbringing in an encampment.  I had several friends, and my childhood was generally a happy one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a farrier</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I left home at a relatively young age, and found refuge in a thieves' guild. I've had a bit of a downturn as a farrier. If it keeps up for much longer, I'm going to begin losing hope. I'm trying to pay off an old debt I owe to a generous benefactor. I will do whatever it takes to become wealthy."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I went to celebrate at a winter festival. While I was there, I saw a sneaky con-artist fool a young couple. <h2>Camerus Layne</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /kæmɝʌs leɪn /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="746a115e-7d1a-40fd-9a45-c71fcbb5c6f7">          <span class="first-character">C</span>amerus Layne    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="e2ea1a48-949e-4fb3-83f0-8d1d785ead2b" id="e2ea1a48-949e-4fb3-83f0-8d1d785ead2b" role="tooltip" title="61 years old, to be exact.">a weathered</span> male human. ">tall</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="886aa3ca-2891-47d6-83e6-d6fb4a221542" id="886aa3ca-2891-47d6-83e6-d6fb4a221542" role="tooltip" title="162lbs. (with a BMI of 21)">wiry</span>, and has pale green eyes        and a bit of peach fuzz on his chin,    with fair skin.    The most notable physical trait of Camerus is that he has a sharply angled face. </p> <p>   Camerus bobs head back and forth when speaking.            He is subjective and cruel.     When he is relaxed, he is artistic.  In moments of stress, he becomes destructive.  Religion-wise, Camerus is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="5faef68a-3da1-4b19-8fac-c7be44d0e495" id="5faef68a-3da1-4b19-8fac-c7be44d0e495" role="tooltip" title="Camerus Layne is a casual follower of Aphrodite, and he likes to provoke heated 'debates' with people who follow other religions.">a cautious listener</span> of <a data-id="aphrodite" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal aphrodite" title="Aphrodite is the goddess of love and scorns those who stay away from relationships. <h2>Erias Glanhig</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ɛɹiʌz ɡlænhɪɡ /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="7d41db16-4498-4801-838c-13487fc87011">          <span class="first-character">E</span>rias Glanhig    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="c38ceba7-a4c1-41dc-88f8-24cb5e90b5e3" id="c38ceba7-a4c1-41dc-88f8-24cb5e90b5e3" role="tooltip" title="246 years old, to be exact.">an incredibly elderly</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="33efedd0-c3e0-48aa-84fb-3f616080c43d" id="33efedd0-c3e0-48aa-84fb-3f616080c43d" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 4″">quite squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="4a8047c2-212f-4d5e-9aec-77ed017f937e" id="4a8047c2-212f-4d5e-9aec-77ed017f937e" role="tooltip" title="171lbs. (with a BMI of 31)">obese</span>, and has yellow eyes        and a long, luxurious beard,    with light tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Erias is that he has fingers like sausages. </p> <p>   Erias drinks too much.         He makes all r-sounds become w-sounds.            He is bashful in the face of praise, but is very self centered, reckless.     When he is relaxed, he is cheerful.  In moments of stress, he becomes destructive.  Religion-wise, Erias is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="38c8523d-1728-4cb8-8824-69533aff071d" id="38c8523d-1728-4cb8-8824-69533aff071d" role="tooltip" title="Erias Glanhig is a casual follower of Aphrodite, and can be quite rude towards those who worship 'inferior' gods.">a cautious listener</span> of <a data-id="aphrodite" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal aphrodite" title="Aphrodite is the goddess of love and scorns those who stay away from relationships. Her love can be a thing of beauty or a thing of terror and destruction." href="#aphrodite">Aphrodite</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against him,         Erias is currently extremely successful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="5b2f4776-8129-400e-93a2-4ac94234503f" id="5b2f4776-8129-400e-93a2-4ac94234503f" role="tooltip" title="An expert in or student of the scientific study of plants.">botanist</span>, with a background of being a sage.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="57178d12-0d0d-43a4-b70c-d9c91a2b46ec" id="57178d12-0d0d-43a4-b70c-d9c91a2b46ec" role="tooltip" title="Erias lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Erias currently has a sling with 10 bullets in his pockets,    and 160 Gold 8 Silver 9 Copper to his name. " href="#b00b276d-6c1a-404e-8199-4c46fad1f650">Noble Plaza</a>.               Erias knows Common and Dwarvish.               He bisexual           </p> <section>Erias currently earns 1 Gold 3 Silver 6 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 5 Silver 3 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 6 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="cacd67f6-849b-44b1-bc31-3913b04dfe24" id="cacd67f6-849b-44b1-bc31-3913b04dfe24" role="tooltip" title="Erias lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 8 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 2 Copper</td></tr>          <tr><td>Money owed to <a data-id="746a115e-7d1a-40fd-9a45-c71fcbb5c6f7" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 746a115e-7d1a-40fd-9a45-c71fcbb5c6f7" title="A weathered human with a sharply angled face called Camerus Layne who is a prisoner." href="#746a115e-7d1a-40fd-9a45-c71fcbb5c6f7">Camerus Layne</a></td><td>351 Gold 1 Silver 4 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by my extended family as an only child. I believe that the path to power and self-improvement is through knowledge."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I got an autograph from a famous priest on the road. During that time I realized my teacher wasn't that great. Because of a promise, I did some time as a sage.I was a novice to <a data-id="a6024dac-90ea-4556-a74d-21c383dab7b0" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal a6024dac-90ea-4556-a74d-21c383dab7b0" title="A diminutive gnomish woman called Veloptima Sympony who is a silversmith." href="#a6024dac-90ea-4556-a74d-21c383dab7b0">Veloptima Sympony</a> a mediocre silversmith. During that time I realized I could never match my master.I learned under the tutelage of <a data-id="f0bc2fd3-8e03-419e-8799-892238747b41" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal f0bc2fd3-8e03-419e-8799-892238747b41" title="A bony male gnome with a narrow ribcage called Dimble Humplebumple who is a barber." href="#f0bc2fd3-8e03-419e-8799-892238747b41">Dimble Humplebumple</a> a mediocre barber. During that time I learned a lot about myself.I'll always remember the time I met the love of my life, who is no longer with me. At one point I was a novice to <a data-id="406019a4-8780-43b0-99b4-12ce7877980d" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 406019a4-8780-43b0-99b4-12ce7877980d" title="A prime adult aged man with a receding chin that makes their nose seem bigger called Nordak Balderk who is a candlemaker." href="#406019a4-8780-43b0-99b4-12ce7877980d">Nordak Balderk</a> a fallen candlemaker. During that time I realized what I truly wanted in life. At one point I used to play cards in a pub, and one time supposedly cheated a <a data-id="a75f0eff-27fb-4b50-bdb0-d5990625e7e5" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal a75f0eff-27fb-4b50-bdb0-d5990625e7e5" title="A gnome with a scraggly beard called Warryn Scheppen who is a peasant." href="#a75f0eff-27fb-4b50-bdb0-d5990625e7e5">man</a> out of his winnings; it was all a setup, but a very good one. I'll gut him like a fish if he crosses my path again. How could I ever forget the time to pay off a debt, I spent some time as a sage. After that, for a time, I worked for a famous poet in my travels.Once I used to play cards in a pub, and one time supposedly cheated a <a data-id="ef25fe7c-3535-47e6-8612-5fcae5f3fc28" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal ef25fe7c-3535-47e6-8612-5fcae5f3fc28" title="A rather tall man with a broad, flat nose called Peren Withrethin who is a peasant." href="#ef25fe7c-3535-47e6-8612-5fcae5f3fc28">man</a> out of his winnings; it was a misunderstanding, but I cannot convince him otherwise. I'm still on the lookout for him to this very day.  At one point, I worked under <a data-id="48a27107-2b7a-498c-afde-1e79202374ee" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 48a27107-2b7a-498c-afde-1e79202374ee" title="A built like a wrestler female dwarf with a mermaid tattoo called Hdeth Fire-Forge who is a cooper." href="#48a27107-2b7a-498c-afde-1e79202374ee">Hdeth Fire-Forge</a> a piss poor cooper. During that time my master beat their teachings into me.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr>       <th>Name</th> <h2>Eldon Murnig</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ɛldʌn mɝnɪɡ /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="2bddc27b-c0ce-478b-a046-44c3d87b0f33">          <span class="first-character">E</span>ldon Murnig    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="7cfc95ab-2fdd-4da1-a061-c4de41fd7f72" id="7cfc95ab-2fdd-4da1-a061-c4de41fd7f72" role="tooltip" title="137 years old, to be exact.">an old</span> male gnome.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="15f63b75-5e99-478e-9f72-8b22d09580e7" id="15f63b75-5e99-478e-9f72-8b22d09580e7" role="tooltip" title="3ft. 10″">rather small</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="1271236e-5249-42f6-95a9-6aad9714487c" id="1271236e-5249-42f6-95a9-6aad9714487c" role="tooltip" title="45lbs. (with a BMI of 14)">bony yet muscular</span>, and has brown eyes    with light tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Eldon is that he has a thin, hooked nose. </p> <p>   Eldon is incredibly gullible.            He is      When he is relaxed, he is agreeable.  In moments of stress, he becomes destructive.  Religion-wise, Eldon is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="336a0ddc-aa39-473d-a92a-3bded50a4833" id="336a0ddc-aa39-473d-a92a-3bded50a4833" role="tooltip" title="Eldon Murnig is a quiet follower of Zeus, and is not shy about criticizing followers of other gods.">a quiet true believer</span> of <a data-id="zeus" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal zeus" title="Zeus is the leader of the Greek gods, and lives atop Mount Olympus, where he rules over the mortal world below." href="#zeus">Zeus</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against him,         Eldon has recently been mildly successful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="75688973-8295-46d1-aded-1fed9aaf7c09" id="75688973-8295-46d1-aded-1fed9aaf7c09" role="tooltip" title="Bets money on sports, card games, or games of chance in the hope of a profit.">gambler</span>, with a background of being an outlander.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="e26c9800-04fd-40c5-88c6-f6c17d3ad300" id="e26c9800-04fd-40c5-88c6-f6c17d3ad300" role="tooltip" title="Eldon lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">peasantry</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Eldon currently has a scrap of paper with unintelligible writing on it in his pockets,    and 210 Gold 3 Silver 8 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403" title="Gunnloa Street is a narrow gravel and hewn rock street. It is made of poorly packed gravel, which shifts around under foot. Grated storm drains at regular intervals grant access to the sewer system. It has been named after Gunnloa Durthane, who was a much beloved prostitute, one of whose clients bought the road as a thankyou." href="#03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403">Gunnloa Street</a>.               Eldon knows Common and Gnomish.           </p> <section>Eldon currently earns 1 Gold 2 Silver 2 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 3 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 8.5 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="4c052197-c366-4ed9-a4d6-17eda80fb692" id="4c052197-c366-4ed9-a4d6-17eda80fb692" role="tooltip" title="Eldon lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 3 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 1 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>               <tr><td>Money owed by <a data-id="cbc8d617-6d8e-432d-9575-4fa5fb7940b4" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal cbc8d617-6d8e-432d-9575-4fa5fb7940b4" title="An adult man with no earlobes called Adrik Silveraxe who is a jeweller." href="#cbc8d617-6d8e-432d-9575-4fa5fb7940b4">Adrik Silveraxe</a></td><td>10 Gold 7 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>      </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born in the home of a midwife, and was raised by my single mother as an only child. I had a modest upbringing in a large house.  I had a few close friends, and my childhood was a relatively normal one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a gambler</summary> <div class="descriptive">"My people live on the edges of civilisation, and I learned the methods of survival from my family. I'm on the upswing as a gambler. Things are looking better. An injury to the unspoiled wilderness of my home is an injury to me. The natural world is more important than all the constructs of civilization."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I spent some time working as a gambler. There was a minor skirmish with some orcs that I was involved with. I suffered only minor injuries, and the wounds all healed without leaving any scars.One time to pay off a debt, I had to work as a outlander. Once a group of travelers and I went to find a tower of knowledge encircled by mountains. I got lost along the way and never made it there, but at least I tried. I forget exactly when, but at one point, I apprenticed under <a data-id="edce17d7-6792-43fb-9ec7-353c22d6e7bc" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal edce17d7-6792-43fb-9ec7-353c22d6e7bc" title="A fair skinned built like a wrestler dwarf called Darrak Brawnanvil who is a weaponsmith." href="#edce17d7-6792-43fb-9ec7-353c22d6e7bc">Darrak Brawnanvil</a> a legendary weaponsmith. During that time I learned a lot about myself. There was this one time, I went to a winter festival. While I was there, I partook in several festival traditions. I met up with an adventurer who generously gave me a Trickster's Miner's Pick of Speed.<blockquote><h4>Trickster's Miner's Pick of Speed</h4>The bearer may cast Minor Illusion once per day. <h2>Sindri Daergel</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /sɪndɹi deɪɛɝɡʌl /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="e864ad41-c288-4870-a529-410591dbe65b">          <span class="first-character">S</span>indri Daergel    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="b426fa7e-c43d-4e6b-8967-1cd43bbc8423" id="b426fa7e-c43d-4e6b-8967-1cd43bbc8423" role="tooltip" title="24 years old, to be exact.">a young adult</span> male gnome.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="33d58a85-2585-4a08-8606-b8b15d0715fe" id="33d58a85-2585-4a08-8606-b8b15d0715fe" role="tooltip" title="4ft. ">somewhat tiny</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="3a68f8a8-55cb-477a-9f81-d09fc452f434" id="3a68f8a8-55cb-477a-9f81-d09fc452f434" role="tooltip" title="47lbs. (with a BMI of 14)">bony yet muscular</span>, and has purple eyes        and a neckbeard,    with fair skin.    The most notable physical trait of Sindri is that he has very rounded ears. </p> <p>   Sindri blinks constantly.         He has a severe underbite.            He is always doubting people, spineless, and bright and energetic.     When he is relaxed, he is driven.  In moments of stress, he becomes cowardly.  Religion-wise, Sindri is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="0f10834f-3d77-4511-8b48-89ac1b3176a2" id="0f10834f-3d77-4511-8b48-89ac1b3176a2" role="tooltip" title="Sindri Daergel is usually a quiet follower of Zeus, but can be quite rude to anyone who criticizes his choice of deity.">a casual observer</span> of <a data-id="zeus" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal zeus" title="Zeus is the leader of the Greek gods, and lives atop Mount Olympus, where he rules over the mortal world below." href="#zeus">Zeus</a>.  <p>      Sindri is a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="79557c97-f853-4df9-8ce3-61831ddbb914" id="79557c97-f853-4df9-8ce3-61831ddbb914" role="tooltip" title="Abducts people and holds them captive, typically to obtain a ransom.">kidnapper</span>, with a background of being a peasant.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="c8cfccda-85e9-4eda-84b8-7aa6632de627" id="c8cfccda-85e9-4eda-84b8-7aa6632de627" role="tooltip" title="Sindri lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">peasantry</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Sindri currently has 22 cp in his pockets,    and  6 Silver 6 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="c3492b51-086e-4701-85ad-9c543b873d49" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal c3492b51-086e-4701-85ad-9c543b873d49" title="Pope Street is a rather wide gravel and hewn rock street. It is a loose gravel that was taken from a river bed. There's a wagon with a cracked wheel by the side of the road. " href="#c3492b51-086e-4701-85ad-9c543b873d49">Pope Street</a>.               Sindri knows Common and Gnomish.               He primarily prefers other genders, but sometimes finds the same gender attractive           </p> <section>Sindri currently earns  7 Silver 5 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td> 8 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 8.5 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td> 7 Silver 5 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="c4d8dec1-f491-488b-bea1-aab632577245" id="c4d8dec1-f491-488b-bea1-aab632577245" role="tooltip" title="Sindri lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">poor</span>)</td><td> 2 Silver 8 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td> 4 Silver 7 Copper</td></tr>               <tr><td>Money owed by <a data-id="cbc8d617-6d8e-432d-9575-4fa5fb7940b4" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal cbc8d617-6d8e-432d-9575-4fa5fb7940b4" title="An adult man with no earlobes called Adrik Silveraxe who is a jeweller." href="#cbc8d617-6d8e-432d-9575-4fa5fb7940b4">Adrik Silveraxe</a></td><td>42 Gold 8 Silver 8 Copper</td></tr>      </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by my single father as an only child. <h2>Adrik Silveraxe</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ɑdɹɪk sɪlvɝeɪks /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="cbc8d617-6d8e-432d-9575-4fa5fb7940b4">          <span class="first-character">A</span>drik Silveraxe    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="ad86d961-4dd8-4d9a-bff9-3a3b9429773d" id="ad86d961-4dd8-4d9a-bff9-3a3b9429773d" role="tooltip" title="36 years old, to be exact.">an adult</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="4c6eb03c-03b3-4a30-99e7-383d2b0106ca" id="4c6eb03c-03b3-4a30-99e7-383d2b0106ca" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 4″">quite squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="43450250-a1d2-466a-9403-7b9cb9b523ab" id="43450250-a1d2-466a-9403-7b9cb9b523ab" role="tooltip" title="192lbs. (with a BMI of 35)">quite large</span>, and has blue eyes        and a goatee,    with brown skin.    The most notable physical trait of Adrik is that he has no earlobes. </p> <p>   Adrik cannot resist flirting.         He sighs after each sentence.            He is bashful in the face of praise, blame-prone, and unable to control any urges.     When he is relaxed, he is greedy.  In moments of stress, he becomes overly protective.  Religion-wise, Adrik is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="b24a8ea8-bb20-4c14-8b4c-dddaf21382df" id="b24a8ea8-bb20-4c14-8b4c-dddaf21382df" role="tooltip" title="Adrik Silveraxe is a casual follower of Hades, and he likes to provoke heated 'debates' with people who follow other religions.">a cautious listener</span> of <a data-id="hades" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal hades" title="Hades is the god of the Dead and the first son of Kronos. However when He, Zeus and Poseidon were drawing lots for the division of the cosmos, Hades gained dominion of the Underworld, where he rules over the dead." href="#hades">Hades</a>.  <p>      Adrik is having reasonable success as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="3ae63eae-95c5-4043-bfd4-a8427ca7a98b" id="3ae63eae-95c5-4043-bfd4-a8427ca7a98b" role="tooltip" title="Designs, makes, and repairs necklaces, bracelets, rings, etc., often containing jewels.">jeweller</span>, with a background of being an acolyte.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="781f3e86-9ff1-4da4-bf26-d0d48a92bdcd" id="781f3e86-9ff1-4da4-bf26-d0d48a92bdcd" role="tooltip" title="Adrik lives a comfortable life, filled with good food and wine">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Adrik currently has spectacles worth 5gp in his pockets,    and 40 Gold 6 Silver 6 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403" title="Gunnloa Street is a narrow gravel and hewn rock street. It is made of poorly packed gravel, which shifts around under foot. Grated storm drains at regular intervals grant access to the sewer system. It has been named after Gunnloa Durthane, who was a much beloved prostitute, one of whose clients bought the road as a thankyou." href="#03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403">Gunnloa Street</a>.               Adrik knows Common and Dwarvish.           </p> <section>Adrik currently earns 2 Gold 1 Silver 8 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>2 Gold 4 Silver 5 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>2 Gold 1 Silver 8 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="e05419af-b9fe-4e10-a32d-5002f979bf97" id="e05419af-b9fe-4e10-a32d-5002f979bf97" role="tooltip" title="Adrik lives a comfortable life, filled with good food and wine">comfortable</span>)</td><td>2 Gold 7 Silver 4 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 5 Silver 6 Copper</td></tr>          <tr><td>Money owed to <a data-id="2bddc27b-c0ce-478b-a046-44c3d87b0f33" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 2bddc27b-c0ce-478b-a046-44c3d87b0f33" title="A rather small gnomish man called Eldon Murnig who is a gambler." href="#2bddc27b-c0ce-478b-a046-44c3d87b0f33">Eldon Murnig</a></td><td>10 Gold 7 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>          <tr><td>Money owed to <a data-id="e864ad41-c288-4870-a529-410591dbe65b" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal e864ad41-c288-4870-a529-410591dbe65b" title="A young adult gnome with very rounded ears called Sindri Daergel who is a kidnapper." href="#e864ad41-c288-4870-a529-410591dbe65b">Sindri Daergel</a></td><td>42 Gold 8 Silver 8 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born among people of a different race, and was raised by my mother and father as an only child. I had a poor upbringing in a rundown shack. <h2>Urshar Loderr</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ɝʃɑɹ loʊdɹ /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="3ff2e70c-79c2-4865-a0d3-101f5b455c72">          <span class="first-character">U</span>rshar Loderr    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="df6d76a7-c810-4232-9d64-f0adb1b626b0" id="df6d76a7-c810-4232-9d64-f0adb1b626b0" role="tooltip" title="33 years old, to be exact.">a mid thirties</span> female dwarf.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="63521d0b-beb5-4168-84ba-79ff2654fd23" id="63521d0b-beb5-4168-84ba-79ff2654fd23" role="tooltip" title="4ft. ">somewhat tiny</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="41e64699-626a-4f64-b0c5-a9dbd126aa31" id="41e64699-626a-4f64-b0c5-a9dbd126aa31" role="tooltip" title="175lbs. (with a BMI of 37)">quite large</span>, and has green eyes    with pale skin.    The most notable physical trait of Urshar is that she has an emotionless gaze. </p> <p>   Urshar cannot resist a juicy secret.            She is perky, merciless, and imprudent.     When she is relaxed, she is carefree.  In moments of stress, she becomes murderous.  Religion-wise, Urshar is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="8b9324dc-95c2-431e-b464-daa14de88a25" id="8b9324dc-95c2-431e-b464-daa14de88a25" role="tooltip" title="Urshar Loderr is a casual follower of Athena, and she likes to provoke heated 'debates' with people who follow other religions.">a cautious listener</span> of <a data-id="athena" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal athena" title="Athena is a wise goddess and protects those that follow her. She does have the rage of a goddess, and affronts to her are paid back with divine retribution." href="#athena">Athena</a>.  <p>          Perhaps due to sexism,       Urshar has recently been unsuccessful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="668bf7b0-0a53-49ba-89b0-a02ba72c0a53" id="668bf7b0-0a53-49ba-89b0-a02ba72c0a53" role="tooltip" title="Makes, alters, repairs, as well as occasionally designing garments.">tailor</span>, with a background of being an acolyte.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="b461113f-8697-403e-9c9f-189d55999d46" id="b461113f-8697-403e-9c9f-189d55999d46" role="tooltip" title="Urshar lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">peasantry</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Urshar currently has a palm-sized glass sphere in her pockets,    and 50 Gold 4 Silver 9 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="ebd5996d-85e2-420b-b1a8-1cb1ad0f6b08" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal ebd5996d-85e2-420b-b1a8-1cb1ad0f6b08" title="Common Crescent is a  gravel and hewn rock road. It is made of colourful rocks and pebbles. A row of houses and buildings is splayed out, with enough room for a horse and cart to turn around. " href="#ebd5996d-85e2-420b-b1a8-1cb1ad0f6b08">Common Crescent</a>.               Urshar knows Common and Dwarvish.           </p> <section>Urshar currently earns  9 Silver 3 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 8.5 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td> 9 Silver 3 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="489e2dec-afe4-4746-b658-4443b9813a67" id="489e2dec-afe4-4746-b658-4443b9813a67" role="tooltip" title="Urshar lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">poor</span>)</td><td> 3 Silver</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td> 6 Silver 3 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born in the home of a midwife, and was raised by my single mother with my brother. I had a modest upbringing in a nice house.  I had a few close friends, and my childhood was a relatively normal one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a tailor</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I followed a lover into religious service, but tragically, they were killed. The faith was the only thing that stopped me from ending my own life. I've had trouble as a tailor. I guess some people are born with it- I'm sure as hell not. I will someday get revenge on the corrupt temple hierarchy who branded me a heretic. I trust that my deity will guide my actions, I have faith that if I work hard, things will go well."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...When I was younger, to pay off a debt, I spent some time as a tailor. Later in my life, I was caught aiding and abetting the crime of murder, but due to my amazing lawyer, I was found not guilty.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr>       <th>Name</th>       <th>Race</th>       <th>Occupation</th>       <th>Relationship</th>            </tr>          <tr>       <td><a <h2>Oloric Fire-Forge</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ʌlɔɝɪk undefinedundefined /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="68f0225b-8a80-4880-b074-a1406a726cf1">          <span class="first-character">O</span>loric Fire-Forge    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="a659cdbf-8d63-4f5a-a629-36934737b88d" id="a659cdbf-8d63-4f5a-a629-36934737b88d" role="tooltip" title="136 years old, to be exact.">a middle aged</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="9dff4cf6-3e4e-4e08-a909-c25ad77f5368" id="9dff4cf6-3e4e-4e08-a909-c25ad77f5368" role="tooltip" title="3ft. 11″">somewhat tiny</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="bc0ba258-0b4d-4803-b04b-84f7c61d9908" id="bc0ba258-0b4d-4803-b04b-84f7c61d9908" role="tooltip" title="170lbs. (with a BMI of 38)">unbelievably large</span>, and has amber eyes        and a rather wild, unkempt beard,    with light tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Oloric is that he has long bangs. </p> <p>   Oloric is always shaking.            He is charitable, quick to believe, generous to a fault.     When he is relaxed, he is compassionate.  In moments of stress, he becomes determined.  Religion-wise, Oloric is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="c67570a9-526b-4c28-8eda-3a23eb34b604" id="c67570a9-526b-4c28-8eda-3a23eb34b604" role="tooltip" title="Oloric Fire-Forge is critical of religion, but is nominally a follower of Apollo. Because of his doubts, he enjoys spirited debates about the flaws of various religions – both other peoples' faiths and his own.">a critical student</span> of <a data-id="apollo" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal apollo" title="The twin brother of Artemis, Apollo is the inventor of music. Those that he loves and loses or those that he hates can find themselves transformed and immortalised as a part of nature. " href="#apollo">Apollo</a>.  <p>          Perhaps due to sexism,       Oloric is somewhat unsuccessful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="bab26d40-b403-40dc-b0b0-34eae0713c3f" id="bab26d40-b403-40dc-b0b0-34eae0713c3f" role="tooltip" title="Steals peoples property, especially by stealth and without using force or violence.">thief</span>, with a background of being a sage.         He belongs to the paupery social class, but lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though.    </p> <p>   Oloric currently has a flask full of salt water in his pockets,    and 60 Gold 2 Silver 3 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403" title="Gunnloa Street is a narrow gravel and hewn rock street. It is made of poorly packed gravel, which shifts around under foot. Grated storm drains at regular intervals grant access to the sewer system. It has been named after Gunnloa Durthane, who was a much beloved prostitute, one of whose clients bought the road as a thankyou." href="#03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403">Gunnloa Street</a>.               Oloric knows Common and Dwarvish.           </p> <section>Oloric currently earns 1 Gold 9 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 9 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="20c6c956-1e44-48cf-b720-3ce8d98d5388" id="20c6c956-1e44-48cf-b720-3ce8d98d5388" role="tooltip" title="Oloric lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>               <tr><td>Money owed by <a data-id="9f200a5a-aed8-4156-abe7-b1bb4e0297d4" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 9f200a5a-aed8-4156-abe7-b1bb4e0297d4" title="A somewhat short male half-orc called Druuk Prathka who is a shoemaker." href="#9f200a5a-aed8-4156-abe7-b1bb4e0297d4">Druuk Prathka</a></td><td>23 Gold 5 Silver</td></tr>      </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born on a wagon, and was raised by my mother and father with my brother. I had a squalid upbringing in a rundown shack.  I had a few close friends, and my childhood was a relatively normal one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a thief</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I impressed a traveling wizard, who told me that I was squandering my talents and that I should seek out an education to take advantage of my gifts. I've had a bit of a downturn as a thief. If it keeps up for much longer, I'm going to begin losing hope. I have an ancient text that holds terrible secrets that must not fall into the wrong hands. I think that the goal of a life of study is the betterment of oneself."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I was caught aiding and abetting the crime of selling contraband , but due to being under a spell, I was found not guilty. I went to an agriculture festival where I saw some durable cherries. At the end of the festival they won  bronze in the growers competition.At one point I met the love of my life, who is no longer with me. How could I ever forget the time I met a <a data-id="32adca1d-f767-4bf0-855d-e8326fbc52e2" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 32adca1d-f767-4bf0-855d-e8326fbc52e2" title="A dwarf with a well-loved beard, with ornamental beads woven into it called Gimgen Goldfinder who is a peasant." href="#32adca1d-f767-4bf0-855d-e8326fbc52e2">man</a>, and we played cards. He decided that I was cheating- it was all a setup, but a very good one. I'm still on the lookout for him to this very day. After that, I once had my home destroyed by magical beings.I'll always remember the time because of a promise, I did some time as a thief. After that, I used to play cards in a pub, and one time supposedly cheated a <a data-id="6566a440-37f6-40e0-a397-776dd0e68722" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 6566a440-37f6-40e0-a397-776dd0e68722" title="A somewhat tiny dwarven man called Darrak Daraln who is a peasant." href="#6566a440-37f6-40e0-a397-776dd0e68722">man</a> out of his winnings; it was a misunderstanding, but I cannot convince him otherwise. I would rather have backup the next time that I face him.Once I came across a horde of ghouls feasting on a dead body in my youth.  At one point, undefinedI met the love of my life, who is no longer with me.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr> <h2>Druuk Prathka</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /dɹʌʌk pɹæθkʌ /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="9f200a5a-aed8-4156-abe7-b1bb4e0297d4">          <span class="first-character">D</span>ruuk Prathka    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="3e9eb2b0-2565-42d7-91b6-83e087d038b5" id="3e9eb2b0-2565-42d7-91b6-83e087d038b5" role="tooltip" title="51 years old, to be exact.">an old</span> male half-orc.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="f2c94085-9b1a-48a7-9790-159ed2aef160" id="f2c94085-9b1a-48a7-9790-159ed2aef160" role="tooltip" title="5ft. 7″">somewhat short</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="1cceb303-bf57-47dd-be14-3f1d5d368789" id="1cceb303-bf57-47dd-be14-3f1d5d368789" role="tooltip" title="200lbs. (with a BMI of 26)">broad and muscular</span>, and has green eyes    with fair skin.    The most notable physical trait of Druuk is that he has thin, fat earlobes. </p> <p>   Druuk chews with an open mouth.            He is always doubting people, restrained, and always thinking twice.     When he is relaxed, he is cautious.  In moments of stress, he becomes meticulous.  Religion-wise, Druuk is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="4e7814ad-dc5f-46f6-8a82-565323a2af80" id="4e7814ad-dc5f-46f6-8a82-565323a2af80" role="tooltip" title="Druuk Prathka is a casual follower of Zeus, and he likes to provoke heated 'debates' with people who follow other religions.">an open-minded seeker</span> of <a data-id="zeus" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal zeus" title="Zeus is the leader of the Greek gods, and lives atop Mount Olympus, where he rules over the mortal world below." href="#zeus">Zeus</a>.  <p>          Perhaps due to sexism,       Druuk has been slightly unsuccessful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="6a5e4d21-6bb3-4a31-adcb-84183920ed8c" id="6a5e4d21-6bb3-4a31-adcb-84183920ed8c" role="tooltip" title="Makes shoes out of different materials.">shoemaker</span>, with a background of being a criminal.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="f18979d2-0758-46ee-a086-34b96d035557" id="f18979d2-0758-46ee-a086-34b96d035557" role="tooltip" title="Druuk lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">peasantry</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Druuk currently has 27 cp in his pockets,    and 80 Gold 3 Silver 7 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="d228384c-7090-4096-9e5d-cc40b0ca71dc" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal d228384c-7090-4096-9e5d-cc40b0ca71dc" title="Baker Road is a path-sized gravel and hewn rock road. It is made of poorly packed gravel, which shifts around under foot. The road has the occasional pothole. " href="#d228384c-7090-4096-9e5d-cc40b0ca71dc">Baker Road</a>.               Druuk knows Common and Orc.           </p> <section>Druuk currently earns 1 Gold 1 Silver 2 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 8.5 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 1 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="6a0017a9-00ca-4a59-862d-7ac8f08e16bf" id="6a0017a9-00ca-4a59-862d-7ac8f08e16bf" role="tooltip" title="Druuk lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 1 Silver 9 Copper</td></tr>          <tr><td>Money owed to <a data-id="68f0225b-8a80-4880-b074-a1406a726cf1" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 68f0225b-8a80-4880-b074-a1406a726cf1" title="A dwarf with a rather wild, unkempt beard called Oloric Fire-Forge who is a thief." href="#68f0225b-8a80-4880-b074-a1406a726cf1">Oloric Fire-Forge</a></td><td>23 Gold 5 Silver</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born in a tower, and was raised by my extended family as an only child. <h2>Artin Battlehammer</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ɑɹtʌn bætʌlhæmɝ /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="4569e416-b02c-4ae2-8187-b5acc0186187">          <span class="first-character">A</span>rtin Battlehammer    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="c072e980-114f-4c0b-a6f9-751e18a93a13" id="c072e980-114f-4c0b-a6f9-751e18a93a13" role="tooltip" title="148 years old, to be exact.">an old</span> female dwarf.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="b43b5ea2-d8fb-427a-9c05-38ffb2606dea" id="b43b5ea2-d8fb-427a-9c05-38ffb2606dea" role="tooltip" title="3ft. 11″">somewhat tiny</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="0d37df51-9f74-47f2-a1e0-8af1a6642ce9" id="0d37df51-9f74-47f2-a1e0-8af1a6642ce9" role="tooltip" title="156lbs. (with a BMI of 35)">plump</span>, and has brown eyes    with dark tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Artin is that she has thick braids of hair banded with gold. </p> <p>   Artin fidgets.            She is blame-prone.     When she is relaxed, she is sensible.  In moments of stress, she becomes caustic.  Religion-wise, Artin is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="317e06d6-4ff0-48fa-9103-8377bf79299f" id="317e06d6-4ff0-48fa-9103-8377bf79299f" role="tooltip" title="Artin Battlehammer is usually a quiet follower of Hermes, but can be quite rude to anyone who criticizes her choice of deity.">a casual observer</span> of <a data-id="hermes" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal hermes" title="Hermes is the hessenger of the gods and the personal messenger of Zeus. He brings the souls of the deceased to the edge of the underworld, where they are ferried deeper by the Cthonic gods" href="#hermes">Hermes</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against her,         Artin is currently having mild success as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="7e47378c-8611-4018-b72b-d0f12e4b400c" id="7e47378c-8611-4018-b72b-d0f12e4b400c" role="tooltip" title="Controls prostitutes and arranges clients for them, taking part of their earnings in return.">pimp</span>, with a background of being a peasant.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="a77578fb-fc7f-4830-b537-e18f4870fada" id="a77578fb-fc7f-4830-b537-e18f4870fada" role="tooltip" title="Artin lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Artin currently has 5 sp in her pockets,    and 40 Gold 2 Silver 1 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="b00b276d-6c1a-404e-8199-4c46fad1f650" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal b00b276d-6c1a-404e-8199-4c46fad1f650" title="Noble Plaza is a path-sized gravel and hewn rock lane. It is made of noisy and shifting gravel. Better watch your footing. Houses lean over into the street on both sides, limiting the amount of sun that is visible. " href="#b00b276d-6c1a-404e-8199-4c46fad1f650">Noble Plaza</a>.               Artin knows Common and Dwarvish.               She prefers the same gender, but sometimes finds other genders attractive           </p> <section>Artin currently earns  9 Silver 1 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td> 9 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="194efcb8-aa57-49d6-a566-75043dc5d3ca" id="194efcb8-aa57-49d6-a566-75043dc5d3ca" role="tooltip" title="Artin lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">poor</span>)</td><td> 3 Silver</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td> 6 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born in the home of a friend, and was raised by my mother and father as an only child. I had a squalid upbringing in a large house.
