<h2>Falkrann Fahack</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /fækɹæn fʌhʌk /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="1f2c392b-cf56-48fd-a228-16a8e75ce96b">          <span class="first-character">F</span>alkrann Fahack    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="5eb26eba-6c63-479b-b8c5-870a18caf364" id="5eb26eba-6c63-479b-b8c5-870a18caf364" role="tooltip" title="138 years old, to be exact.">a middle aged</span> female dwarf.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="124434ca-6a0c-40e7-badf-677a35d862d4" id="124434ca-6a0c-40e7-badf-677a35d862d4" role="tooltip" title="3ft. 9″">rather small</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="58feeba9-59c0-42b6-a533-64868520c22c" id="58feeba9-59c0-42b6-a533-64868520c22c" role="tooltip" title="138lbs. (with a BMI of 34)">quite large</span>, and has blue eyes    with translucent skin.    The most notable physical trait of Falkrann is that she has a scar on the throat. </p> <p>   Falkrann cannot resist a juicy secret.            She is reckless.     When she is relaxed, she is carefree.  In moments of stress, she becomes spiteful.  Religion-wise, Falkrann is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="44e715ab-920e-4f67-9460-3710e2fdd5f7" id="44e715ab-920e-4f67-9460-3710e2fdd5f7" role="tooltip" title="Falkrann Fahack is usually a quiet follower of Hermes, but can be quite rude to anyone who criticizes her choice of deity.">a quiet true believer</span> of <a data-id="hermes" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal hermes" title="Hermes is the hessenger of the gods and the personal messenger of Zeus. He brings the souls of the deceased to the edge of the underworld, where they are ferried deeper by the Cthonic gods" href="#hermes">Hermes</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against her,         Falkrann is currently having extreme success as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="92543def-4a13-423f-8fcf-d774f6552a41" id="92543def-4a13-423f-8fcf-d774f6552a41" role="tooltip" title="Cuts hair and shaves or trims beards.">barber</span>, with a background of being an outlander.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="eaf89495-e50a-491d-bee8-9f9e4665f5b5" id="eaf89495-e50a-491d-bee8-9f9e4665f5b5" role="tooltip" title="Falkrann lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Falkrann currently has thirteen mouse teeth in her pockets,    and 350 Gold 5 Silver 4 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="b00b276d-6c1a-404e-8199-4c46fad1f650" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal b00b276d-6c1a-404e-8199-4c46fad1f650" title="Noble Plaza is a path-sized gravel and hewn rock lane. It is made of noisy and shifting gravel. Better watch your footing. Houses lean over into the street on both sides, limiting the amount of sun that is visible. " href="#b00b276d-6c1a-404e-8199-4c46fad1f650">Noble Plaza</a>.               Falkrann knows Common and Dwarvish.               She primarily prefers other genders, but sometimes finds the same gender attractive           </p> <section>Falkrann currently earns  9 Silver 1 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td> 9 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="a82ba9ff-3fec-4bbf-829f-ccdb77c6324b" id="a82ba9ff-3fec-4bbf-829f-ccdb77c6324b" role="tooltip" title="Falkrann lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">poor</span>)</td><td> 3 Silver</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td> 6 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by my single mother as an only child. I had a comfortable upbringing in a very impressive house.  I had a few close friends, and my childhood was a relatively normal one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a barber</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I spent a lot of time in the wilderness as a youngster, and I came to love that way of life. I have a steady hand, and like to think that I am a good conversationalist- barbering was a natural fit. It is my duty to provide children to sustain my tribe. If I dishonor myself, I bring dishonor to my whole tribe"</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time there was a civil war within the town that I fought in. I managed to escape the battle unscathed, but many of my friends were killed or injured. To pay off a debt, I had to work as a barber.How could I ever forget the time because of a promise, I did some time as a outlander. I'll always remember the time I worked under <a data-id="5851c661-16f2-44d9-b9b5-42699ed012e1" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 5851c661-16f2-44d9-b9b5-42699ed012e1" title="A rather squat female dwarf called Jarana Bofdarm who is a locksmith." href="#5851c661-16f2-44d9-b9b5-42699ed012e1">Jarana Bofdarm</a> a famous locksmith. During that time I learned a lot of valuable life lessons. At one point I saved a wizard's life, and as a token of his thanks, he gave me a Drunkard's Bronze Figurine of Falsehoods.<blockquote><h4>Drunkard's Bronze Figurine of Falsehoods</h4>The bearer always knows the direction to the closest alcoholic beverage. The bearer gains a +1 bonus to Charisma (Deception) checks.</blockquote> One time I was a novice to <a data-id="630d7365-4af9-4ed4-9f8c-247193d03f85" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 630d7365-4af9-4ed4-9f8c-247193d03f85" title="A somewhat tiny male dwarf with a thin unibrow called Dain Rubyeye who is a silversmith." href="#630d7365-4af9-4ed4-9f8c-247193d03f85">Dain Rubyeye</a> a skilled, but hidden silversmith. During that time I learned a lot about myself. Oh, and I can't forget the time I spent some time working as a outlander. One time I had a brief stint working for a famous bard while on a long journey. Once I met the love of my life, who is no longer with me. You might not believe it, but for a while I did some work as a outlander.  At one point, there was a small war between a rival lord that I was forced to take part with. I suffered some serious injuries, and had to be carried off the field.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr> <h2>Erias Eversharp</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ɛɹiʌz ɛvɝʃɑɹp /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="2df24fb6-82c5-411c-869a-9a872a88a8f0">          <span class="first-character">E</span>rias Eversharp    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="bcaf9a0e-388e-4f09-80e2-31efb07f954b" id="bcaf9a0e-388e-4f09-80e2-31efb07f954b" role="tooltip" title="105 years old, to be exact.">a middle aged</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="6bf3a8b5-da05-4a72-a32f-1361dd473464" id="6bf3a8b5-da05-4a72-a32f-1361dd473464" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 5″">somewhat squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="b1d83289-f015-4ffc-bce5-2d764b745e70" id="b1d83289-f015-4ffc-bce5-2d764b745e70" role="tooltip" title="222lbs. (with a BMI of 39)">built like a brick shithouse</span>, and has hazel eyes        and a dreadful beard,    with translucent skin.    The most notable physical trait of Erias is that he has a squashed nose. </p> <p>   Erias drinks too much.         He mutters.            He is imprudent, indulgent, and energetic.     When he is relaxed, he is mischeivous.  In moments of stress, he becomes fanatical.  Religion-wise, Erias is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="2577656f-f118-4ca1-aabb-68154a9338fb" id="2577656f-f118-4ca1-aabb-68154a9338fb" role="tooltip" title="Erias Eversharp is a casual follower of Aphrodite, and he likes to provoke heated 'debates' with people who follow other religions.">a cautious listener</span> of <a data-id="aphrodite" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal aphrodite" title="Aphrodite is the goddess of love and scorns those who stay away from relationships. Her love can be a thing of beauty or a thing of terror and destruction." href="#aphrodite">Aphrodite</a>.  <p>      Erias is slightly unsuccessful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="83db1cd9-f438-471d-9e4a-d77d48aa61f9" id="83db1cd9-f438-471d-9e4a-d77d48aa61f9" role="tooltip" title="An ordained minister of an order ranking below that of priest.">deacon</span>, with a background of being a sage.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="f9145eae-9537-44d7-a20d-b59c04f304f5" id="f9145eae-9537-44d7-a20d-b59c04f304f5" role="tooltip" title="Erias lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Erias currently has a mess kit in his pockets,    and 110 Gold 4 Silver 2 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="02ff1684-74e8-47c3-b854-120a0fd8bde2" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 02ff1684-74e8-47c3-b854-120a0fd8bde2" title="Strongheart Crescent is a wide, multi-lane gravel and rock square. It is made of colourful rocks and pebbles. There's a wagon with a cracked wheel by the side of the road. It was named after Therlin Strongheart, who was a dwarf who brought riches to the people of Bugshaw." href="#02ff1684-74e8-47c3-b854-120a0fd8bde2">Strongheart Crescent</a>.               Erias knows Common and Dwarvish.           </p> <section>Erias currently earns 1 Gold 8 Silver 2 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>2 Gold 4 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 8 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="bb2a25f6-8490-4a90-9eb8-10abc9fd4671" id="bb2a25f6-8490-4a90-9eb8-10abc9fd4671" role="tooltip" title="Erias lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 5 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td> 3 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born in a barn, and was raised by my single father as an only child. I had a modest upbringing in a large house.  I spent most of my childhood alone, and had no close friends.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a deacon</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I was always an avid reader, and became a sage to learn more from the thousands of books that I tended to. I've had a bit of a downturn as a deacon. If it keeps up for much longer, I'm going to begin losing hope. I've been searching my whole life for the answer to a certain question. Knowledge is, in my opinion, the path to power and domination."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I used to play cards in a pub, and one time supposedly cheated a <a data-id="da03f582-4f40-4599-ba5f-08e005a4269d" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal da03f582-4f40-4599-ba5f-08e005a4269d" title="A lean male half-elf with big, floppy ears called Fivin Hill who is a peasant." href="#da03f582-4f40-4599-ba5f-08e005a4269d">man</a> out of his winnings; I suppose that I'm at least partially to blame. I doubt I'll ever meet him again. I forget exactly when, but at one point, I won second place at a garden tournament for my delectable honeyberries. I'll always remember the time some friends and I went to a festival. While I was there, I ate enough to not eat the next day. Not to mention there was the time there was a minor skirmish with some orcs that I was involved with. I managed to escape the battle unscathed, but many of my friends were killed or injured.One time I was nearly caught and convicted in the middle of counterfeiting, but managed to escape. They are still after me, though. Oh, and I can't forget the time I had a mishap with a mind control spell- someone I thought of as family tried to fool me into giving up my title, but their spell failed. One time there was no other work so for a while I was a sage. Not to mention there was the time I had a brief stint working for a famous historian when I was spending some time as a sage.You might not believe it, but I made an <a data-id="f3797642-da29-4128-aba1-fa4a1ea826cc" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal f3797642-da29-4128-aba1-fa4a1ea826cc" title="A dwarf with a scraggly beard called Thoradin Silveraxe who is a peasant." href="#f3797642-da29-4128-aba1-fa4a1ea826cc">enemy</a> for life in my travels- it was a misunderstanding, but I cannot convince him otherwise. I'm still on the lookout for him to this very day. Oh, and I can't forget the time I came across a famous enchanter in my travels.  At one point, I was a novice to <a data-id="00d12f4d-2d2c-4b30-896e-accf2833c76b" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 00d12f4d-2d2c-4b30-896e-accf2833c76b" title="An adult dwarf with thin, fat earlobes called Sannl Bloodkith who is an artist." href="#00d12f4d-2d2c-4b30-896e-accf2833c76b">Sannl Bloodkith</a> a legendary artist. <h2>Kildrak Holderhek</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /kɪldɹʌk hoʊldɝhɛk /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="6c910ab4-f5db-468c-a838-f08c52e11dd3">          <span class="first-character">K</span>ildrak Holderhek    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="511d046a-9429-4dfe-9194-3e9beda2f9d2" id="511d046a-9429-4dfe-9194-3e9beda2f9d2" role="tooltip" title="33 years old, to be exact.">a mid thirties</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="b3bbd107-c82e-44cd-bbd7-75bd524ffd8d" id="b3bbd107-c82e-44cd-bbd7-75bd524ffd8d" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 1″">rather squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="b6e8de6d-9475-47ba-8714-0363c0048f83" id="b6e8de6d-9475-47ba-8714-0363c0048f83" role="tooltip" title="158lbs. (with a BMI of 32)">quite solidly built</span>, and has gray eyes        and a long, flowing beard,    with tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Kildrak is that he has a well sculpted jaw. </p> <p>   Kildrak loses train of thought easily.            He is      When he is relaxed, he is outspoken.  In moments of stress, he becomes manipulative.  Religion-wise, Kildrak is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="97c8502c-4c48-433a-882c-ab64a6952f68" id="97c8502c-4c48-433a-882c-ab64a6952f68" role="tooltip" title="Kildrak Holderhek is critical of religion, but is nominally a follower of Aphrodite. Despite his supposed faith, he enjoys ragging on any and all religions, and will openly criticize any faithful people he meets.">a critical student</span> of <a data-id="aphrodite" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal aphrodite" title="Aphrodite is the goddess of love and scorns those who stay away from relationships. Her love can be a thing of beauty or a thing of terror and destruction." href="#aphrodite">Aphrodite</a>.  <p>      Kildrak is a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="eb66b368-ea45-4682-ae57-4f83b7d76980" id="eb66b368-ea45-4682-ae57-4f83b7d76980" role="tooltip" title="Uses their artistic talents to induce magical effects.">bard</span>, with a background of being an entertainer.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="6dc88d57-0a79-4ec3-9d1b-6c5a8f90ef81" id="6dc88d57-0a79-4ec3-9d1b-6c5a8f90ef81" role="tooltip" title="Kildrak lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Kildrak currently has thirteen mouse teeth in his pockets,    and 110 Gold 1 Silver 8 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="02ff1684-74e8-47c3-b854-120a0fd8bde2" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 02ff1684-74e8-47c3-b854-120a0fd8bde2" title="Strongheart Crescent is a wide, multi-lane gravel and rock square. It is made of colourful rocks and pebbles. There's a wagon with a cracked wheel by the side of the road. It was named after Therlin Strongheart, who was a dwarf who brought riches to the people of Bugshaw." href="#02ff1684-74e8-47c3-b854-120a0fd8bde2">Strongheart Crescent</a>.               Kildrak knows Common and Dwarvish.           </p> <section>Kildrak currently earns 1 Gold 8 Silver 2 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>2 Gold 4 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 8 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="6e9f93e8-0188-4a1f-8190-1e02deb66869" id="6e9f93e8-0188-4a1f-8190-1e02deb66869" role="tooltip" title="Kildrak lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 5 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td> 3 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born in a street, and was raised by my mother and father as an only child. I had a comfortable upbringing in a small house.  I had a few close friends, and my childhood was a relatively normal one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a bard</summary> <div class="descriptive">"A traveling entertainer took me in to teach me the trade, and I learned to love it. I joined a society of scholars and orators, who helped teach me how to harness my music and turn it into magic. I want to be famous, whatever it takes. When I perform, I want to make beautiful things for the pleasure of my audience"</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I had the honor to go to the royal banquet of a local <a data-id="e6b45ff6-1ae6-4296-8154-81644d1fb7ae" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal e6b45ff6-1ae6-4296-8154-81644d1fb7ae" title="A middle aged dwarf with a snake tattoo called Orsik Fire-Forge who is a peasant." href="#e6b45ff6-1ae6-4296-8154-81644d1fb7ae">noble</a> in celebration of a recent coronation. I'll always remember the time for a time, I worked for a famous sculptor in my travels. I was a novice to <a data-id="c148cf8f-8bf4-417c-bec4-3c96932471a9" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal c148cf8f-8bf4-417c-bec4-3c96932471a9" title="A young adult dwarf with a flabby face called Erias Morigak who is a silversmith." href="#c148cf8f-8bf4-417c-bec4-3c96932471a9">Erias Morigak</a> a well known silversmith. During that time I learned I'm not very good at the trade. At one point, for a while I did some work as a entertainer.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr>       <th>Name</th> <h2>Vistra Deepdelver</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /vɪstɹʌ dipdɛlvɝ /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="5ca415fa-a639-46de-b169-7709a836966e">          <span class="first-character">V</span>istra Deepdelver    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="c7424268-e75d-4c2f-bbbf-d4e168da2401" id="c7424268-e75d-4c2f-bbbf-d4e168da2401" role="tooltip" title="108 years old, to be exact.">a middle aged</span> female dwarf.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="e452dacd-00ad-4aa5-94e8-c83f68475c3f" id="e452dacd-00ad-4aa5-94e8-c83f68475c3f" role="tooltip" title="4ft. ">somewhat tiny</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="90fd97ec-ae5c-46b1-8334-b32141aa2961" id="90fd97ec-ae5c-46b1-8334-b32141aa2961" role="tooltip" title="155lbs. (with a BMI of 33)">rather round</span>, and has gray eyes        and a dreadful beard,    with pale skin.    The most notable physical trait of Vistra is that she has very full lips. </p> <p>   Vistra corrects people's grammar when they speak.            She is reckless.     When she is relaxed, she is carefree.  In moments of stress, she becomes spiteful.  Religion-wise, Vistra is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="af379832-594c-411a-bace-a49db55ef53c" id="af379832-594c-411a-bace-a49db55ef53c" role="tooltip" title="Vistra Deepdelver is a casual follower of Demeter, and can be quite rude towards those who worship 'inferior' gods.">a cautious listener</span> of <a data-id="demeter" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal demeter" title="Demeter is the goddess of Agriculture - her favour promised a bountiful harvest and more grain then could be eaten. However her anger promised frosts and famine." href="#demeter">Demeter</a>.  <p>          Perhaps due to sexism,       Vistra is slightly unsuccessful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="6acfca80-7f76-4f82-8d89-17855bced58d" id="6acfca80-7f76-4f82-8d89-17855bced58d" role="tooltip" title="Unlawfully occupies an uninhabited building or unused land.">squatter</span>, with a background of being a peasant.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="de173f04-e449-48a4-b6bc-fcc33b97b9ec" id="de173f04-e449-48a4-b6bc-fcc33b97b9ec" role="tooltip" title="Vistra lives a squalid existence, eating terrible food with no alcohol, and few creature comforts">paupery</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Vistra currently has the cork from a wine bottle in her pockets,    and 130 Gold 4 Silver 4 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="ebd5996d-85e2-420b-b1a8-1cb1ad0f6b08" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal ebd5996d-85e2-420b-b1a8-1cb1ad0f6b08" title="Common Crescent is a  gravel and hewn rock road. It is made of colourful rocks and pebbles. A row of houses and buildings is splayed out, with enough room for a horse and cart to turn around. " href="#ebd5996d-85e2-420b-b1a8-1cb1ad0f6b08">Common Crescent</a>.               Vistra knows Common and Dwarvish.           </p> <section>Vistra currently earns  1 Silver 3 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td> 1 Silver 5 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td> 1 Silver 3 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="114c9432-583d-4cca-a84d-8ffda7048f82" id="114c9432-583d-4cca-a84d-8ffda7048f82" role="tooltip" title="Vistra lives a squalid existence, eating terrible food with no alcohol, and few creature comforts">squalid</span>)</td><td> 1 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td> 2 Copper</td></tr>               <tr><td>Money owed by <a data-id="235fc7f0-e90d-46c6-9be6-648fd5f6bef5" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 235fc7f0-e90d-46c6-9be6-648fd5f6bef5" title="A dark tan skinned quite squat dwarf called Orsik Silverstone who is a wizard." href="#235fc7f0-e90d-46c6-9be6-648fd5f6bef5">Orsik Silverstone</a></td><td>107 Gold 1 Copper</td></tr>      </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by my adoptive family as an only child. I had a squalid upbringing in no real permanent address. I didn't know my parents growing up. I always found it easy to make friends, and I loved being around people.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a squatter</summary> <div class="descriptive">"  I've had a bit of a downturn as a squatter. If it keeps up for much longer, I'm going to begin losing hope.   <b>Stoicism</b>. I must be strong for those that rely on me, no matter what."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I was caught and convicted of arson, and spent 4 years in jail before being released. You might not believe it, but I spent some time working as a squatter. Oh, and I can't forget the time I was caught and convicted of extortion, and spent 1 years in jail before being released. After that, to pay off a debt, I had to work as a squatter. At one point, I was framed by a <a data-id="c4f4cdc7-e6fa-44a2-b9a1-c1827610f650" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal c4f4cdc7-e6fa-44a2-b9a1-c1827610f650" title="A quite large male dwarf called Tordek Dankil who is a peasant." href="#c4f4cdc7-e6fa-44a2-b9a1-c1827610f650">scoundrel</a> for a crime I didn't commit- it was all a setup, but a very good one. That's all behind me now and I hope it stays that way.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr>       <th>Name</th> <h2>Orsik Silverstone</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ɔɹsɪk sɪlvɝstoʊn /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="235fc7f0-e90d-46c6-9be6-648fd5f6bef5">          <span class="first-character">O</span>rsik Silverstone    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="4ae62edf-2e33-4628-8c6d-d5e97c942e62" id="4ae62edf-2e33-4628-8c6d-d5e97c942e62" role="tooltip" title="23 years old, to be exact.">a young adult</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="175f064e-9277-4f14-99ad-7386af96de4d" id="175f064e-9277-4f14-99ad-7386af96de4d" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 3″">quite squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="b7608f54-bd74-474e-91d2-a905dfe7afd5" id="b7608f54-bd74-474e-91d2-a905dfe7afd5" role="tooltip" title="210lbs. (with a BMI of 40)">morbidly obese</span>, and has brown eyes        and a well-loved beard, with ornamental beads woven into it,    with dark tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Orsik is that he has impossibly enormous hands. </p> <p>   Orsik blinks constantly.            He is      When he is relaxed, he is agreeable.  In moments of stress, he becomes angry.  Religion-wise, Orsik is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="2b113862-7c38-4c92-8f15-d0a3f873f1af" id="2b113862-7c38-4c92-8f15-d0a3f873f1af" role="tooltip" title="Orsik Silverstone is a casual follower of Artemis, and can be quite rude towards those who worship 'inferior' gods.">an open-minded seeker</span> of <a data-id="artemis" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal artemis" title="Artemis is the goddess of the Hunt and young girls. She can change others into animals as punishment for transgressions against her and she demands appropriate respect from mortals." href="#artemis">Artemis</a>.  <p>          Perhaps due to sexism,       Orsik has been unsuccessful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="f6862f86-c3ff-49d3-8f60-0a3f06aeb868" id="f6862f86-c3ff-49d3-8f60-0a3f06aeb868" role="tooltip" title="Derives their magical abilities through study.">wizard</span>, with a background of being a sage.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="4e9a9f27-9eab-44a0-93a4-ebce56f731cf" id="4e9a9f27-9eab-44a0-93a4-ebce56f731cf" role="tooltip" title="Orsik lives a comfortable life, filled with good food and wine">nobility</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Orsik currently has the cork from a wine bottle in his pockets,    and  6 Silver to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="c3492b51-086e-4701-85ad-9c543b873d49" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal c3492b51-086e-4701-85ad-9c543b873d49" title="Pope Street is a rather wide gravel and hewn rock street. It is a loose gravel that was taken from a river bed. There's a wagon with a cracked wheel by the side of the road. " href="#c3492b51-086e-4701-85ad-9c543b873d49">Pope Street</a>.               Orsik knows Common and Dwarvish.           </p> <section>Orsik currently earns 2 Gold 5 Silver 7 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>3 Gold 6 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 6 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>2 Gold 5 Silver 7 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="14e7d7e4-9b39-459b-a2e0-1c218910dc33" id="14e7d7e4-9b39-459b-a2e0-1c218910dc33" role="tooltip" title="Orsik lives a comfortable life, filled with good food and wine">comfortable</span>)</td><td>2 Gold 9 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 3 Silver 5 Copper</td></tr>          <tr><td>Money owed to <a data-id="5ca415fa-a639-46de-b169-7709a836966e" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 5ca415fa-a639-46de-b169-7709a836966e" title="A dwarf with a dreadful beard called Vistra Deepdelver who is a squatter." href="#5ca415fa-a639-46de-b169-7709a836966e">Vistra Deepdelver</a></td><td>107 Gold 1 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by my mother and father as an only child. I had a comfortable upbringing in a small house.  I had several friends, and my childhood was generally a happy one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a wizard</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I was always an avid reader, and became a sage to learn more from the thousands of books that I tended to. <h2>Taklinn Ironfist</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /tæklɪn aɪɝnfʌst /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="d30e76cd-2bc7-475b-a9bb-95ba914a70a6">          <span class="first-character">T</span>aklinn Ironfist    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="757f61f0-9e95-4d07-9d6e-e30e54256951" id="757f61f0-9e95-4d07-9d6e-e30e54256951" role="tooltip" title="123 years old, to be exact.">a middle aged</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="21ffbb52-5f68-47d3-8422-5adb7e7416c8" id="21ffbb52-5f68-47d3-8422-5adb7e7416c8" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 5″">somewhat squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="11ea9956-b7a8-429a-bfcd-7c515dab7a5f" id="11ea9956-b7a8-429a-bfcd-7c515dab7a5f" role="tooltip" title="238lbs. (with a BMI of 42)">unbelievably large</span>, and has hazel eyes        and a long, luxurious beard,    with pale skin.    The most notable physical trait of Taklinn is that he has wild, unkempt hair. </p> <p>   Taklinn exaggerates details.         He speaks in such a way that all L-sounds become w-sounds.            He is slothful.     When he is relaxed, he is lazy.  In moments of stress, he becomes courageous.  Religion-wise, Taklinn is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="0956ebd7-b7fc-4d86-957b-af0748e940ef" id="0956ebd7-b7fc-4d86-957b-af0748e940ef" role="tooltip" title="Taklinn Ironfist is usually a quiet follower of Apollo, but can be quite rude to anyone who criticizes his choice of deity.">a casual observer</span> of <a data-id="apollo" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal apollo" title="The twin brother of Artemis, Apollo is the inventor of music. Those that he loves and loses or those that he hates can find themselves transformed and immortalised as a part of nature. " href="#apollo">Apollo</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against him,         Taklinn is currently successful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="e4e63ea8-3c1e-4275-8f5f-788b5493ff39" id="e4e63ea8-3c1e-4275-8f5f-788b5493ff39" role="tooltip" title="A common warrior.">fighter</span>, with a background of being a soldier.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="0e63ce3b-d0d4-450c-abd5-5ab13b8bf285" id="0e63ce3b-d0d4-450c-abd5-5ab13b8bf285" role="tooltip" title="Taklinn lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Taklinn currently has a pouch full of dried berries in his pockets,    and 40 Gold 5 Silver 2 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716" title="Main Street is a path-sized gravel and hewn rock street. It is a loose gravel that was taken from a river bed. There are rows of potted plants and herbs, the produce of which people are free to pick at their leisure. " href="#2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716">Main Street</a>.               Taklinn knows Common and Dwarvish.               He prefers the same gender, but sometimes finds other genders attractive           </p> <section>Taklinn currently earns 1 Gold 8 Silver 2 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>2 Gold 4 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 8 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="143f338f-da33-4803-9aaa-747b0064386b" id="143f338f-da33-4803-9aaa-747b0064386b" role="tooltip" title="Taklinn lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 5 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td> 3 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born on a wagon, and was raised by my extended family, along with my 2 siblings. I had a comfortable upbringing in an apartment in a rundown neighborhood.  I had several friends, and my childhood was generally a happy one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a fighter</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I was forced to enlist in the local militia to fight for my lord. Many of my friends are dead because of him. Monster attacks led me to believe that there was no other way for me to be able to defend my family. I would lay down my life for the people I served with. Our lot is to lay down our lives in defense of others."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I shook the hand of a passing <a data-id="3b7fc58c-a2e6-42e9-a139-bf4111fdfd1f" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 3b7fc58c-a2e6-42e9-a139-bf4111fdfd1f" title="An adult woman with a spade of a chin called Sora Gygazzylyshrift who is a peasant." href="#3b7fc58c-a2e6-42e9-a139-bf4111fdfd1f">noble</a>. If I recall their handshake was strong and commanding. I'll always remember the time I met a well known armorer while on a long journey. I'll always remember the time I once had my home destroyed by warlocks. After that, I once found a cursed book. The book turned the reader blind.I forget exactly when, but at one point, to pay off a debt, I spent some time as a fighter. I'll always remember the time I met a <a data-id="8a286d9f-f9e8-4e2d-a441-b90c18011f5b" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 8a286d9f-f9e8-4e2d-a441-b90c18011f5b" title="A somewhat tiny male dwarf with a dragon tattoo called Travok Gorunn who is a peasant." href="#8a286d9f-f9e8-4e2d-a441-b90c18011f5b">man</a>, and we played cards. He decided that I was cheating- I'll freely admit that I'm to blame. I'm still on the lookout for him to this very day. One time I made an <a data-id="8c7d621b-4b96-4dc1-ab01-440ac1f24909" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 8c7d621b-4b96-4dc1-ab01-440ac1f24909" title="A mid thirties man with a spider web tattoo called Gardain Eversharp who is a peasant." href="#8c7d621b-4b96-4dc1-ab01-440ac1f24909">enemy</a> for life in my travels- I'm not quite sure what happened. I couldn't care less if he tries to do anything about it.  At one point, I saw the carriage of a <a data-id="8617689b-cccc-4c5b-bfcf-e61efd791dfe" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 8617689b-cccc-4c5b-bfcf-e61efd791dfe" title="A short-ish draconian man called Heskan Turnuroth who is a peasant." href="#8617689b-cccc-4c5b-bfcf-e61efd791dfe">noble</a> while traveling, and it was being cheered on by the adoring townsfolk.</div></details>  <div <h2>Kilvar Torunn</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /kɪlvɹ tɔɹʌn /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="90fc56a8-d234-4b2f-8b79-485c7a44e743">          <span class="first-character">K</span>ilvar Torunn    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="e8e34c2a-f263-47df-8719-631a9e019589" id="e8e34c2a-f263-47df-8719-631a9e019589" role="tooltip" title="120 years old, to be exact.">a middle aged</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="7bfbebdc-4251-4815-a8e0-d368be6c940b" id="7bfbebdc-4251-4815-a8e0-d368be6c940b" role="tooltip" title="4ft. ">somewhat tiny</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="9e0ff7c4-a618-48ce-8dd5-2b85372e19d7" id="9e0ff7c4-a618-48ce-8dd5-2b85372e19d7" role="tooltip" title="177lbs. (with a BMI of 38)">built like a brick shithouse</span>, and has gray eyes        and a well-groomed beard going down to his chest,    with light tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Kilvar is that he has a very narrow waist. </p> <p>   Kilvar eats too much.            He is indulgent and prudent.     When he is relaxed, he is weak-willed.  In moments of stress, he becomes practical.  Religion-wise, Kilvar is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="2187eae4-4012-46e4-836c-224daea2fbfe" id="2187eae4-4012-46e4-836c-224daea2fbfe" role="tooltip" title="Kilvar Torunn is a quiet follower of Zeus, and is not shy about criticizing followers of other gods.">a casual observer</span> of <a data-id="zeus" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal zeus" title="Zeus is the leader of the Greek gods, and lives atop Mount Olympus, where he rules over the mortal world below." href="#zeus">Zeus</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against him,         Kilvar is successful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="a5ae54f8-6212-43c7-b969-c7a57118000e" id="a5ae54f8-6212-43c7-b969-c7a57118000e" role="tooltip" title="A peasant.">peasant</span>, with a background of being a noble.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="9fafec85-adc2-480f-a8ef-ae518461167f" id="9fafec85-adc2-480f-a8ef-ae518461167f" role="tooltip" title="Kilvar lives a squalid existence, eating terrible food with no alcohol, and few creature comforts">peasantry</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Kilvar currently has a box of candles in his pockets,    and 80 Gold 7 Silver 9 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403" title="Gunnloa Street is a narrow gravel and hewn rock street. It is made of poorly packed gravel, which shifts around under foot. Grated storm drains at regular intervals grant access to the sewer system. It has been named after Gunnloa Durthane, who was a much beloved prostitute, one of whose clients bought the road as a thankyou." href="#03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403">Gunnloa Street</a>.               Kilvar knows Common and Dwarvish.           </p> <section>Kilvar currently earns  1 Silver 3 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td> 1 Silver 4 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 8.5 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td> 1 Silver 3 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="7f1386c8-7e25-4d92-8400-8c2c9f503d7f" id="7f1386c8-7e25-4d92-8400-8c2c9f503d7f" role="tooltip" title="Kilvar lives a squalid existence, eating terrible food with no alcohol, and few creature comforts">squalid</span>)</td><td> 1 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td> 2 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>    <p>     Has some jewellery.   </p>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born in the home of a friend, and was raised by my mother and father as an only child. <h2>Nurkara Deepdelver</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /nɝkɑɹʌ dipdɛlvɝ /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="00af63cc-6f90-4c19-9dd2-dcb1c4d2d38d">          <span class="first-character">N</span>urkara Deepdelver    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="6f893041-e8e7-4e15-8d1b-2423178f368d" id="6f893041-e8e7-4e15-8d1b-2423178f368d" role="tooltip" title="25 years old, to be exact.">a young adult</span> female dwarf.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="e5b6b8f8-a86b-4806-830d-25888ec3041b" id="e5b6b8f8-a86b-4806-830d-25888ec3041b" role="tooltip" title="4ft. ">somewhat tiny</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="2086bb8e-d193-4772-be89-8c05b679bb7c" id="2086bb8e-d193-4772-be89-8c05b679bb7c" role="tooltip" title="160lbs. (with a BMI of 34)">quite large</span>, and has dark brown eyes    with light tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Nurkara is that she has a youthful looking face. </p> <p>   Nurkara is often sarcastic.            She is bright and energetic.     When she is relaxed, she is eager.  In moments of stress, she becomes calculating.  Religion-wise, Nurkara is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="82d7bb65-b416-4218-8c44-1218740e92b9" id="82d7bb65-b416-4218-8c44-1218740e92b9" role="tooltip" title="Nurkara Deepdelver is a casual follower of Hermes, and she likes to provoke heated 'debates' with people who follow other religions.">a cautious listener</span> of <a data-id="hermes" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal hermes" title="Hermes is the hessenger of the gods and the personal messenger of Zeus. He brings the souls of the deceased to the edge of the underworld, where they are ferried deeper by the Cthonic gods" href="#hermes">Hermes</a>.  <p>          Perhaps due to sexism,       Nurkara has recently been somewhat unsuccessful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="9c7bdaa3-da39-4f76-bcc5-b946a0e11d39" id="9c7bdaa3-da39-4f76-bcc5-b946a0e11d39" role="tooltip" title="Controls a network of persons involved in the illegal drugs trade and transactions.">drug lord</span>, with a background of being a hermit.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="2f28d720-8af8-4203-b6d3-59f5cc7a8f56" id="2f28d720-8af8-4203-b6d3-59f5cc7a8f56" role="tooltip" title="Nurkara lives a comfortable life, filled with good food and wine">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Nurkara currently has map of the local area in her pockets,    and  2 Silver to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="36400128-f336-4c8e-9072-030ddab0d4a1" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 36400128-f336-4c8e-9072-030ddab0d4a1" title="Duke Road is a wide paved rock road. <h2>Marastyr Burrowfound</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /mɑɹæstɹ bɝoʊfaʊnd /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="c3cb6fb4-8eca-4b11-8926-9e28e81d858d">          <span class="first-character">M</span>arastyr Burrowfound    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="8778040a-7947-4a3f-aed4-2c12c189891f" id="8778040a-7947-4a3f-aed4-2c12c189891f" role="tooltip" title="38 years old, to be exact.">an adult</span> female dwarf.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="629e2784-9458-486f-bb59-78926406bcde" id="629e2784-9458-486f-bb59-78926406bcde" role="tooltip" title="3ft. 9″">rather small</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="c59bbe31-30ba-4404-a674-96d52ce7cce8" id="c59bbe31-30ba-4404-a674-96d52ce7cce8" role="tooltip" title="128lbs. (with a BMI of 31)">obese</span>, and has aqua eyes        and a dreadful beard,    with tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Marastyr is that she has a weak chin. </p> <p>   Marastyr bobs head back and forth when speaking.            She is prudent and narcissistic.     When she is relaxed, she is boastful.  In moments of stress, she becomes practical.  Religion-wise, Marastyr is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="57bff0a6-4e7f-4beb-a38c-a7fbc0f44561" id="57bff0a6-4e7f-4beb-a38c-a7fbc0f44561" role="tooltip" title="Marastyr Burrowfound is a casual follower of Athena, and can be quite rude towards those who worship 'inferior' gods.">an open-minded seeker</span> of <a data-id="athena" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal athena" title="Athena is a wise goddess and protects those that follow her. She does have the rage of a goddess, and affronts to her are paid back with divine retribution." href="#athena">Athena</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against her,         Marastyr is currently having mild success as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="9fca5abc-b4d5-4555-bc11-181c56af635e" id="9fca5abc-b4d5-4555-bc11-181c56af635e" role="tooltip" title="Sells and trades goods.">merchant</span>, with a background of being a commoner.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="8019445b-d9ff-4bb5-9192-d8d593d7ad1c" id="8019445b-d9ff-4bb5-9192-d8d593d7ad1c" role="tooltip" title="Marastyr lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Marastyr currently has a lead amulet in her pockets,    and  5 Silver 3 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="ed6d7af5-caa3-499d-a759-3d4b334f931f" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal ed6d7af5-caa3-499d-a759-3d4b334f931f" title="Thrahak Road is a rather wide gravel and hewn rock road. It is made of colourful rocks and pebbles. There is a large rock to the side of the road. The name comes from the Thrahak family who wield an amount of political power." href="#ed6d7af5-caa3-499d-a759-3d4b334f931f">Thrahak Road</a>.               Marastyr knows Common and Dwarvish.               She predominantly prefers other genders, but sometimes finds the same gender attractive            , and has a husband, <a data-id="49c88e6a-15b1-40a6-8a8e-92a59a9b141a" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 49c88e6a-15b1-40a6-8a8e-92a59a9b141a" title="A dwarf with a long, well-kempt beard called Harbek Aranore who is a drug lord." href="#49c88e6a-15b1-40a6-8a8e-92a59a9b141a">Harbek Aranore</a>.           </p> <section>Marastyr currently earns 1 Gold 9 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 9 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="7ee0a334-9dfe-4348-ae2a-0f5de6a90441" id="7ee0a334-9dfe-4348-ae2a-0f5de6a90441" role="tooltip" title="Marastyr lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>          <tr><td>Money owed to <a data-id="00af63cc-6f90-4c19-9dd2-dcb1c4d2d38d" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 00af63cc-6f90-4c19-9dd2-dcb1c4d2d38d" title="A young adult woman with a youthful looking face called Nurkara Deepdelver who is a drug lord." href="#00af63cc-6f90-4c19-9dd2-dcb1c4d2d38d">Nurkara Deepdelver</a></td><td>27 Gold 6 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by my mother and father with my brother. I had a modest upbringing in a large house.  I had several friends, and my childhood was generally a happy one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a merchant</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I was born into a lowly family, and that's where I'll likely stay. I grew up poor. I learnt to hock stuff off to feed myself. My lord raised the taxes to absurd levels so he could conscript people as punishment. I broke into my lord's manor one night, took a string of pearls, and sold it. I'll never forget that thrill. The low are lifted up"</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I won honorable mention at a garden tournament for my giant hydrangeas. At one point, while I was journeying through a field of lavender, I caught sight of a shimmering dragon! I got close enough to touch it.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr>       <th>Name</th>       <th>Race</th> <h2>Pynelope Pitt</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /paɪnɛloʊp pɪt /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="28d514fc-8a4c-46f6-a3f0-927bf25d0150">          <span class="first-character">P</span>ynelope Pitt    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="4222659e-eb4a-4423-9317-0bbcb86f6b0c" id="4222659e-eb4a-4423-9317-0bbcb86f6b0c" role="tooltip" title="25 years old, to be exact.">a prime adult aged</span> female human.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="3bc309b9-19f5-4fb9-99d8-d17c75f27334" id="3bc309b9-19f5-4fb9-99d8-d17c75f27334" role="tooltip" title="5ft. 4″">short</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="e37895fa-f129-425c-ba9a-0a51c7e4868c" id="e37895fa-f129-425c-ba9a-0a51c7e4868c" role="tooltip" title="129lbs. (with a BMI of 22)">lean</span>, and has blue eyes    with light skin.    The most notable physical trait of Pynelope is that she has a sharp chin. </p> <p>   Pynelope cannot stop staring at you.            She is energetic.     When she is relaxed, she is driven.  In moments of stress, she becomes industrious.  Religion-wise, Pynelope is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="3101d483-a1ac-43ab-8bcb-efd9dc956df9" id="3101d483-a1ac-43ab-8bcb-efd9dc956df9" role="tooltip" title="Pynelope Pitt is usually a quiet follower of Athena, but can be quite rude to anyone who criticizes her choice of deity.">a quiet true believer</span> of <a data-id="athena" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal athena" title="Athena is a wise goddess and protects those that follow her. She does have the rage of a goddess, and affronts to her are paid back with divine retribution." href="#athena">Athena</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against her,         Pynelope is having reasonable success as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="54571447-787c-415f-a331-f7a05e1a9499" id="54571447-787c-415f-a331-f7a05e1a9499" role="tooltip" title="Sells and trades goods.">merchant</span>, with a background of being a charlatan.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="b2c506a1-15de-4cef-9c06-7c6ca7b24bd1" id="b2c506a1-15de-4cef-9c06-7c6ca7b24bd1" role="tooltip" title="Pynelope lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Pynelope currently has a worn leather strap in her pockets,    and 30 Gold 7 Silver 7 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="ab084fd0-08e9-4d0e-a2e4-320e42f6e9a3" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal ab084fd0-08e9-4d0e-a2e4-320e42f6e9a3" title="Autumn Street is a wide gravel and hewn rock street. It is a loose gravel that was taken from a river bed. There's a bench on the side of the road, with the wood being smoothed out from many sittings. " href="#ab084fd0-08e9-4d0e-a2e4-320e42f6e9a3">Autumn Street</a>.                     She predominantly prefers the same gender, but finds other genders attractive           </p> <section>Pynelope currently earns 1 Gold 9 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 9 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="3d3a34ac-e2df-4820-bf0b-a385022d485b" id="3d3a34ac-e2df-4820-bf0b-a385022d485b" role="tooltip" title="Pynelope lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by my mother and father, along with my 5 siblings. I had a comfortable upbringing in a rundown shack.  I had several friends, and my childhood was generally a happy one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a merchant</summary> <div class="descriptive">"After a charlatan fleeced my family, I decided to learn all the tricks I could so I would never fall for another scam. Some people just have the gift of the gab- I have a talent for sales. I swindled and ruined a person who didn't deserve it, and now I seek to atone for my misdeeds but might never be able to forgive myself. I'm determined to make something of myself."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...When I was younger, some friends and I went to a flower festival where I saw some unusual bluebells. I think they won first place in the growers competition. Later in my life, for a while I did some work as a merchant.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr>       <th>Name</th> <h2>Diesa Rumnaheim</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /disʌ ɹʌmnʌhaɪm /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="d22452e3-ff6e-4b75-9e15-83c776ddd8d7">          <span class="first-character">D</span>iesa Rumnaheim    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="4ffa520a-e92f-495d-bedc-581b6b4b3362" id="4ffa520a-e92f-495d-bedc-581b6b4b3362" role="tooltip" title="37 years old, to be exact.">an adult</span> female dwarf.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="08ca0cf7-8a24-49c3-bb72-373d1e5a6735" id="08ca0cf7-8a24-49c3-bb72-373d1e5a6735" role="tooltip" title="3ft. 9″">rather small</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="3defcc7e-a7ef-4d48-9615-92f6b6e182d9" id="3defcc7e-a7ef-4d48-9615-92f6b6e182d9" role="tooltip" title="134lbs. (with a BMI of 33)">quite solidly built</span>, and has brown eyes    with light tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Diesa is that she has a long, horselike face. </p> <p>   Diesa is a habitual liar.            She is fair.     When she is relaxed, she is loyal.  In moments of stress, she becomes caustic.  Religion-wise, Diesa is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="2720e5b6-0293-432e-afd2-d1b23928daf1" id="2720e5b6-0293-432e-afd2-d1b23928daf1" role="tooltip" title="Diesa Rumnaheim is a casual follower of Demeter, and can be quite rude towards those who worship 'inferior' gods.">a cautious listener</span> of <a data-id="demeter" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal demeter" title="Demeter is the goddess of Agriculture - her favour promised a bountiful harvest and more grain then could be eaten. However her anger promised frosts and famine." href="#demeter">Demeter</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against her,         Diesa has recently had mild success as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="72652fa4-fb13-4624-b2cb-70fd07ab7e39" id="72652fa4-fb13-4624-b2cb-70fd07ab7e39" role="tooltip" title="Sells and trades goods.">merchant</span>, with a background of being a commoner.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="61033649-bbef-4071-8509-c442f30e3d3f" id="61033649-bbef-4071-8509-c442f30e3d3f" role="tooltip" title="Diesa lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Diesa currently has a palm-sized glass sphere in her pockets,    and 70 Gold 3 Silver 2 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716" title="Main Street is a path-sized gravel and hewn rock street. It is a loose gravel that was taken from a river bed. There are rows of potted plants and herbs, the produce of which people are free to pick at their leisure. " href="#2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716">Main Street</a>.               Diesa knows Common and Dwarvish.                 Diesa has a husband, <a data-id="0ecb8a0d-da3b-4d9e-bb61-3df5447a8298" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 0ecb8a0d-da3b-4d9e-bb61-3df5447a8298" title="An early middle aged man with a dimpled nose called Oskar Burrowfound who is a peasant." href="#0ecb8a0d-da3b-4d9e-bb61-3df5447a8298">Oskar Burrowfound</a>.    </p> <section>Diesa currently earns 1 Gold 9 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 9 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="40632172-d65d-4773-9429-b15e6d3a96b7" id="40632172-d65d-4773-9429-b15e6d3a96b7" role="tooltip" title="Diesa lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born among people of a different race, and was raised by my mother and father as an only child. I had a comfortable upbringing in a mansion.  I had several friends, and my childhood was generally a happy one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a merchant</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I was a soldier in the army, with a lot of potential. But then, I made a tactical mistake, which led to my dismissal. I grew up poor. I learnt to hock stuff off to feed myself. I was a farmer, got conscripted, went off to war, and came back broken. I want my grandchildren to have peaceful lives. The low are lifted up"</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I was part of a,I played in a,I was in a pretty unpopular band for a short time. The band only ever played on the open streets. There was a pretty nasty zombie outbreak which I had to defend my town against. I suffered only minor injuries, and the wounds all healed without leaving any scars.After that, I met the love of my life, [object Object]. At one point, there was no other work so for a while I was a commoner.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr>       <th>Name</th>       <th>Race</th>       <th>Occupation</th>       <th>Relationship</th>            </tr>          <tr>       <td><a data-id="0ecb8a0d-da3b-4d9e-bb61-3df5447a8298" href="#0ecb8a0d-da3b-4d9e-bb61-3df5447a8298">Oskar Burrowfound</a></td>       <td>Dwarf</td>       <td><span class="tip dotted" data-id="ee4b8699-3d76-41bc-a663-d4343582e7ca" <h2>Oskar Foamtankard</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /oʊskɑɹ foʊmtæŋkɝd /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="98a206db-8a47-4bb8-a34d-dde7b66c8eb3">          <span class="first-character">O</span>skar Foamtankard    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="e22ee9c1-5ff6-42c4-a80a-6941cdb1c377" id="e22ee9c1-5ff6-42c4-a80a-6941cdb1c377" role="tooltip" title="32 years old, to be exact.">an earlyish thirties</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="dbf8bac9-a93b-4eb2-8a1c-54b48cb95517" id="dbf8bac9-a93b-4eb2-8a1c-54b48cb95517" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 2″">rather squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="610aa08e-320c-4a75-a9fc-dc745b4baed0" id="610aa08e-320c-4a75-a9fc-dc745b4baed0" role="tooltip" title="185lbs. (with a BMI of 37)">quite large</span>, and has brown eyes        and a well-groomed beard going down to his chest,    with fair skin.    The most notable physical trait of Oskar is that he has a square chin. </p> <p>   Oskar paces about incessantly.            He is fearless and modest.     When he is relaxed, he is agreeable.  In moments of stress, he becomes courageous.  Religion-wise, Oskar is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="3b7afc02-1e20-4ef0-a150-64d54ef7df71" id="3b7afc02-1e20-4ef0-a150-64d54ef7df71" role="tooltip" title="Oskar Foamtankard is a casual follower of Zeus, and can be quite rude towards those who worship 'inferior' gods.">a cautious listener</span> of <a data-id="zeus" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal zeus" title="Zeus is the leader of the Greek gods, and lives atop Mount Olympus, where he rules over the mortal world below." href="#zeus">Zeus</a>.  <p>          Perhaps due to sexism,       Oskar is a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="44ca5e2f-721d-4d22-aebe-657eda88307e" id="44ca5e2f-721d-4d22-aebe-657eda88307e" role="tooltip" title="Sells and trades goods.">merchant</span>, with a background of being a charlatan.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="bd25d431-25e6-4ede-9c39-4c5436c14580" id="bd25d431-25e6-4ede-9c39-4c5436c14580" role="tooltip" title="Oskar lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Oskar currently has a clove of garlic in his pockets,    and 80 Gold 4 Silver 1 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716" title="Main Street is a path-sized gravel and hewn rock street. It is a loose gravel that was taken from a river bed. There are rows of potted plants and herbs, the produce of which people are free to pick at their leisure. " href="#2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716">Main Street</a>.               Oskar knows Common and Dwarvish.               He bisexual            , and has a wife, <a data-id="d090e66a-aff9-4c77-8b6f-c5b5ceb8f6a7" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal d090e66a-aff9-4c77-8b6f-c5b5ceb8f6a7" title="A rather squat dwarven woman called Orifi Dankil who is a fighter." href="#d090e66a-aff9-4c77-8b6f-c5b5ceb8f6a7">Orifi Dankil</a>.           </p> <section>Oskar currently earns 1 Gold 9 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 9 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="1b04cfc5-58bd-40cc-b232-9a4f04e5164f" id="1b04cfc5-58bd-40cc-b232-9a4f04e5164f" role="tooltip" title="Oskar lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born in a field, and was raised by my maternal grandparents as an only child. I had a modest upbringing in a very impressive house.  I had a few close friends, and my childhood was a relatively normal one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a merchant</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I learned early on that people are easy to exploit, and are gullible and too trusting. I grew up poor. I learnt to hock stuff off to feed myself. Somewhere out there I have a child, litte Bastyen, who doesn't know me. I'm going to try and make the world better for him. I am a free spirit– no one tells me what to do."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I came across a horde of ghouls feasting on a dead body in my youth. How could I ever forget the time I had a brief stint working for a famous rogue during one of my youthful adventures.  At one point, I worked as a merchant.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr>       <th>Name</th>       <th>Race</th> <h2>Olunt Loderr</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /oʊlʌnt loʊdɹ /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="b5f63f8e-9591-4158-913d-66b33e3cc005">          <span class="first-character">O</span>lunt Loderr    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="3ca0d7ea-0eda-486f-8f55-7f25362250b9" id="3ca0d7ea-0eda-486f-8f55-7f25362250b9" role="tooltip" title="141 years old, to be exact.">an old</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="9a26df80-ed4f-4ac1-a576-e2ce6a00f075" id="9a26df80-ed4f-4ac1-a576-e2ce6a00f075" role="tooltip" title="3ft. 11″">somewhat tiny</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="ff347531-9d99-44cc-be24-b69bba65cdcf" id="ff347531-9d99-44cc-be24-b69bba65cdcf" role="tooltip" title="166lbs. (with a BMI of 37)">built like a wrestler</span>, and has gray eyes        and a scraggly beard,    with tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Olunt is that he has hair greased into a ducktail. </p> <p>   Olunt makes poor eye contact.            He is controlled and sober.     When he is relaxed, he is reserved.  In moments of stress, he becomes pushy.  Religion-wise, Olunt is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="c84b091e-1c1c-4542-af08-94f2098ab631" id="c84b091e-1c1c-4542-af08-94f2098ab631" role="tooltip" title="Olunt Loderr is critical of religion, but is nominally a follower of Poseidon. Because of his doubts, he enjoys spirited debates about the flaws of various religions – both other peoples' faiths and his own.">a cautious listener</span> of <a data-id="poseidon" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal poseidon" title="Poseidon is the god of the Sea - all things underwater are under his purview" href="#poseidon">Poseidon</a>.  <p>          Perhaps due to sexism,       Olunt is a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="a7082c7b-b7b1-495c-a551-cc1008ca5bcf" id="a7082c7b-b7b1-495c-a551-cc1008ca5bcf" role="tooltip" title="Sells and trades goods.">merchant</span>, with a background of being a commoner.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="72e548c7-919b-48d3-ae50-38c3b935f491" id="72e548c7-919b-48d3-ae50-38c3b935f491" role="tooltip" title="Olunt lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Olunt currently has a lead amulet in his pockets,    and 100 Gold 3 Silver 2 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="ab084fd0-08e9-4d0e-a2e4-320e42f6e9a3" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal ab084fd0-08e9-4d0e-a2e4-320e42f6e9a3" title="Autumn Street is a wide gravel and hewn rock street. It is a loose gravel that was taken from a river bed. There's a bench on the side of the road, with the wood being smoothed out from many sittings. " href="#ab084fd0-08e9-4d0e-a2e4-320e42f6e9a3">Autumn Street</a>.               Olunt knows Common and Dwarvish.               He predominantly prefers other genders, but sometimes finds the same gender attractive            , and has a wife, <a data-id="605b492e-afc2-4e0e-8ee1-41f13ece781b" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 605b492e-afc2-4e0e-8ee1-41f13ece781b" title="A rather small woman with ears that curl like an exotic shell called Eridred Rumnaheim who is a peasant." href="#605b492e-afc2-4e0e-8ee1-41f13ece781b">Eridred Rumnaheim</a>.           </p> <section>Olunt currently earns 1 Gold 9 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 9 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="b46fbe90-e366-4f99-8610-34a3a74dd2fb" id="b46fbe90-e366-4f99-8610-34a3a74dd2fb" role="tooltip" title="Olunt lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born in a tower, and was raised by my single mother, along with my 2 siblings. I had a comfortable upbringing in a small house.  I had a few close friends, and my childhood was a relatively normal one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a merchant</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I was one of many children, and when I was old enough to work, my parents put me to it. I spent my youth selling whatever scraps I could find, never got tired of it. When my mother died, I found a list of men in her possessions. One of them is my father. I'll find him. The rich need to be shown what life and death are like in the gutters."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I spent some time working as a commoner. I forget exactly when, but at one point, I was nearly caught and convicted in the middle of murder, but managed to escape. They are still after me, though. You might not believe it, but I ventured out to see an upside-down castle in a desert where the dunes whisper secrets. I got to see that place, but it was not what I was truly looking for. I forget exactly when, but at one point, I once woke up miles away from my home- I don't know if it was due to drinking or some other, magical force at work, but I've sworn off the grog ever since. Oh, and I can't forget the time I won honorable mention at a garden tournament for my enormous pointsettias. One time there was a civil war within the town that I fought in. I suffered only minor injuries, and the wounds all healed without leaving any scars.  At one point, there was no other work so for a while I was a commoner.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr> <h2>Ilanis Firahel</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ɪlænɪs fɪɹʌhʌl /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="95e34511-f8db-42ba-909f-00760449a8e1">          <span class="first-character">I</span>lanis Firahel    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="0966df83-0cf0-465a-9cf0-7e3fd508f746" id="0966df83-0cf0-465a-9cf0-7e3fd508f746" role="tooltip" title="272 years old, to be exact.">a prime adult aged</span> female elf.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="8bad4567-91e6-4d13-9f1e-1c0f4cd39e42" id="8bad4567-91e6-4d13-9f1e-1c0f4cd39e42" role="tooltip" title="5ft. 9″">medium sized</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="2d1af656-a216-4929-ae7b-34ac1cfc39d6" id="2d1af656-a216-4929-ae7b-34ac1cfc39d6" role="tooltip" title="98lbs. (with a BMI of 14)">bony</span>, and has pale blue eyes    with light skin.    The most notable physical trait of Ilanis is that she has perfect posture. </p> <p>   Ilanis embellishes the truth.            She is cowardly.     When she is relaxed, she is mischeivous.  In moments of stress, she becomes cowardly.  Religion-wise, Ilanis is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="2fb9c04e-71b3-4853-990d-b1af290ce472" id="2fb9c04e-71b3-4853-990d-b1af290ce472" role="tooltip" title="Ilanis is a faithful follower of Hermes, and enjoys confronting others to challenge beliefs that differ from her own.">a conspicuously faithful believer</span> of <a data-id="hermes" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal hermes" title="Hermes is the hessenger of the gods and the personal messenger of Zeus. He brings the souls of the deceased to the edge of the underworld, where they are ferried deeper by the Cthonic gods" href="#hermes">Hermes</a>.  <p>          Perhaps due to sexism,       Ilanis is a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="a9763ff4-1068-4eb4-99c5-44032c177b05" id="a9763ff4-1068-4eb4-99c5-44032c177b05" role="tooltip" title="Attacks and robs ships at sea.">pirate</span>, with a background of being a soldier.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="10d2cb19-83dc-4c5e-a5d2-44b0d8296616" id="10d2cb19-83dc-4c5e-a5d2-44b0d8296616" role="tooltip" title="Ilanis lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">peasantry</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Ilanis currently has a pouch of ruby powder in her pockets,    and 60 Gold 3 Silver 6 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="d228384c-7090-4096-9e5d-cc40b0ca71dc" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal d228384c-7090-4096-9e5d-cc40b0ca71dc" title="Baker Road is a path-sized gravel and hewn rock road. It is made of poorly packed gravel, which shifts around under foot. The road has the occasional pothole. " href="#d228384c-7090-4096-9e5d-cc40b0ca71dc">Baker Road</a>.               Ilanis knows Common and Elvish.               She prefers the same gender, but sometimes finds other genders attractive           </p> <section>Ilanis currently earns 1 Gold 8 Silver 7 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>2 Gold 4 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 8.5 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 8 Silver 7 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="b53958c7-ff5b-4c6f-a51e-fe6343159f03" id="b53958c7-ff5b-4c6f-a51e-fe6343159f03" role="tooltip" title="Ilanis lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 5 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td> 3 Silver 6 Copper</td></tr>               <tr><td>Money owed by <a data-id="3a606413-e3b1-4fa5-8213-57e3b2005600" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 3a606413-e3b1-4fa5-8213-57e3b2005600" title="A rather squat male dwarf with a long, thin scar running up the arm called Traubon Trollbleeder who is a merchant." href="#3a606413-e3b1-4fa5-8213-57e3b2005600">Traubon Trollbleeder</a></td><td>27 Gold 6 Copper</td></tr>      </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born in the home of a midwife, and was raised by my mother and father, along with my 5 siblings. I had a poor upbringing in a very impressive house.  Others saw me as different, or strange, and so I had few companions.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a pirate</summary> <div class="descriptive">"Invaders attacked my village, and I vowed to never let my family be unprotected again, so I picked up the sword. I'm working as a pirate. The work is alright, though it can be a bit tedious I would lay down my life for the people I served with. Our lot is to lay down our lives in defense of others."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I worked as a soldier. I'll always remember the time I once saw a true miracle. A man stumbled into town claiming to be sent from a god and told us we were being blessed, but some thought this to be blasphemy. For the next year we had a huge economic boom in our town. After that, I was nearly caught and convicted in the middle of arson, but managed to escape. They are still after me, though.At one point I met a <a data-id="770c7060-b7e7-43e4-8ae7-3ebebc6af0a5" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 770c7060-b7e7-43e4-8ae7-3ebebc6af0a5" title="A quite squat dwarven man called Nalral Trollbleeder who is a peasant." href="#770c7060-b7e7-43e4-8ae7-3ebebc6af0a5">man</a>, and we played cards. He decided that I was cheating- I'll freely admit that I'm to blame. I couldn't care less if he tries to do anything about it.  At one point, I once found a cursed book. The book retold the reader's life but with a horrible twist ending.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr>
