<h2>Traubon Trollbleeder</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /tɹɔbɑn tɹoʊlblidɝ /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="3a606413-e3b1-4fa5-8213-57e3b2005600">          <span class="first-character">T</span>raubon Trollbleeder    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="198326f4-9498-4f68-af28-2c7d898bb591" id="198326f4-9498-4f68-af28-2c7d898bb591" role="tooltip" title="300 years old, to be exact.">an ancient</span> male dwarf.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="c59aa057-a1d0-4e10-b472-64015cbc2400" id="c59aa057-a1d0-4e10-b472-64015cbc2400" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 1″">rather squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="15ef12b4-510e-4f08-b1d5-f333dd9aa5a5" id="15ef12b4-510e-4f08-b1d5-f333dd9aa5a5" role="tooltip" title="182lbs. (with a BMI of 37)">built like a wrestler</span>, and has dark brown eyes        and a rather wild, unkempt beard,    with dark tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Traubon is that he has a chunk of left ear missing. </p> <p>   Traubon is a know it all.            He is merciless and narcissistic.     When he is relaxed, he is boastful.  In moments of stress, he becomes manipulative.  Religion-wise, Traubon is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="25c237f8-ac3a-4f64-9638-35014439e70b" id="25c237f8-ac3a-4f64-9638-35014439e70b" role="tooltip" title="Traubon Trollbleeder is a casual follower of Zeus, and he likes to provoke heated 'debates' with people who follow other religions.">a cautious listener</span> of <a data-id="zeus" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal zeus" title="Zeus is the leader of the Greek gods, and lives atop Mount Olympus, where he rules over the mortal world below." href="#zeus">Zeus</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against him,         Traubon is having mild success as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="5ce9ee72-9258-4e10-a2f9-1971cc7f382d" id="5ce9ee72-9258-4e10-a2f9-1971cc7f382d" role="tooltip" title="Sells and trades goods.">merchant</span>, with a background of being a noble.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="39bef88b-3536-429d-9412-e12be8f7ee48" id="39bef88b-3536-429d-9412-e12be8f7ee48" role="tooltip" title="Traubon lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Traubon currently has a box of candles in his pockets,    and 110 Gold 6 Silver 5 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="ebd5996d-85e2-420b-b1a8-1cb1ad0f6b08" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal ebd5996d-85e2-420b-b1a8-1cb1ad0f6b08" title="Common Crescent is a  gravel and hewn rock road. It is made of colourful rocks and pebbles. A row of houses and buildings is splayed out, with enough room for a horse and cart to turn around. " href="#ebd5996d-85e2-420b-b1a8-1cb1ad0f6b08">Common Crescent</a>.               Traubon knows Common and Dwarvish.               He predominantly prefers the same gender, but finds other genders attractive           </p> <section>Traubon currently earns 1 Gold 9 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 9 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="1dbb1e79-b459-4ea5-8698-d6e8a32f5462" id="1dbb1e79-b459-4ea5-8698-d6e8a32f5462" role="tooltip" title="Traubon lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>          <tr><td>Money owed to <a data-id="95e34511-f8db-42ba-909f-00760449a8e1" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 95e34511-f8db-42ba-909f-00760449a8e1" title="A prime adult aged elf with perfect posture called Ilanis Firahel who is a pirate." href="#95e34511-f8db-42ba-909f-00760449a8e1">Ilanis Firahel</a></td><td>27 Gold 6 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by the orphanage as an only child. I had a comfortable upbringing in an apartment in a rundown neighborhood. I didn't know my parents growing up. I had a few close friends, and my childhood was a relatively normal one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a merchant</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I hope to increase my family's power and influence. I love gold. Unashamedly, I really do. So what? Selling is an honest living. Sue me. Nothing is more important that the other members of my family. I believe that blood runs thicker than water."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I spent some time working as a merchant. How could I ever forget the time I was falsely accused of extortion, but eventually was acquitted. It took up years of my life, though, and I still get antsy around guards that I don't know. Once there was a minor skirmish with some orcs that I was involved with. I suffered some serious injuries, and had to be carried off the field. Once there was no other work so for a while I was a merchant. Not to mention there was the time On my bed I found a Conjurer's Scales of the Sentinel.<blockquote><h4>Conjurer's Scales of the Sentinel</h4>The bearer may cast Prestidigitation once per day. Faintly glows when creatures of a certain race (DMs choice) are within a 100 foot radius.</blockquote>I forget exactly when, but at one point, I went to celebrate at a festival. While I was there, I visited several brewing stalls and drank to my heart's content. At one point I made an <a data-id="e1880f50-cae9-4906-9ea1-3ecde9c704d6" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal e1880f50-cae9-4906-9ea1-3ecde9c704d6" title="An overweight draconian man called Kaladan Zzzxaaxthroth who is a peasant." href="#e1880f50-cae9-4906-9ea1-3ecde9c704d6">enemy</a> for life in my travels- I'm ashamed to admit that I'm to blame. That's all behind me now and I hope it stays that way.  At one point, I met the love of my life, who is no longer with me.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr> <h2>Bella Tallfellow</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /bɛlʌ tælfɛloʊ /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="dee762e4-7aea-4fb5-b473-6b2a1a133dd3">          <span class="first-character">B</span>ella Tallfellow    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="e065d76d-96dd-42f6-b822-5a9881837bf3" id="e065d76d-96dd-42f6-b822-5a9881837bf3" role="tooltip" title="86 years old, to be exact.">an old</span> female halfling.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="e98e30a5-0ab5-4169-bc46-d6f5cb013bb8" id="e98e30a5-0ab5-4169-bc46-d6f5cb013bb8" role="tooltip" title="3ft. ">quite diminutive</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="94376403-d59a-4b66-aef5-7ebc55c489d5" id="94376403-d59a-4b66-aef5-7ebc55c489d5" role="tooltip" title="31lbs. (with a BMI of 16)">scrawny</span>, and has red eyes    with light skin.    The most notable physical trait of Bella is that she has narrow shoulders. </p> <p>   Bella is skeptical of everything.            She is controlled and sober.     When she is relaxed, she is reserved.  In moments of stress, she becomes destructive.  Religion-wise, Bella is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="c64f0167-5a77-49f4-8b31-7b07efe1d976" id="c64f0167-5a77-49f4-8b31-7b07efe1d976" role="tooltip" title="Bella Tallfellow is a quiet follower of Demeter, and is not shy about criticizing followers of other gods.">a casual observer</span> of <a data-id="demeter" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal demeter" title="Demeter is the goddess of Agriculture - her favour promised a bountiful harvest and more grain then could be eaten. However her anger promised frosts and famine." href="#demeter">Demeter</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against her,         Bella has been having mild success as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="7c2fceb2-3932-47eb-b09c-ac9482544b60" id="7c2fceb2-3932-47eb-b09c-ac9482544b60" role="tooltip" title="A peasant.">peasant</span>, with a background of being an urchin.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="6c36e30f-8ccb-471d-bc57-2d192d1f6ac5" id="6c36e30f-8ccb-471d-bc57-2d192d1f6ac5" role="tooltip" title="Bella lives a squalid existence, eating terrible food with no alcohol, and few creature comforts">peasantry</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Bella currently has fragments of a shattered sword in her pockets,    and  4 Silver 1 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="d228384c-7090-4096-9e5d-cc40b0ca71dc" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal d228384c-7090-4096-9e5d-cc40b0ca71dc" title="Baker Road is a path-sized gravel and hewn rock road. It is made of poorly packed gravel, which shifts around under foot. The road has the occasional pothole. " href="#d228384c-7090-4096-9e5d-cc40b0ca71dc">Baker Road</a>.               Bella knows Common and Halfling.           </p> <section>Bella currently earns  1 Silver 3 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td> 1 Silver 4 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 8.5 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td> 1 Silver 3 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="7852115a-7ab3-490b-a7de-9d338619bca4" id="7852115a-7ab3-490b-a7de-9d338619bca4" role="tooltip" title="Bella lives a squalid existence, eating terrible food with no alcohol, and few creature comforts">squalid</span>)</td><td> 1 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td> 2 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born in a field, and was raised by my single father as an only child. I had a modest upbringing in a rundown shack.  I had a few close friends, and my childhood was a relatively normal one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a peasant</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I had to escape my homelife. I lived off crumbs and scraps, but it was better than the alternative. I'm on the upswing as a peasant. Things are looking better. I sponsor an orphanage to keep others from enduring what I was forced to endure. The low are lifted up, and we all benefit from that."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I used to play cards in a pub, and one time supposedly cheated a <a data-id="b76ced1d-2a6f-4785-98a4-24a24ef577c1" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal b76ced1d-2a6f-4785-98a4-24a24ef577c1" title="A somewhat tiny male dwarf called Beloril Bloodkith who is a peasant." href="#b76ced1d-2a6f-4785-98a4-24a24ef577c1">man</a> out of his winnings; I'm ashamed to admit that I'm to blame. I don't exactly care to run into him again. At one point I made an <a data-id="2617e12b-dea9-490a-ade2-7f9eb2718cf9" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 2617e12b-dea9-490a-ade2-7f9eb2718cf9" title="A light skinned bony halfling called Gilbert Strongbones who is a peasant." href="#2617e12b-dea9-490a-ade2-7f9eb2718cf9">enemy</a> for life in my travels- I admit that I am at least partially at fault. I'm afraid that he'll kill me in my sleep.  At one point, I worked under <a data-id="5e76c349-73d1-4f52-bbd6-25af3553ae07" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 5e76c349-73d1-4f52-bbd6-25af3553ae07" title="A rather squat male dwarf with a sharply angled face called Kildrak Bofdarm who is a weaponsmith." href="#5e76c349-73d1-4f52-bbd6-25af3553ae07">Kildrak Bofdarm</a> a rather unskilled weaponsmith. During that time I learned a lot about myself.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr>       <th>Name</th> <h2>Bardryn Glanhig</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /bɑɹdɹʌn ɡlænhɪɡ /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="76713025-f7aa-4e18-ad26-db4458a63cb4">          <span class="first-character">B</span>ardryn Glanhig    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="252134ce-371a-40a4-95a2-dc5e96ebd3ae" id="252134ce-371a-40a4-95a2-dc5e96ebd3ae" role="tooltip" title="26 years old, to be exact.">a young adult</span> female dwarf.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="fe1c2bfe-5cb4-4310-895c-550b0c03fef0" id="fe1c2bfe-5cb4-4310-895c-550b0c03fef0" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 2″">rather squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="a694d12d-6dd8-4150-ba59-dbe5f3020540" id="a694d12d-6dd8-4150-ba59-dbe5f3020540" role="tooltip" title="190lbs. (with a BMI of 38)">unbelievably large</span>, and has dark brown eyes        and a goatee that seems to be trying to level up into a beard,    with tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Bardryn is that she has elephant-like ears. </p> <p>   Bardryn swears often.            She is always doubting people.     When she is relaxed, she is assertive.  In moments of stress, she becomes courageous.  Religion-wise, Bardryn is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="74bb9e6e-fa66-4b91-a6f2-f167f50501ea" id="74bb9e6e-fa66-4b91-a6f2-f167f50501ea" role="tooltip" title="Bardryn Glanhig is a casual follower of Hera, and can be quite rude towards those who worship 'inferior' gods.">an open-minded seeker</span> of <a data-id="hera" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal hera" title="Hera is the Queen of the gods, forever tested by her husband Zeus. Unable to attack Zeus, her anger is often directed to his consorts or his children." href="#hera">Hera</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against her,         Bardryn is extremely successful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="bc43ea95-f207-4cab-b37e-c428f4f39646" id="bc43ea95-f207-4cab-b37e-c428f4f39646" role="tooltip" title="Held in confinement as a punishment for crimes they have been convicted of.">prisoner</span>, with a background of being a soldier.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="5eb9d121-b4c0-4b46-ab9f-447eb2747e63" id="5eb9d121-b4c0-4b46-ab9f-447eb2747e63" role="tooltip" title="Bardryn lives a wretched life of constant filth and misery. There is no respite to this poverty">paupery</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Bardryn currently has a vial of quicksilver in her pockets,    and 40 Gold 4 Silver 4 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403" title="Gunnloa Street is a narrow gravel and hewn rock street. It is made of poorly packed gravel, which shifts around under foot. Grated storm drains at regular intervals grant access to the sewer system. It has been named after Gunnloa Durthane, who was a much beloved prostitute, one of whose clients bought the road as a thankyou." href="#03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403">Gunnloa Street</a>. <h2>Helja Strongheart</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /hɛldʒʌ stɹɔŋɑɹt /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="95f81f4c-bdef-4b78-add8-e396cd25c06d">          <span class="first-character">H</span>elja Strongheart    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="def23bba-9544-43e9-83db-c592e6e1850d" id="def23bba-9544-43e9-83db-c592e6e1850d" role="tooltip" title="34 years old, to be exact.">a mid thirties</span> female dwarf.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="7c9ddf58-f5c6-41cc-922e-b5e70daa6548" id="7c9ddf58-f5c6-41cc-922e-b5e70daa6548" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 1″">rather squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="1c7ca703-5e28-4efd-9a19-62d416ba4e04" id="1c7ca703-5e28-4efd-9a19-62d416ba4e04" role="tooltip" title="162lbs. (with a BMI of 33)">rather round</span>, and has blue eyes    with fair skin.    The most notable physical trait of Helja is that she has thick, full lips. </p> <p>   Helja is always shaking.            She is blame-prone.     When she is relaxed, she is artistic.  In moments of stress, she becomes spiteful.  Religion-wise, Helja is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="4ef9b93e-c4c2-4d1e-a927-4017934dae11" id="4ef9b93e-c4c2-4d1e-a927-4017934dae11" role="tooltip" title="Helja Strongheart is a casual follower of Dionysus, and can be quite rude towards those who worship 'inferior' gods.">a cautious listener</span> of <a data-id="dionysus" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal dionysus" title="Dionysus is the god of Wine and Theatre, his revelry is open to all. However, he has his dark side - he is the god of madness the anger of Dionysus is a terrifying thing" href="#dionysus">Dionysus</a>.  <p>          Despite sexism against her,         Helja has been mildly successful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="06c95264-8f08-4a06-b571-b1cf2adbcdbd" id="06c95264-8f08-4a06-b571-b1cf2adbcdbd" role="tooltip" title="A pickpocket or thief.">cutpurse</span>, with a background of being a soldier.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="f0654bf5-da6f-43e0-9ae3-68664d5951f1" id="f0654bf5-da6f-43e0-9ae3-68664d5951f1" role="tooltip" title="Helja lives a poor life, having to count copper and save for purchases">peasantry</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Helja currently has a vial of quicksilver in her pockets,    and 110 Gold 5 Silver 2 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403" title="Gunnloa Street is a narrow gravel and hewn rock street. It is made of poorly packed gravel, which shifts around under foot. Grated storm drains at regular intervals grant access to the sewer system. It has been named after Gunnloa Durthane, who was a much beloved prostitute, one of whose clients bought the road as a thankyou." href="#03d053ff-d689-4773-92e6-d7098fd25403">Gunnloa Street</a>. <h2>Usk</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /ʌsk /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="32afd250-aeec-4703-81ea-04e2c7ce0678">          <span class="first-character">U</span>sk    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="401e892e-d9d7-4266-8947-dd4022fcd84b" id="401e892e-d9d7-4266-8947-dd4022fcd84b" role="tooltip" title="53 years old, to be exact.">an old</span> male lizardfolk.    He is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="a0c6ba1d-c8e1-4459-ae27-41e61d41f703" id="a0c6ba1d-c8e1-4459-ae27-41e61d41f703" role="tooltip" title="6ft. 2″">quite tall</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="1c08d0c3-b68a-4bfb-a221-57fc6cf49db1" id="1c08d0c3-b68a-4bfb-a221-57fc6cf49db1" role="tooltip" title="282lbs. (with a BMI of 30)">quite fat</span>, and has yellow eyes    with light tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Usk is that he has long, spindly fingers. </p> <p>   Usk is a know it all.        When he is relaxed, he is fearful.  In moments of stress, he becomes impractical.  Religion-wise, Usk is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="97901a36-fe8f-4a37-837e-f655de42cbc8" id="97901a36-fe8f-4a37-837e-f655de42cbc8" role="tooltip" title="Usk is a casual follower of Apollo, and he likes to provoke heated 'debates' with people who follow other religions.">an open-minded seeker</span> of <a data-id="apollo" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal apollo" title="The twin brother of Artemis, Apollo is the inventor of music. Those that he loves and loses or those that he hates can find themselves transformed and immortalised as a part of nature. " href="#apollo">Apollo</a>.  <p>          Perhaps due to sexism,       Usk is a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="e97c0de1-c363-46f4-9097-cd4305247acb" id="e97c0de1-c363-46f4-9097-cd4305247acb" role="tooltip" title="A sneaky person.">rogue</span>, with a background of being a criminal.         He belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="7accfd99-a316-4321-8f9c-c14eea071f84" id="7accfd99-a316-4321-8f9c-c14eea071f84" role="tooltip" title="Usk lives a comfortable life, filled with good food and wine">commoner</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Usk currently has a flask full of salt water in his pockets,    and 110 Gold 7 Silver 9 Copper to his name.        He lives on <a data-id="2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal 2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716" title="Main Street is a path-sized gravel and hewn rock street. It is a loose gravel that was taken from a river bed. There are rows of potted plants and herbs, the produce of which people are free to pick at their leisure. " href="#2e0d421b-79c2-404a-ad9e-905677350716">Main Street</a>.               Usk knows Common and Draconic.               He bisexual           </p> <section>Usk currently earns 2 Gold 2 Silver 7 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>2 Gold 5 Silver 5 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 1 Silver 1 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>2 Gold 2 Silver 7 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="aebaba0b-e75c-4d2a-b727-dbced17ce37b" id="aebaba0b-e75c-4d2a-b727-dbced17ce37b" role="tooltip" title="Usk lives a comfortable life, filled with good food and wine">comfortable</span>)</td><td>2 Gold 7 Silver 7 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 5 Silver</td></tr>          <tr><td>Money owed to <a data-id="76713025-f7aa-4e18-ad26-db4458a63cb4" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 76713025-f7aa-4e18-ad26-db4458a63cb4" title="A young adult woman with elephant-like ears called Bardryn Glanhig who is a prisoner." href="#76713025-f7aa-4e18-ad26-db4458a63cb4">Bardryn Glanhig</a></td><td>13 Gold 1 Copper</td></tr>          <tr><td>Money owed to <a data-id="95f81f4c-bdef-4b78-add8-e396cd25c06d" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 95f81f4c-bdef-4b78-add8-e396cd25c06d" title="A rather squat female dwarf with thick, full lips called Helja Strongheart who is a cutpurse." href="#95f81f4c-bdef-4b78-add8-e396cd25c06d">Helja Strongheart</a></td><td>39 Gold 2 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by my mother and father as an only child. Others saw me as different, or strange, and so I had few companions.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a rogue</summary> <div class="descriptive">"I left home at a relatively young age, and found refuge in a thieves' guild. An experienced rogue saw something in me, and taught me several useful tricks. I'm guilty of a terrible crime. I hope I can redeem myself for it. I'm loyal to my friends"</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I got really drunk, and woke up in the middle of nowhere. From there, I had to trek back home, and on the way, I lost something of sentimental value to me. To pay off a debt, I had to work as a rogue.After that, I used to play cards in a pub, and one time supposedly cheated a <a data-id="4813b309-2a51-405a-b9ce-d6fece9483d1" data-object-type="npc" class="link-internal 4813b309-2a51-405a-b9ce-d6fece9483d1" title="A youthful adult man with jug-like ears called Erky Leffery who is a peasant." href="#4813b309-2a51-405a-b9ce-d6fece9483d1">man</a> out of his winnings; I'll freely admit that I'm to blame. I'm still on the lookout for him to this very day.How could I ever forget the time I had gone for a walk, when I found a horse. It spoke to me, and told me to leave the town I was in before sundown. I was planning on leaving anyway, so I did, and then when I had reached the next town, there were rumours that the village had been attacked by ghouls.  At one point, I met the love of my life, who is no longer with me.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr> <h2>Balifra Bloodkith</h2>
<span class="macro-live macro-live-block">  <quote>   /bælʌfɹʌ blʌdkɪθ /. </quote> <p class="no-indent"> <span id="914ecd4c-fc60-4f1c-837d-f71144352f60">          <span class="first-character">B</span>alifra Bloodkith    </span> is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="2aabd229-47e4-4daf-ab11-2fb5c52f5f0a" id="2aabd229-47e4-4daf-ab11-2fb5c52f5f0a" role="tooltip" title="35 years old, to be exact.">a mid thirties</span> female dwarf.    She is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="e34be3da-0ea7-4015-aa7d-7f928140fc6c" id="e34be3da-0ea7-4015-aa7d-7f928140fc6c" role="tooltip" title="4ft. 2″">rather squat</span> and <span class="tip dotted" data-id="3b961ed0-6c90-47aa-bf22-46cc7ea22a66" id="3b961ed0-6c90-47aa-bf22-46cc7ea22a66" role="tooltip" title="183lbs. (with a BMI of 36)">built like a wrestler</span>, and has yellow eyes        and a long, luxurious beard,    with tan skin.    The most notable physical trait of Balifra is that she has a large number of freckles. </p> <p>   Balifra sweats profusely and easily.            She is      When she is relaxed, she is mischievous.  In moments of stress, she becomes industrious.  Religion-wise, Balifra is <span class="tip dotted" data-id="2129bf2a-6e02-4690-92a7-f03333e82b58" id="2129bf2a-6e02-4690-92a7-f03333e82b58" role="tooltip" title="Balifra Bloodkith is usually a quiet follower of Artemis, but can be quite rude to anyone who criticizes her choice of deity.">a quiet true believer</span> of <a data-id="artemis" data-object-type="deity" class="link-internal artemis" title="Artemis is the goddess of the Hunt and young girls. She can change others into animals as punishment for transgressions against her and she demands appropriate respect from mortals." href="#artemis">Artemis</a>.  <p>      Balifra is slightly unsuccessful as a <span class="tip dotted" data-id="44b42bb5-a909-4d39-80dd-bab7527e1dbe" id="44b42bb5-a909-4d39-80dd-bab7527e1dbe" role="tooltip" title="Engages in sexual activity for payment.">harlot</span>, with a background of being a peasant.         She belongs to the <span class="tip dotted" data-id="de7d3b9d-4769-48fb-a4d3-fdec89d4e570" id="de7d3b9d-4769-48fb-a4d3-fdec89d4e570" role="tooltip" title="Balifra lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">peasantry</span> social class.    </p> <p>   Balifra currently has pocket sand in her pockets,    and 50 Gold 6 Silver 2 Copper to her name.        She lives on <a data-id="fe95c8d8-14ea-4c39-a7df-ef48072c80bd" data-object-type="road" class="link-internal fe95c8d8-14ea-4c39-a7df-ef48072c80bd" title="Finelien's Square is a wide paved rock road. It is made of broad flagstones, hewn perfectly flat and level. There's a laundry line connecting two houses that are slightly closer together than usual. The name comes from Finelien Goldfinder, who was a well respected local who was killed in war." href="#fe95c8d8-14ea-4c39-a7df-ef48072c80bd">Finelien's Square</a>.               Balifra knows Common and Dwarvish.           </p> <section>Balifra currently earns 1 Gold 1 Silver 2 Copper per day. <details open=""><summary>Finances</summary> <table>     <tr>         <th>Type</th>         <th>Amount</th>     </tr>     <tr><td>Gross Income</td><td>1 Gold 2 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td><i>Tax</i></td><td><i> 8.5 Copper</i></td></tr>     <tr><td>Net Income</td><td>1 Gold 1 Silver 2 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Total Lifestyle Expenses (<span class="tip dotted" data-id="c16b9491-1893-4096-b23d-42f80a093a35" id="c16b9491-1893-4096-b23d-42f80a093a35" role="tooltip" title="Balifra lives modestly- not without creature comforts of wine and decent food thanks to frugality, though">modest</span>)</td><td>1 Gold 3 Silver 1 Copper</td></tr>     <tr><td>Profit</td><td>- 1 Silver 9 Copper</td></tr>           </table></details></section>  <section><details open="">   <summary>Early Life</summary> <div class="descriptive">I was born at home, and was raised by my single father as an only child. I had a squalid upbringing in a mansion.  I had a few close friends, and my childhood was a relatively normal one.</div> </details></section> <section><details open="">   <summary>Becoming a harlot</summary> <div class="descriptive">"  I've had a bit of a downturn as a harlot. If it keeps up for much longer, I'm going to begin losing hope.   <b>Amity</b>. You are never too downtrodden to be a good person to someone."</div> </details></section> <details open=""><summary>Life Events</summary><div class="descriptive">Well, I certainly have a tale or two...This one time I was given a magical trinket- it's a Bold Leather Pouch of Leaping.<blockquote><h4>Bold Leather Pouch of Leaping</h4>Contains 1d4 unreplenishable charges of the Heroism spell (1st level). Contains 1d4 unreplenishable charges of the Jump spell (1st level).</blockquote> I witnessed a terrible curse once- Honest to god. An old woman once came into town claiming to be a god and told us she had cast a miracle on our town, but nobody paid attention to them. That night, monsters descended upon our town. At one point, because of a promise, I did some time as a peasant.</div></details>  <div class="classTable">   <details open=""><summary>Relationships</summary>   <table>       <tr>       <th>Name</th>
